# HarnessX: A Composable, Adaptive, and Evolvable Agent Harness Foundry
# HarnessX：一个可组合、可自适应且可演化的智能体支撑架构


Darwin Agent Team
Darwin 智能体团队


See Contributions and Acknowledgments section for a full author list.
完整作者名单请参见“贡献与致谢”部分。


## Abstract
## 摘要


AI agent performance depends critically on the runtime harness, comprising the prompts, tools, memory, and control flow that mediate how a model observes, reasons, and acts. Yet today's harnesses remain largely hand-crafted and static: each new model or task still demands bespoke scaffolding, and the rich traces produced during execution are rarely distilled back into systematic improvement. We introduce HarnessX, a foundry for composable, adaptive, and evolvable agent harnesses. HarnessX assembles typed harness primitives via a substitution algebra, adapts them through AEGIS, a trace-driven multi-agent evolution engine grounded in an operational mirror between symbolic adaptation and reinforcement learning, and closes the harness-model loop by turning trajectories into both harness updates and model training signal. Across five benchmarks (ALFWorld, GAIA, WebShop, 73-Bench, and SWE-bench Verified), HarnessX yields an average gain of +14.5% (up to +44.0%), with gains largest where baselines are lowest. These results suggest that agent progress need not come from model scaling alone: composing and evolving runtime interfaces from execution feedback is an actionable and complementary lever. The complete codebase will be open-sourced in a future release.
AI 代理的性能在很大程度上取决于运行时 harness，它由提示、工具、记忆和控制流组成，决定模型如何观察、推理并行动。然而，今天的 harness 仍大多依赖手工构建且静态不变：每来一个新模型或新任务，仍需定制脚手架，而执行过程中产生的丰富轨迹也很少被提炼回系统性的改进。我们提出 HarnessX，一个用于构建可组合、可适应、可演化代理 harness 的 foundry。HarnessX 通过替换代数组合带类型的 harness 基元，经由 AEGIS 进行自适应——这是一种由轨迹驱动的多智能体进化引擎，其基础是符号自适应与强化学习之间的操作镜像——并通过将轨迹转化为 harness 更新和模型训练信号，闭合 harness-模型循环。在五个基准（ALFWorld、GAIA、WebShop、73-Bench 和 SWE-bench Verified）上，HarnessX 平均提升 +14.5%（最高 +44.0%），且基线越低，收益越大。这些结果表明，代理进步未必只来自模型规模的扩张：从执行反馈中组合并演化运行时接口，是一种可行且互补的杠杆。完整代码库将在未来版本中开源。

## 1 Introduction
## 1 引言


The capacity of modern agents depends not only on the underlying model $\left\lbrack  {6,9,{36},{42}}\right\rbrack$ ,but on the mediation imposed by the surrounding harness $\left\lbrack  {2,{20},{24}}\right\rbrack$ . This harness converts raw model outputs into structured agent behaviors by determining how tasks are represented, how external services are accessed, and how intermediate decisions are communicated during execution. As agents tackle longer-horizon tasks in richer environments, harness design becomes integral to agent development.
现代智能体的能力不仅取决于底层模型 $\left\lbrack  {6,9,{36},{42}}\right\rbrack$ ，还取决于周围封装（harness）所施加的中介作用 $\left\lbrack  {2,{20},{24}}\right\rbrack$ 。该封装通过决定任务如何被表示、外部服务如何被访问，以及执行过程中中间决策如何被传达，把原始模型输出转换为结构化的智能体行为。随着智能体在更丰富的环境中处理更长时间跨度的任务，封装设计便成为智能体开发的关键环节。


Despite this importance, harness development remains far from a mature engineering discipline. First, harnesses are hand-engineered and static: any change in model version, tooling, or problem domain requires bespoke modification, with no mechanism for experience-driven improvement. Second, harnesses are architecturally entangled: they typically combine prompt templates, tool wrappers, retry policies, and memory in the same codepaths, so changes to one component silently break others, and reuse across domains reduces to copying rather than composition. Third, harness engineering and model training operate independently: trajectory data collected while improving the harness is discarded rather than incorporated into model training, and model improvements do not translate into harness improvements.
尽管如此重要，封装开发仍远未达到成熟的工程学科水平。首先，封装是手工工程且静态的：任何对模型版本、工具或问题领域的更改都需要进行定制化修改，而缺乏基于经验的改进机制。其次，封装在架构上高度耦合：它们通常在同一代码路径中同时组合提示模板、工具封装、重试策略和记忆，因此对某一组件的改动会在不经意间破坏其他组件，而跨领域复用往往只是复制而非组合。第三，封装工程与模型训练是独立进行的：在改进封装时收集到的轨迹数据被丢弃，而不是纳入模型训练；模型的改进也不会转化为封装的改进。


We address these gaps by treating the harness as a first-class object that can be composed, adapted, and evolved alongside the model. HarnessX embodies this principle as a unified harness foundry. It begins with a modular foundation: harness primitives spanning context, tools [7], skills, control, and memory are described via typed interfaces and composed via a substitution algebra. This separates concerns that existing systems typically conflate. On top of this substrate, we introduce AEGIS, an observability-driven and auditable harness adaptation engine. Framing harness adaptation not as ad-hoc editing but as a learning problem over symbolic artifacts (prompts [51], tools, memory, and control policies) reveals that standard RL pathologies (reward hacking, catastrophic forgetting [15], under-exploration [16]) become concrete design risks. To address these risks, AEGIS combines full trace observability with a four-stage pipeline (Digester, Planner, Evolver, and Critic) that compresses traces, plans adaptations, generates candidates, and assesses changes. Finally, we close the loop between harness adaptation and model training via harness-model co-evolution. Traces produced during harness adaptation serve as reinforcement-learning signal for model training, so that model improvements feed back into subsequent harness evolution.
我们通过将封装视为一种一等对象来弥补这些缺口：它能够与模型一起被组合、被适配，并被进化。HarnessX 将这一原则体现在统一的封装“铸造厂”中。它从模块化基础开始：覆盖上下文、工具 [7]、技能、控制和记忆的封装原语，通过类型化接口进行描述，并通过替换代数进行组合。这将现有系统通常混为一谈的关注点进行了分离。在这一底层之上，我们引入 AEGIS——一个以可观测性驱动并可审计的封装适配引擎。将封装适配不再视为临时的人工编辑，而是把它表述为对符号工件（提示 [51]、工具、记忆和控制策略）的学习问题，能够揭示标准 RL 的常见病理（奖励投机、灾难性遗忘 [15]、欠探索 [16]）会变成具体的设计风险。为应对这些风险，AEGIS 结合全量轨迹可观测性，并采用四阶段流水线（Digester、Planner、Evolver 和 Critic），对轨迹进行压缩、生成适配计划、产生候选方案并评估变更。最后，我们通过封装-模型协同进化，将封装适配与模型训练闭环起来：封装适配过程中产生的轨迹作为强化学习信号用于模型训练，使得模型改进能够反过来反馈到后续封装进化中。


We empirically validate HarnessX across five benchmarks (GAIA,ALFWorld,WebShop, ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench,SWE-bench Verified), three task-agent families (Claude Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5.4, Qwen3.5-9B), and up to 15 evolution rounds. Harness evolution yields an average absolute gain of +14.5% across 15 model-benchmark configurations, with individual gains ranging from ${0.0}\%$ to $+ {44.0}\%$ among improving configurations (14 of 15),from +1.1% ( ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench,near-ceiling baseline) to +44.0% (ALFWorld,weakest agent). Gains exhibit an inverse-scaling pattern: on ALFWorld and GAIA, the weakest task agent benefits most (+44.0% for Qwen3.5-9B vs. +11.2% for Sonnet 4.6 on ALFWorld), suggesting that evolved harnesses address behavioral gaps that weaker models cannot self-correct. On heterogeneous task sets (GAIA), single-harness evolution stagnates; a variant-isolation ablation restores stable improvement (+13.6%, non-degrading over 15 rounds).
我们在五个基准（GAIA、ALFWorld、WebShop、${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench、SWE-bench Verified）上、在三类任务-智能体家族（Claude Sonnet 4.6、GPT-5.4、Qwen3.5-9B）上，并进行最多 15 轮进化的实验验证。封装进化在 15 种模型-基准配置上平均带来 +14.5% 的绝对增益；在实现改进的配置中，单项增益范围为 ${0.0}\%$ 到 $+ {44.0}\%$（共 15 轮中的 14 轮出现改进），从 +1.1%（ ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench，接近上限的基线）到 +44.0%（ALFWorld，最弱智能体）。增益呈现反向规模化模式：在 ALFWorld 和 GAIA 上，最弱任务智能体受益最多（例如在 ALFWorld 上，Qwen3.5-9B 从 +44.0%，而 Sonnet 4.6 为 +11.2%），这表明进化后的封装能够弥补更弱模型无法自行纠正的行为缺口。在异构任务集合（GAIA）上，单一封装进化会停滞；通过“变体隔离”的消融可以恢复稳定改进（+13.6%，15 轮内不降级）。


In summary, our contributions are four-fold:
总结而言，我们的贡献有四点：


- Harness Composition (Section 3). We formalize the harness as a first-class, typed object composed of processors attached to lifecycle hooks. A nine-dimensional taxonomy spans the full behavioral space, and a substitution algebra enables per-task configuration with type-safe insertion and removal. This compositional structure makes the intended scope of each behavioral change explicit-a precondition for the variant isolation that stabilizes evolution.
- 封装组合（第 3 节）。我们将封装形式化为一种一等、类型化对象，由挂接在生命周期钩子上的处理器组成。九维分类覆盖完整的行为空间，而替换代数使得能够针对每个任务进行类型安全的插入与移除配置。这种组合结构使每一项行为变更的预期范围变得明确——这是实现“变体隔离”以稳定进化的前提条件。


- Harness Adaptation (Section 4). We introduce AEGIS, a trace-driven, multi-agent harness evolution engine. An operational mirror maps harness adaptation onto standard RL constructs, converting familiar RL pathologies (reward hacking, catastrophic forgetting, under-exploration) into concrete design risks addressed by a four-stage pipeline (Digester, Planner, Evolver, Critic) with deterministic gating. An optional variant-isolation strategy prevents cross-task interference on heterogeneous benchmarks.
- 封装适配（第 4 节）。我们提出 AEGIS，一个由轨迹驱动的多智能体封装进化引擎。一个操作镜像将封装适配映射到标准 RL 构件上，把熟悉的 RL 病理（奖励投机、灾难性遗忘、欠探索）转化为具体的设计风险，并通过四阶段流水线（Digester、Planner、Evolver、Critic）配合确定性门控来加以解决。可选的变体隔离策略能够在异构基准上防止跨任务干扰。


- Harness-Model Co-Evolution (Section 5). We close the optimization loop by interleaving harness evolution with model reinforcement learning over a shared replay buffer. Cross-harness GRPO enables the model to internalize strategies from successive harness versions, breaking the scaffolding ceiling that limits harness-only adaptation and the training-signal ceiling that limits model-only RL.
- Harness-模型协同进化（第5节）。我们通过将伴随回放缓冲区进行的模型强化学习与Harness演化交错，闭合优化回路。跨Harness的GRPO使模型能够从连续的Harness版本中内化策略，打破仅Harness适配受限于搭手架上限、仅模型RL受限于训练信号上限这两重天花板。


- Empirical Validation (Section 6). Across five benchmarks, three task-agent families, and up to 15 evolution rounds,HarnessX yields an average gain of +14.5% (up to +44.0%), with gains largest where baselines are lowest. A variant-isolation ablation resolves stagnation on heterogeneous task sets, and co-evolution yields an additional +4.7% over harness-only evolution (Section 6.5).
- 实证验证（第6节）。在五个基准、三类任务-智能体家族以及最多15轮演化中，HarnessX带来平均+14.5%的增益（最高+44.0%），且增益在基线最低的地方最大。针对异构任务集的变体隔离消融可消除停滞，而协同进化相较仅Harness进化还带来额外+4.7%（第6.5节）。


## 2 Related Work
## 2 相关工作


### 2.1 Harness Engineering
### 2.1 运行时工程


Existing agent infrastructure occupies a spectrum of increasingly opinionated harness abstractions. At the primitive layer, libraries such as LangChain [1], LlamaIndex [23], and Smolagents [32] provide typed building blocks for prompts, tools, retrieval, and memory. These primitives can be tested in isolation but do not support harness-level composition: two harnesses built from identical primitives may still differ in structure.
现有的代理基础设施处于一系列日益具备明确主张的运行时抽象之中。在最基础层，LangChain [1]、LlamaIndex [23] 和 Smolagents [32] 等库为提示、工具、检索和记忆提供了有类型的构建块。这些原语可以单独测试，但不支持运行时级组合：由相同原语构建的两个运行时在结构上仍可能不同。


The next level of abstraction orchestrates these primitives into reusable patterns. LangGraph [17] models the behavior of an agent with a stateful graph; AutoGen [39] models multi-agent interaction as structured conversation; CrewAI [26] assigns role-based identities to agents; and Letta [28] couples autonomous loops with persistent memory. Although these frameworks make harness writing easier, they impose a particular control loop, so combining patterns, replacing components, and porting enhancements across tasks mostly remain manual.
下一层抽象将这些原语编排成可复用模式。LangGraph [17] 用有状态图来建模代理行为；AutoGen [39] 将多代理交互建模为结构化对话；CrewAI [26] 为代理分配基于角色的身份；Letta [28] 则将自主循环与持久记忆相结合。尽管这些框架让运行时编写更容易，但它们施加了特定的控制循环，因此组合模式、替换组件以及将改进移植到不同任务之间，基本仍需手工完成。


Lastly, there are productized, domain-specific harnesses such as Claude Code [2], Cursor [4], Manus [34], and DeerFlow [5]. These systems demonstrate the impact of harness design but remain architecturally static, evolving only through manual iteration.
最后，还有 Claude Code [2]、Cursor [4]、Manus [34] 和 DeerFlow [5] 这类产品化、领域特定的运行时。这些系统展示了运行时设计的影响，但在架构上仍是静态的，只能通过人工迭代演进。


Two structural gaps persist across all three layers. First, no layer exposes the harness as a substitutable entity composed of typed elements, so building a per-task harness always involves rewriting. Second, no mechanism exists for in-loop improvement: once defined, a harness evolves only through human iteration between releases.
这三层都存在两个结构性缺口。第一，没有任何一层将运行时暴露为由有类型元素组成、可替换的实体，因此构建按任务定制的运行时总离不开重写。第二，不存在循环内改进机制：一旦定义，运行时只能通过人类在发布之间的迭代来演化。


Concurrently, Claude Code introduced Dynamic Workflows [3], enabling the model to generate task-specific harness scripts at runtime. While this represents a step toward adaptive harnesses, it operates within a single session without persistent trace-based optimization, cross-session evolution, or harness-model co-training. HarnessX addresses both gaps by treating harness adaptation as a multi-round, trace-driven learning problem with typed composition for variant isolation, structured observability for pathology detection, and a shared replay buffer that closes the loop between harness evolution and model training.
与此同时，Claude Code 引入了 Dynamic Workflows [3]，使模型能够在运行时生成任务特定的运行时脚本。尽管这代表着向自适应运行时迈出了一步，但它仅在单次会话内运行，没有基于轨迹的持久优化、跨会话演化或运行时-模型协同训练。HarnessX 通过将运行时适配视为一个多轮、由轨迹驱动的学习问题，并借助用于变体隔离的有类型组合、用于病理检测的结构化可观测性，以及一个闭合运行时演化与模型训练之间循环的共享回放缓冲区，来同时解决这两个缺口。


### 2.2 Self-Evolving Agents
### 2.2 自我进化型代理


Research on self-evolving agents investigates how an agent system can improve without retraining the underlying foundation model. Early work focused on the single most easily editable aspect: the prompt. Approaches like APE [52], OPRO [43], EvoPrompt [11], Promptbreeder [8] treat instruction formulation as a black-box optimization problem, while ProTeGi [29] and TextGrad [46] introduce gradient-inspired textual feedback to make the optimization process explicit. DSPy [14] and MIPRO [27] extend this approach by compiling a declarative LM program, whose prompts are optimized against labeled data. These approaches establish instructions as a learnable component, but harness-level features (tools, memory, control flow) remain outside the optimization scope.
关于自我进化型代理的研究，探讨代理系统如何在不对底层基础模型进行再训练的情况下持续改进。早期工作聚焦于最容易编辑的单一环节：提示词。诸如 APE [52]、OPRO [43]、EvoPrompt [11]、Promptbreeder [8] 的方法，将指令制定视为黑盒优化问题；而 ProTeGi [29] 与 TextGrad [46] 则引入受梯度启发的文本反馈，使优化过程显式化。DSPy [14] 和 MIPRO [27] 通过编译一个声明式的 LM 程序，将该思路进一步扩展：其提示词会针对带标注的数据进行优化。这些方法将指令作为可学习的组成部分，但集成层特性（工具、记忆、控制流）仍超出优化范围。


Another line of work improves agents by accumulating and reusing prior execution experience in memory: Memento [50] improves agents through case-based memory without fine-tuning the model, while MIA [30] unifies non-parametric and parametric memory within a single Manager-Planner-Executor framework: a non-parametric store of compressed trajectories and a parametric planner that evolves on the fly at test time, coupled by a bidirectional loop that continually converts experience between the two, demonstrating superiority across eleven benchmarks.
另一条研究路线通过在记忆中累积并复用先前的执行经验来改进代理：Memento [50] 通过基于案例的记忆提升代理，而无需对模型进行微调；MIA [30] 在同一个 Manager-Planner-Executor 框架内统一了非参数记忆与参数记忆：一方面有压缩轨迹的非参数存储，另一方面有会在测试时动态演化的参数型规划器，并通过一个双向循环持续在两者之间转换经验，从而在十一项基准测试中体现出优越性。


Subsequent works extend optimization to agent workflows. GPTSwarm [54], ADAS [12], AFlow [48], A ${}^{2}$ Flow [49], AgentSwift [21], ResMAS [53], and EvoAgentX [37] search over collaboration strategies, agent ordering, and aggregation mechanisms. These works demonstrate that workflow structure is learnable and yields larger gains than prompt-only optimization. However, component-level artifacts (tool implementations, memory policies, node-internal prompts) remain static: the optimization scope covers inter-component relations but does not encompass the full harness.
后续工作将优化扩展到代理工作流。GPTSwarm [54]、ADAS [12]、AFlow [48]、A ${}^{2}$ Flow [49]、AgentSwift [21]、ResMAS [53] 和 EvoAgentX [37] 会在协作策略、代理排序以及聚合机制上进行搜索。这些工作表明，工作流结构是可学习的，并带来比仅优化提示词更大的收益。然而，组件级产物（工具实现、记忆策略、节点内部的提示词）保持不变：优化范围覆盖组件之间的关系，却不包含整个 harness。


A final group treats harness evolution explicitly. SICA [31] optimizes a SWE-bench agent's source code directly, while Darwin Gödel Machine [18] proposes open-ended optimization over a database of agent variants. HyperAgents [47] makes the optimization process itself adaptable; Meta-Harness [19] improves sampling efficiency via a file-system-based interface. AHE [22] and Life-Harness [41] emphasize observability, explainability, and source-code rewriting. Collectively, these works establish the harness as an evolutionary target and demonstrate that observability is essential for stable self-improvement. However, their designs lack a unifying theoretical framework that connects observed failure modes to principled defenses.
最后一组研究将 harness 演化明确地纳入考虑。SICA [31] 直接优化 SWE-bench 代理的源代码，而 Darwin Gödel Machine [18] 提出对一个代理变体数据库进行开放式优化。HyperAgents [47] 使优化过程本身具有可适应性；Meta-Harness [19] 通过基于文件系统的接口提升采样效率。AHE [22] 和 Life-Harness [41] 强调可观测性、可解释性以及源代码重写。总体而言，这些工作将 harness 确立为一个进化目标，并证明可观测性对于稳定的自我改进至关重要。然而，它们的设计缺少一个能够将已观测到的失败模式与有原则的防御联系起来的统一理论框架。


The heuristic-learning theory [38] partially addresses this gap by mapping RL concepts to symbolic self-optimization updates. In this framework, observable traces correspond to proper credit assignment, falsifiable change manifests correspond to reward shaping, and proposal-critique cycles provide structured exploration. HarnessX instantiates this paradigm, formalizing the correspondence as the operational mirror between RL and symbolic harness evolution (Section 4.1).
启发式学习理论 [38] 在一定程度上弥补了这一缺口：它将强化学习（RL）的概念映射到符号式自优化更新。在该框架中，可观测的轨迹对应合理的归因（credit assignment），可证伪的变化表现对应奖励塑形（reward shaping），而提案-批判循环提供了结构化的探索。HarnessX 具体实现了这种范式：通过将其形式化为 RL 与符号式 harness 演化之间的操作性镜像（第 4.1 节）。


## 3 Harness Composition
## 3 Harness 组成


The gap identified in Section 2.1 is the absence of an infrastructure layer that exposes the harness as a typed, substitutable entity. Primitive libraries leave composition to application code, orchestrators expose a fixed set of patterns, and product harnesses are opaque end-to-end. Without a compositional substrate, every behavioral change or cross-team handoff requires re-implementation. HarnessX addresses this via a unified design principle: the harness is a first-class value, the processor is a typed atomic component, and composition proceeds via processor insertion at typed hook points. We formalize the harness (Section 3.1), its building block, the processor (Section 3.2), and the nine-dimensional processor taxonomy (Section 3.3). Definitions are intentionally concise: their role is to establish the vocabulary and expose the edit surface on which harness evolution (Section 4) operates.
第 2.1 节中识别出的差距在于缺少一层基础设施，将 harness 作为一种有类型、可替换的实体暴露出来。基础原语库把组合交给应用代码；编排器只暴露一组固定模式；产品级 harness 则是端到端的不透明黑盒。没有可组合的承载层，每一次行为变化或跨团队交接都意味着需要重新实现。HarnessX 通过一项统一的设计原则来解决：harness 是一等值（first-class value），处理器是一个有类型的原子组件，而组合通过在有类型的挂钩点（hook points）处插入处理器来推进。我们在第 3.1 节形式化 harness，在第 3.2 节介绍其构建模块——处理器，以及第 3.3 节给出的九维处理器分类。定义刻意保持精炼：其作用是建立术语，并暴露 harness 演进（第 4 节）所依托的可编辑界面。


<table><tr><td>Hook</td><td>Event type</td><td>Permitted modifications</td></tr><tr><td>task_start</td><td>TaskStartEvent</td><td>system prompt</td></tr><tr><td>step_start</td><td>StepStartEvent</td><td>structural history edits</td></tr><tr><td>before_model</td><td>BeforeModelEvent</td><td>last user content; one user-message append</td></tr><tr><td>after_model</td><td>ModelResponseEvent</td><td>response content, tool calls</td></tr><tr><td>before_tool</td><td>ToolCallEvent</td><td>tool input, approval flag</td></tr><tr><td>after_tool</td><td>ToolResultEvent</td><td>tool result</td></tr><tr><td>step_end</td><td>StepEndEvent</td><td>read-only</td></tr><tr><td>task_end</td><td>TaskEndEvent</td><td>read-only</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td>挂钩</td><td>事件类型</td><td>允许的修改</td></tr><tr><td>task_start</td><td>TaskStartEvent</td><td>系统提示</td></tr><tr><td>step_start</td><td>StepStartEvent</td><td>结构性历史编辑</td></tr><tr><td>before_model</td><td>BeforeModelEvent</td><td>上一次用户内容；追加一条用户消息</td></tr><tr><td>after_model</td><td>ModelResponseEvent</td><td>响应内容、工具调用</td></tr><tr><td>before_tool</td><td>ToolCallEvent</td><td>工具输入、审批标志</td></tr><tr><td>after_tool</td><td>ToolResultEvent</td><td>工具结果</td></tr><tr><td>step_end</td><td>StepEndEvent</td><td>只读</td></tr><tr><td>task_end</td><td>TaskEndEvent</td><td>只读</td></tr></tbody></table>


Table 1 Hook points and their permitted modifications.
表 1：挂接点及其允许的修改内容。


### 3.1 The Harness as a First-Class Object
### 3.1 将 Harness 视为一等对象


A harness in HarnessX is the pair $\mathcal{H} = \left( {\mathcal{M},\mathcal{C}}\right)$ ,where $\mathcal{M}$ is a model configuration and $\mathcal{C}$ is a harness configuration. The two address disjoint concerns: $\mathcal{M}$ records which model serves which role (main,judge, evaluator) and the fallback policy for each role; $\mathcal{C}$ records how the agent behaves independently of model identity. They combine into an executable agent via agent = model_config.agentic(harness_config): an agent in HarnessX is a processor pipeline bound to a model, both independently substitutable.
在 HarnessX 中，harness 是一对 $\mathcal{H} = \left( {\mathcal{M},\mathcal{C}}\right)$ ，其中 $\mathcal{M}$ 是模型配置，$\mathcal{C}$ 是 harness 配置。两者划分了互不相交的关注点：$\mathcal{M}$ 记录哪些模型分别承担各角色（主模型、裁判、评估器）以及每个角色的回退策略；$\mathcal{C}$ 记录代理在不依赖模型身份的情况下如何表现。它们通过 agent = model_config.agentic(harness_config) 组合成可执行的代理：在 HarnessX 中，代理是绑定到模型的处理流水线，且二者都可独立替换。


The harness configuration itself decomposes as $\mathcal{C} = \left( {\mathbf{P},\mathbf{S}}\right) .\mathbf{P} : \mathcal{H}$ ook $\rightarrow$ List[Processor] is a hook-indexed list of processors,where Hook is the eight-element set of lifecycle events in Table 1. S is a fixed set of orthogonal slot resources: tool registry, tracer, workspace, sandbox provider, and plugin list. Slots are singletons, shared across all processors in a configuration; processor state is instance-private. $\mathbf{P}$ implements all per-step behavior; S houses the shared infrastructure that processors depend on but do not own.
harness 配置本身可分解为 $\mathcal{C} = \left( {\mathbf{P},\mathbf{S}}\right) .\mathbf{P} : \mathcal{H}$ ook $\rightarrow$ List[Processor] ，它是一个按 hook 索引的处理器列表，其中 Hook 是表 1 中八个生命周期事件构成的集合。S 是一组固定的、相互正交的插槽资源：工具注册表、追踪器、工作区、沙盒提供方，以及插件列表。插槽是单例，并在同一配置中的所有处理器之间共享；处理器状态对具体实例私有。$\mathbf{P}$ 实现所有逐步行为；S 承载处理器依赖但不拥有的共享基础设施。


We call $\mathcal{C}$ a first-class object because it is independently serializable,comparable,hashable,and substitutable. Two agents sharing $\mathcal{C}$ but differing in $\mathcal{M}$ execute the same processor pipeline,with behavior differing only in model responses; two agents sharing $\mathcal{M}$ but differing in $\mathcal{C}$ are behaviorally distinct. This reification is the precondition for programmatic evolution (Section 4).
我们称 $\mathcal{C}$ 为一等对象，是因为它可独立序列化、可比较、可哈希，并且可替换。两个代理共享 $\mathcal{C}$ 但在 $\mathcal{M}$ 上不同，它们执行相同的处理流水线，行为仅在模型响应上有所差异；两个代理共享 $\mathcal{M}$ 但在 $\mathcal{C}$ 上不同，它们在行为上是不同的。这种实体化是程序化演化（第 4 节）的前提。


### 3.2 The Processor Abstraction
### 3.2 处理器抽象


Every per-step behavior in HarnessX is implemented as a processor, an object satisfying the protocol async def process(self, event: Event) -> AsyncIterator[Event]. A processor consumes one event and yields zero or more, producing exactly one of five outcomes: pass-through (yield unchanged), transform (yield modified), split (yield multiple same-type events, processed independently downstream), intercept (yield nothing, blocking propagation), or interrupt (raise an exception, which halts the loop). This restricted interface enables compositionality: every processor at a given hook consumes and yields the same event type, so processors compose by sequential application and can be inserted or removed without affecting type correctness of the surrounding pipeline.
HarnessX 中每一步的行为都由处理器实现；处理器是满足协议 async def process(self, event: Event) -> AsyncIterator[Event] 的对象。处理器消费一个事件并产出零个或多个事件，且恰好产生以下五种结果之一：透传（原样产出）、变换（产出修改后的事件）、分裂（产出多个同类型事件，并在下游独立处理）、拦截（不产出任何内容，阻止传播）或中断（抛出异常，从而终止循环）。这种受限接口使其具备可组合性：在给定 hook 处的每个处理器都消费并产出相同的事件类型，因此处理器可通过顺序应用进行组合，并且可以插入或移除而不影响周围管道的类型正确性。


As listed in Table 1, processors attach to one of eight hook points emitted by the run loop. The run loop validates hook contracts after each invocation: a violation (e.g., modifying a read-only field) raises an exception immediately rather than silently propagating corrupted state. Each processor carries three class-level metadata fields that govern composition: _singleton_group names a mutual-exclusion class, ensuring at most one processor per group; _order is an ordering hint within a hook (with constants PRE, NORMAL, POST); and after is a list of soft dependencies on other singleton groups.
如表 1 所示，处理器挂接到运行循环发出的八个 hook 点之一。运行循环会在每次调用后验证 hook 契约：若发生违例（例如修改只读字段），会立即抛出异常，而不是静默传播损坏的状态。每个处理器都带有三个类级元数据字段，用于约束组合：_singleton_group 指定一个互斥类，确保每个组最多只有一个处理器；_order 是 hook 内部的顺序提示（常量为 PRE、NORMAL、POST）；而 after 则是对其他 singleton group 的软依赖列表。


This design makes harness evolution a first-class operation: AEGIS can insert a new processor at a specific hook, replace an existing one by matching its singleton group, or remove a processor entirely-all without touching other processors at the same or different hooks. Because the type contract (input event type $=$ output event type) is enforced per-hook, any such substitution preserves the well-typedenses of the overall pipeline. The metadata fields further constrain composition: _singleton_group prevents conflicting duplicates, and _order ensures that newly inserted processors interact predictably with existing ones. These guarantees are the mechanism by which variant isolation (Section 4.5) operates each variant differs only in which processors occupy which hooks, and the type system ensures that no variant can silently violate the pipeline contract during evolution.
这一设计使 harness 演化成为一等操作：AEGIS 可以在特定 hook 处插入新的处理器，通过匹配其 singleton group 替换现有处理器，或将某个处理器彻底移除——而无需触碰同一或不同 hook 上的其他处理器。由于类型契约（输入事件类型 $=$ 输出事件类型）按 hook 强制执行，这类替换都能保持整体管道的良好类型性。元数据字段进一步约束组合：_singleton_group 防止冲突性重复，_order 则确保新插入的处理器与现有处理器以可预测方式交互。这些保证构成了变体隔离（第 4.5 节）得以运行的机制：每个变体的差异仅在于哪些处理器占据哪些 hook，而类型系统确保任何变体在演化过程中都不会静默违反管道契约。


### 3.3 The Nine-Dimensional Taxonomy
### 3.3 九维分类法


We organize the behavioral space along nine dimensions: model selection (D1) decides which model serves which role; context assembly (D2) determines what is presented to the model at each step; memory management (D3) governs what carries across steps and sessions; tool ecosystem (D4) controls which tools the agent can invoke; execution environment (D5) determines where tool-induced side-effects materialize; evaluation and reward (D6) specifies how outcomes are judged; control and safety (D7) enforces rules that keep the agent from looping, overspending, or drifting from intent; observability (D8) records each event, model call, and tool invocation; and the training bridge (D9) converts execution trajectories into reinforcement-learning records. Figure 2 illustrates the full taxonomy along with representative processors and the hooks at which they typically attach in a standard configuration.
我们沿九个维度来组织行为空间：模型选择（D1）决定哪个模型承担哪种角色；上下文组装（D2）确定每一步向模型呈现的内容；记忆管理（D3）规定哪些信息会跨步骤与跨会话延续；工具生态（D4）控制智能体可调用哪些工具；执行环境（D5）决定由工具引发的副作用在哪里出现；评估与奖励（D6）明确如何判断结果；控制与安全（D7）强制执行规则，防止智能体陷入循环、超支，或偏离初衷；可观测性（D8）记录每个事件、每次模型调用以及每次工具调用；训练桥接（D9）将执行轨迹转换为强化学习记录。图 2 展示了完整分类法，并给出了典型处理器及其通常在标准配置中挂接的挂钩点。


In practice, AEGIS edits span all nine dimensions during evolution: D2 (context assembly) and D4 (tool ecosystem) are the most frequent edit targets (Section 6.2), while D8 (observability) provides the trace substrate on which AEGIS itself reasons, and D9 (training bridge) supplies trajectory records for co-evolution (Section 5), closing the optimization loop.
在实践中，AEGIS 在进化过程中会覆盖所有九个维度：D2（上下文组装）和 D4（工具生态）是最常见的编辑目标（第 6.2 节）；D8（可观测性）提供了轨迹层，AEGIS 本身正是在其上进行推理；D9（训练桥接）为协同进化（第 5 节）提供轨迹记录，从而闭合优化回路。


<table><tr><td>RL concept</td><td>Symbolic-space dual</td><td>AEGIS realization</td></tr><tr><td>Policy $\pi$</td><td>Harness-update procedure ${\pi }_{\text{ evo }}$</td><td>Four-stage pipeline (Section 4.3)</td></tr><tr><td>State ${s}_{t}$</td><td>$\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t}}\right)$</td><td>Harness configuration + trace store</td></tr><tr><td>Action ${a}_{t}$</td><td>Typed harness edit</td><td>Builder operation + change manifest</td></tr><tr><td>Feedback</td><td>Trace $\tau  +$ verifier score $r$</td><td>Observability layer</td></tr><tr><td>Update</td><td>${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  U\left( {{\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t},{r}_{t}}\right)$</td><td>Deterministic acceptance gate</td></tr></table>
