Table 2 Operational mirror: RL concepts and their symbolic-space duals in AEGIS.
表2 运行镜像：RL 概念及其在 AEGIS 中的符号空间对应项。


## 4 Harness Adaptation
## 4 Harness 适配


The composition layer (Section 3) provides a typed, substitutable harness; as illustrated in Figure 2, AEGIS is the system that evolves it. The key insight is that harness evolution maps structurally onto reinforcement learning in a symbolic space: harness configurations are states, typed edits are actions, and execution traces plus verifier scores constitute feedback. This mapping is predictive: it identifies three failure modes analogous to known RL pathologies (reward hacking, catastrophic forgetting, under-exploration) that motivate AEGIS's architectural defenses and are empirically confirmed in Section 6.6.
组合层（第 3 节）提供了一个带类型、可替换的 harness；如图 2 所示，AEGIS 就是用于演化它的系统。关键洞见在于：harness 演化在符号空间中在结构上对应强化学习——harness 配置是状态，带类型的编辑是动作，而执行轨迹加上验证器评分构成反馈。这种映射具有可预测性：它能识别出三种与已知 RL 病理相对应的失效模式（奖励投机、灾难性遗忘、欠探索），从而促成 AEGIS 的架构防御，并在第 6.6 节中通过实证得到证实。


We formalize the correspondence (Section 4.1), analyze the pathologies it predicts (Section 4.2), derive the four-stage pipeline as a defense architecture (Section 4.3), present the adaptation loop (Section 4.4), and introduce variant isolation for stable multi-variant evolution (Section 4.5).
我们在第 4.1 节形式化这种对应关系，在第 4.2 节分析它所预测的病理，在第 4.3 节将四阶段流水线推导为一种防御架构，在第 4.4 节给出适配闭环，并在第 4.5 节引入变体隔离以实现稳定的多变体演化。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_6.jpg?x=210&y=1009&w=1383&h=560&r=0"/>



Figure 2 The AEGIS evolution loop. A single meta-agent $\mathcal{M}$ drives all four stages (Digester,Planner,Evolver,Critic), selectively invoking each based on whether sufficient signal exists to continue. A deterministic gate ships or rejects the candidate edit.
图 2 AEGIS 演化回路。单个元智能体 $\mathcal{M}$ 驱动四个阶段（Digester、Planner、Evolver、Critic），根据是否存在足够信号来决定是否继续，从而对各阶段进行选择性调用。确定性门控用于接收或拒绝候选编辑。


### 4.1 The Operational Mirror
### 4.1 运行镜像


We formalize harness evolution as an MDP over symbolic artifacts. Table 2 summarizes the mapping; we first state three definitions that ground the correspondence.
我们将训练支架的演化形式化为在符号化工件上的马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）。表2概括了映射关系；我们首先给出三个定义，用以奠定二者之间的对应。


Definition 1 (Harness Configuration). A harness configuration is a tuple $\mathcal{H} = \left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\ldots ,{c}_{9}}\right)$ ,where each ${c}_{i} \in  {\mathcal{C}}_{i}$ instantiates one of the nine behavioral dimensions (Section 3.3): model selection $\left( {c}_{1}\right)$ ,context assembly $\left( {c}_{2}\right)$ ,memory management $\left( {c}_{3}\right)$ ,tool ecosystem $\left( {c}_{4}\right)$ ,execution environment $\left( {c}_{5}\right)$ ,evaluation and reward $\left( {c}_{6}\right)$ , control and safety $\left( {c}_{7}\right)$ ,observability $\left( {c}_{8}\right)$ ,and training bridge $\left( {c}_{9}\right)$ . Each ${\mathcal{C}}_{i}$ is the set of valid processor configurations for dimension $i$ ,constrained by hook-type contracts and singleton-group exclusion (Section 3.2).
定义1（训练支架配置）。训练支架配置是一个元组 $\mathcal{H} = \left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\ldots ,{c}_{9}}\right)$ ，其中每个 ${c}_{i} \in  {\mathcal{C}}_{i}$ 实例化九个行为维度之一（第3.3节）：模型选择 $\left( {c}_{1}\right)$ 、上下文组装 $\left( {c}_{2}\right)$ 、记忆管理 $\left( {c}_{3}\right)$ 、工具生态 $\left( {c}_{4}\right)$ 、执行环境 $\left( {c}_{5}\right)$ 、评估与奖励 $\left( {c}_{6}\right)$ 、控制与安全 $\left( {c}_{7}\right)$ 、可观测性 $\left( {c}_{8}\right)$ 以及训练桥接 $\left( {c}_{9}\right)$ 。每个 ${\mathcal{C}}_{i}$ 都是维度 $i$ 的有效处理器配置集合，受钩子类型合约约束，并排除单例组（第3.2节）。


Definition 2 (Harness Edit). A harness edit is a function $e : \mathcal{H} \rightarrow  \mathcal{H}$ that modifies one or more dimensions while preserving type contracts. The action space $\mathcal{E}$ is discrete but open-ended: each edit is a code-level artifact (new processor source, modified prompt template, reconfigured tool registry, or control-flow rewrite) generated by the meta-agent LLM, not selected from a pre-enumerated set. Combinatorial explosion is managed not by exhaustive search but by the LLM's generative capacity - the Planner proposes edits from trace-grounded hypotheses and by type constraints that prune invalid compositions at generation time.
定义2（训练支架编辑）。训练支架编辑是一个函数 $e : \mathcal{H} \rightarrow  \mathcal{H}$ ，它在保持类型合约的前提下修改一个或多个维度。动作空间 $\mathcal{E}$ 是离散的但开放式的：每次编辑都是代码级工件（新的处理器源代码、修改后的提示模板、重新配置的工具注册表，或控制流重写），由元智能体LLM生成，而不是从预先枚举的集合中选择。组合爆炸不是通过穷尽搜索来管理，而是通过LLM的生成能力——规划器基于由轨迹支撑的假设提出编辑，并通过类型约束在生成时剪枝掉无效的组合。


Definition 3 (Operational Mirror). The operational mirror is the tuple $\left( {\mathcal{H},\mathcal{E},\mathcal{R},\mathcal{T}}\right)$ ,where $\mathcal{H}$ is the harness-configuration space (states), $\mathcal{E}$ is the code-level edit space (actions), $\mathcal{R} : \mathcal{H} \times  \mathcal{E} \rightarrow  \mathbb{R}$ maps a configuration-edit pair to a scalar reward (verifier scores aggregated over an adaptation batch), and $\mathcal{T}$ is the trace store that provides structured feedback beyond the scalar signal. This tuple forms an MDP at the harness level: harness configurations are states, typed edits are actions, execution traces plus verifier scores constitute feedback, and a deterministic acceptance gate governs state transitions.
定义3（运行镜像）。运行镜像是一个元组 $\left( {\mathcal{H},\mathcal{E},\mathcal{R},\mathcal{T}}\right)$ ，其中 $\mathcal{H}$ 是训练支架配置空间（状态），$\mathcal{E}$ 是代码级编辑空间（动作），$\mathcal{R} : \mathcal{H} \times  \mathcal{E} \rightarrow  \mathbb{R}$ 将“配置-编辑”对映射到标量奖励（在一次适配批次上，验证器分数进行聚合），以及 $\mathcal{T}$ 是轨迹存储，用于在标量信号之外提供结构化反馈。该元组在训练支架层面构成一个MDP：训练支架配置是状态，带类型的编辑是动作，执行轨迹加上验证器分数构成反馈，而一个确定性的接收门控规则决定状态转移。


MDP instantiation. Let ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ denote the harness configuration at iteration $t$ (the model $\mathcal{M}$ is fixed throughout evolution),and let ${\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ denote the trace store accumulated from all previous executions. We define the symbolic state as ${s}_{t} = \left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t}}\right)$ . A harness-update policy ${\pi }_{\text{ evo }}$ selects an action ${a}_{t} \sim  {\pi }_{\text{ evo }}\left( {\cdot  \mid  {s}_{t}}\right)$ ,where ${a}_{t} \in  \mathcal{E}$ is a code-level edit drawn from the builder algebra. Applying this edit yields a candidate harness ${\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t} = {a}_{t}\left( {\mathcal{H}}_{t}\right)$ . Running the candidate on an adaptation batch (with the fixed model $\mathcal{M}$ ) produces new traces $\Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ and per-task verifier scores ${r}_{t}$ . A deterministic acceptance operator $U\left( {{\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t},{r}_{t}}\right)$ then either commits the candidate $\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} = {\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}}\right)$ or rejects it $\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} = {\mathcal{H}}_{t}}\right)$ ,enforcing the seesaw constraint: the candidate must not regress any previously solved task recorded in ${\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ . In both cases,the trace store grows: ${\mathcal{T}}_{t + 1} = {\mathcal{T}}_{t} \cup  \Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ .
MDP 实例化。设 ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ 表示第 $t$ 次迭代时的 harness 配置（模型 $\mathcal{M}$ 在整个演化过程中保持固定），并设 ${\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ 表示从所有先前执行中累积的轨迹存储。我们将符号状态定义为 ${s}_{t} = \left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t}}\right)$。一个 harness 更新策略 ${\pi }_{\text{ evo }}$ 选择一个动作 ${a}_{t} \sim  {\pi }_{\text{ evo }}\left( {\cdot  \mid  {s}_{t}}\right)$，其中 ${a}_{t} \in  \mathcal{E}$ 是从构建器代数中抽取的代码级编辑。应用该编辑得到一个候选 harness ${\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t} = {a}_{t}\left( {\mathcal{H}}_{t}\right)$。在适应批次上运行该候选（使用固定模型 $\mathcal{M}$）会产生新的轨迹 $\Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ 和逐任务验证器分数 ${r}_{t}$。随后，一个确定性的接受算子 $U\left( {{\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t},{r}_{t}}\right)$ 要么提交该候选 $\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} = {\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}}\right)$，要么拒绝它 $\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} = {\mathcal{H}}_{t}}\right)$，从而强制满足跷跷板约束：候选不得使 ${\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ 中记录的任何先前已解决任务退步。在两种情况下，轨迹存储都会增长：${\mathcal{T}}_{t + 1} = {\mathcal{T}}_{t} \cup  \Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t}$。


This MDP operates at the harness level: within a single task, ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ (together with the fixed $\mathcal{M}$ ) determines the agent’s behavior; across iterations,the harness-update policy ${\pi }_{\text{ evo }}$ modifies the harness. AEGIS realizes ${\pi }_{\text{ evo }}$ as a four-stage pipeline (Digester,Planner,Evolver,Critic) that maps ${s}_{t}$ to candidate edits through trace compression, adaptation planning, edit generation, and candidate assessment.
该 MDP 在 harness 层运行：在单个任务内，${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$（连同固定的 $\mathcal{M}$）决定代理的行为；在迭代之间，harness 更新策略 ${\pi }_{\text{ evo }}$ 修改 harness。AEGIS 将 ${\pi }_{\text{ evo }}$ 实现为一个四阶段流水线（Digester、Planner、Evolver、Critic），通过轨迹压缩、适应规划、编辑生成和候选评估，将 ${s}_{t}$ 映射为候选编辑。


### 4.2 Pathologies in Symbolic Space
### 4.2 符号空间中的病理


The mirror is not merely an analogy; it converts reinforcement-learning concepts into design requirements. We refer to three well-documented failure modes in RL, namely reward hacking [10], catastrophic forgetting [15], and under-exploration [16], collectively as RL pathologies. Once harness adaptation is cast as an MDP over symbolic artifacts, these pathologies reappear in amplified form, shaped by two properties of the symbolic setting: (1) a language-model evolver can construct structured exploits that numerical parameter perturbations cannot express, and (2) edits to shared components propagate non-locally through the harness. Each pathology below motivates a corresponding architectural defense in Section 4.3.
这面镜子并非只是类比；它把强化学习概念转化为设计要求。我们将 RL 中三种广为人知的失败模式——奖励黑客、灾难性遗忘和欠探索——统称为 RL 病理。一旦将 harness 适应表述为关于符号工件的 MDP，这些病理就会以放大的形式重现，并受符号环境的两个特性影响：(1) 语言模型进化器能够构造数值参数扰动无法表达的结构化漏洞；(2) 对共享组件的编辑会通过 harness 非局部传播。以下每种病理都促成了第 4.3 节中的相应架构防御。


Reward hacking. In standard RL, reward hacking [10] exploits loopholes in the reward signal without genuine task completion. Symbolic harness evolution amplifies this risk because the evolver can target the verification protocol directly: embedding benchmark answers into prompts, exploiting format regularities in the verifier, or introducing a processor that rewrites outputs to match verifier expectations.
奖励黑客。在标准 RL 中，奖励黑客 [10] 是在不真正完成任务的情况下利用奖励信号中的漏洞。符号化 harness 演化会放大这一风险，因为进化器可以直接针对验证协议：把基准答案嵌入提示词，利用验证器中的格式规律，或引入一个将输出重写为符合验证器预期的处理器。


Catastrophic forgetting. Catastrophic forgetting [15] occurs when improving performance on one region of the task distribution harms another. In symbolic harness evolution,an edit that repairs failure pattern $A$ can silently regress pattern $B$ ,because effects propagate through shared context,tools,memory policies,and control rules. Without explicit regression checking, an evolver conditioned only on failing-task traces cannot distinguish local gain from global regression.
灾难性遗忘。灾难性遗忘 [15] 指的是在提升任务分布某一区域的表现时，损害了另一部分。 在符号化 harness 演化中，对失败模式 $A$ 的修复性编辑，可能会因影响通过共享上下文、工具、记忆策略和控制规则传播，而悄然使模式 $B$ 退化。若没有显式回归检查，仅以失败任务轨迹为条件的进化器无法区分局部提升与全局退化。


Under-exploration. Under-exploration [16] manifests as a bias toward low-risk local edits: prompt rephrasing, tool-description tuning, or minor control-flow tweaks. These edits are cheap to generate and frequently pass gating without regressing solved tasks, biasing subsequent Planner hypotheses toward the same edit neighborhood. Structural changes (decomposing one agent into several, replacing the control strategy, or adopting a new memory architecture) require deliberate hypothesis formation and rarely emerge from trace-conditional local repair. Without a mechanism to propose edits beyond the immediate failure neighborhood, the system plateaus once local edits are exhausted.
欠探索。欠探索 [16] 表现为偏向低风险的局部编辑：重写提示词、调整工具描述，或微调控制流。这些编辑生成成本低，且常常在不使已解决任务退化的情况下通过门控，从而使后续 Planner 的假设偏向同一编辑邻域。结构性变更（将一个代理拆分为多个、替换控制策略，或采用新的记忆架构）需要有意形成假设，且很少从基于轨迹的局部修复中自然出现。若没有提出超出直接失败邻域编辑的方法，系统在局部编辑耗尽后就会停滞。


Summary. Symbolic harness evolution inherits the structural risks of RL (reward hacking, catastrophic forgetting, and under-exploration), and AEGIS addresses each with a dedicated mechanism: the Critic (reward hacking), the deterministic gating layer (catastrophic forgetting), and the Planner (under-exploration).
总结。符号化 harness 演化继承了 RL 的结构性风险（奖励黑客、灾难性遗忘和欠探索），而 AEGIS 通过专门机制分别应对：Critic（奖励黑客）、确定性门控层（灾难性遗忘）以及 Planner（欠探索）。


Algorithm 1: AEGIS Harness Evolution Loop (selective invocation)
算法 1：AEGIS Harness 演化循环（选择性调用）


---



Input: Initial harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{0}$ ,meta-agent $\mathcal{M}$ ,budget $T$ ,patience $P$ ,threshold $\alpha$
输入：初始 harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{0}$ ，元代理 $\mathcal{M}$ ，预算 $T$ ，耐心值 $P$ ，阈值 $\alpha$


Output: Evolved harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1}$ ,trace store ${\mathcal{T}}_{t + 1}$
输出：演化后的 harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1}$ ，轨迹存储 ${\mathcal{T}}_{t + 1}$


${\mathcal{T}}_{0} \leftarrow  \varnothing$



idle $\leftarrow  0$ ;
空闲 $\leftarrow  0$ ;


for $t = 0,1,\ldots ,T - 1$ do
对于 $t = 0,1,\ldots ,T - 1$ 执行


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Sample batch ${B}_{t}$ ;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;采样批次 ${B}_{t}$ ;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;run ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ on ${B}_{t}$ to get traces $\Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ ;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;在 ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ 上运行 ${B}_{t}$ 以获得轨迹 $\Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t}$ ;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;${\mathcal{T}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{T}}_{t} \cup  \Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t}$



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/* Digester (selective)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/* Digester（选择性）


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(evidence ${t}_{t},{a}_{t}$ ) $\leftarrow  \mathcal{M}$ .DIGESTER $\left( {\Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t}}\right)$ ;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;（证据 ${t}_{t},{a}_{t}$ ） $\leftarrow  \mathcal{M}$ .DIGESTER $\left( {\Delta {\mathcal{T}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t}}\right)$ ;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if ${a}_{t} < \alpha$ then ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ ;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;如果 ${a}_{t} < \alpha$ 则 ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ ;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;idle++;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;idle++;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;continue;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;continue;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/* Planner (selective)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/* 规划器（选择性）


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;${\text{ landscape }}_{t} \leftarrow  \mathcal{M}$ .PLANNER(evidence ${e}_{t}$ );
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;${\text{ landscape }}_{t} \leftarrow  \mathcal{M}$ .PLANNER(证据 ${e}_{t}$ );


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if landscap ${e}_{t} = \varnothing$ then ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ ;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;如果 landscap ${e}_{t} = \varnothing$ 则 ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ ;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;idle++;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;idle++;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;continue;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;continue;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/* Evolver (selective)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/* 演化器（选择性）


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;${\left\{  \left( {\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{k},{\text{ manifest }}_{k}\right) \right\}  }_{k = 1}^{{K}_{t}} \leftarrow  \mathcal{M}.\operatorname{EVOLVER}\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t},{\text{ landscape }}_{t}}\right) ;$



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if ${K}_{t} = 0$ then ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ ;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;如果 ${K}_{t} = 0$ 则 ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ ;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;idle++;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;idle++;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;continue;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;continue;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/* Critic & Gate (mandatory)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/* 评审器与门控（必需）


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ranking $\leftarrow  \mathcal{M}.\operatorname{CRITIC}\left( \left\{  \left( {{\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{k},{\text{ manifest }}_{k}}\right) \right\}  \right)$ ,evidence ${e}_{t}$ );
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;排名 $\leftarrow  \mathcal{M}.\operatorname{CRITIC}\left( \left\{  \left( {{\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{k},{\text{ manifest }}_{k}}\right) \right\}  \right)$ ,证据 ${e}_{t}$ );


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;${k}^{ \star  } \leftarrow   \bot$



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;foreach $k$ in ranking do
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;遍历 $k$ 于 ranking 中 do


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if DeterministicGate $\left( {{\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{k},{\mathcal{H}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t}}\right)$ passes then ${k}^{ \star  } \leftarrow  k$ ;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;如果 DeterministicGate $\left( {{\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{k},{\mathcal{H}}_{t},{\mathcal{T}}_{t}}\right)$ 通过则 ${k}^{ \star  } \leftarrow  k$ ;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;break;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;break;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;end
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;end


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if ${k}^{ \star  } \neq   \bot$ then ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{{k}^{ \star  }}$ ;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;如果${k}^{ \star  } \neq   \bot$则${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{{k}^{ \star  }}$；


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;${idle} \leftarrow  0$



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;else ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{H}}_{t}$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;否则${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  {\mathcal{H}}_{t}$


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;idle++;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;idle++;


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if ${idle} \geq  P$ then break;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;如果${idle} \geq  P$则break;


end
end


return ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1},{\mathcal{T}}_{t + 1}$
返回${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1},{\mathcal{T}}_{t + 1}$


---



### 4.3 AEGIS Architecture
### 4.3 AEGIS 架构


AEGIS is the harness-evolution engine of HarnessX. It comprises four stages arranged in a predefined workflow-Digester, Planner, Evolver, Critic-all driven by the same meta-agent LLM, which selectively invokes them: no external router decides stage execution; instead, the meta-agent itself determines at each stage whether sufficient signal exists to continue. The Digester, Planner, and Evolver each evaluate a continuation condition and may short-circuit the round (below-threshold actionability, empty landscape, or zero viable candidates), while the Critic together with the deterministic gating layer is mandatory for every candidate that reaches it.
AEGIS 是 HarnessX 的基准级 harness 演进引擎。它包含四个阶段，按预设工作流排列——Digester、Planner、Evolver、Critic——并由同一个元智能体 LLM 驱动，由它选择性调用：没有外部路由器决定阶段执行；相反，元智能体会在每个阶段自行判断是否存在足够信号以继续。Digester、Planner 和 Evolver 各自评估是否应继续的条件，并可能短路该轮（低于阈值的可执行性、空的局面，或零个可行候选），而 Critic 与确定性门控层一起，必须对所有到达它的候选执行。


No edit can ship without passing through the Critic and gate. The division of labor across stages addresses the pathologies of Section 4.2: the Digester compresses raw traces into structured task-level evidence; the Planner constructs an adaptation landscape spanning both incremental and structural changes; the Evolver produces typed builder edits with explicit change manifests; and the Critic, together with the gating layer, rejects edits whose claimed improvement lacks trace support or whose acceptance would regress previously solved tasks.
任何编辑都不能在未通过 Critic 和门控之前交付。各阶段分工用于应对 4.2 节中的病理：Digester 将原始轨迹压缩为结构化的任务级证据；Planner 构建一个覆盖增量与结构性变更的适配局面；Evolver 生成带类型的构建器编辑，并附带明确的变更清单；Critic 则与门控层一起，拒绝那些其声称改进缺乏轨迹支撑的编辑，或那些接受会回退先前已解决任务的编辑。


All stages share a single information substrate: the trace store, a structured record of execution events, verifier-scored outcomes, regression signals, and shipped or rejected edits. No stage consumes input beyond the trace store and the current harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ . Data flows forward through the pipeline with selective gating: the Digester may determine that no actionable failures exist (all tasks pass or signal is too sparse), terminating the round immediately; the Planner may find no viable adaptation landscape given the current evidence and edit history; and the Evolver may produce no type-safe candidates. In each case the round exits cleanly with a no-op outcome. Only the Critic and deterministic gate are unconditional: any candidate that survives the upstream stages must pass through both before shipping. The Critic may additionally issue a single revision request to the Evolver before returning its final verdict.
所有阶段共享单一信息载体：轨迹存储，一个结构化记录，包含执行事件、由验证器评分的结果、回归信号，以及已交付或被拒绝的编辑。任何阶段都不会超出轨迹存储和当前 harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ 之外消耗输入。数据沿流水线向前流动，并经过选择性门控：Digester 可能判定不存在可操作的失败（所有任务通过，或信号过于稀疏），从而立即终止该轮；Planner 在当前证据与编辑历史下可能找不到可行的适配局面；Evolver 也可能生成不了类型安全的候选。在每种情况下，该轮都会以无操作（no-op）结果干净退出。只有 Critic 与确定性门控是无条件的：任何在上游阶段存活的候选，在交付前都必须同时通过两者。Critic 还可能在给出最终裁决前，额外向 Evolver 发出一次单独的修订请求。


Digester. A single iteration on GAIA (103 tasks, pass@2) generates $\sim  {10}\mathrm{M}$ tokens of raw traces: model reasoning steps, tool invocations with their outputs, and timing metadata. Passing this volume directly to downstream stages exceeds context limits, yet naive truncation discards diagnostic signal. The Digester compresses each task's traces into a structured per-task summary: binary outcome, failure category (if any), implicated component identifiers, and supporting evidence excerpts. It also provides cross-iteration continuity: each task's summary links to its history of prior outcomes and shipped edits, enabling the Planner to distinguish persistent failures from transient noise.
Digester：对 GAIA（103 个任务，pass@2）进行一次迭代，会生成 $\sim  {10}\mathrm{M}$ 个原始轨迹 token：模型推理步骤、带输出的工具调用，以及时序元数据。若直接把这份规模的内容送入下游阶段，会超出上下文限制，但盲目截断又会丢弃诊断信号。Digester 将每个任务的轨迹压缩为结构化的、逐任务的摘要：二元结果、失败类别（如有）、涉及的组件标识符，以及支撑证据片段。它还提供跨迭代的连续性：每个任务的摘要都会链接到其先前结果历史与已交付编辑的记录，使 Planner 能区分持续性失败与偶发噪声。


Planner. The Planner receives the Digester's output (task-level summaries enriched with cross-iteration history) and constructs an adaptation landscape: which tasks are failing, what edits have been attempted, which components are implicated, and which edit types (prompt, tool, processor, configuration) remain untried. This stage is the primary defense against under-exploration: by constructing the landscape before edit generation, it prevents the pipeline from converging on trace-conditional local repair, ensuring that structural changes (tool additions, processor rewrites, memory-policy redesigns) are considered alongside incremental prompt edits.
Planner：Planner 接收 Digester 的输出（逐任务摘要，并融合跨迭代历史），并构建适配局面：哪些任务正在失败、尝试过哪些编辑、涉及哪些组件，以及哪些编辑类型（提示、工具、处理器、配置）尚未尝试。该阶段是对“探索不足”的主要防线：通过在生成编辑之前先构建局面，它能阻止流水线收敛到基于轨迹条件的局部修补，从而确保结构性变更（添加工具、重写处理器、重新设计内存策略）与增量提示编辑一并被纳入考虑。


Evolver. Given the Planner's adaptation landscape, the Evolver produces one or more candidate harnesses ${\left\{  {\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{k}\right\}  }_{k = 1}^{{K}_{t}}$ ,each specified as a typed builder operation on the current harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ . Each candidate carries a change mannifest: the edited components, the intended behavioral effect, and the tasks expected to improve or regress. When introducing new processor code, the Evolver must also provide a smoke test confirming that the processor instantiates and runs on synthetic input without raising exceptions. The builder algebra guarantees type-safety (every candidate satisfies hook-type contracts and processor-composition rules) but not behavioral safety; an edit that type-checks may still produce non-local behavioral effects, detectable only by the Critic and gating layer.
Evolver：在给定 Planner 的适配局面的情况下，Evolver 生成一个或多个候选 harnesses ${\left\{  {\widetilde{\mathcal{H}}}_{t}^{k}\right\}  }_{k = 1}^{{K}_{t}}$ ，每个候选都被定义为对当前 harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ 的带类型构建器操作。每个候选都携带变更清单（change mannifest）：被编辑的组件、预期的行为效果，以及预计会改进或回归的任务。当引入新的处理器代码时，Evolver 还必须提供一个冒烟测试，用于确认该处理器会在合成输入上实例化并运行，且不会抛出异常。构建器代数保证类型安全（每个候选都满足 hook-type 合约与处理器组合规则），但不保证行为安全；即使某个编辑能通过类型检查，它仍可能产生非局部的行为影响，这只能由 Critic 与门控层检测出来。


Critic and gating. The Critic defends against reward hacking; the deterministic gating layer defends against catastrophic forgetting. The Critic evaluates each candidate by comparing its change manifest against trace evidence and assessing whether edits risk non-local effects through shared state or control flow. When gaps are detected, it issues a single revision request to the Evolver. After at most one revision cycle, the Critic returns either no_op or an ordered ship_ranking. The deterministic gate then applies acceptance checks in sequence: manifest completeness, configuration normalization (ensuring the candidate is in canonical form), build or smoke tests (when applicable), and the seesaw constraint (regression check on previously passing tasks; Section 4.1). The first failing check halts the sequence; passing candidates are committed and failing ones archived with their rejection reason. This decouples LLM judgment from acceptance: regardless of the Critic's recommendation, only deterministic checks govern shipping.
评审与门控。评审用于防止奖励投机；确定性门控层用于防止灾难性遗忘。评审通过将每个候选的变更清单与追踪证据进行对照，并评估所作修改是否会通过共享状态或控制流带来非局部影响，从而对每个候选进行评估。若发现缺口，则向演化器发出一次性的修订请求。至多一个修订周期后，评审返回 no_op 或一个有序的 ship_ranking。随后，确定性门按顺序执行接收检查：变更清单的完整性、配置规范化（确保候选处于规范形式）、构建或冒烟测试（如适用），以及跷跷板约束（对先前已通过的任务进行回归检查；第4.1节）。一旦某项检查失败即中止流程；通过的候选将被提交，失败的则归档并附上被拒原因。这样就将 LLM 的判断与接收流程解耦：无论评审的建议为何，只有确定性检查才能决定是否发版。


Design principle. Language-model subagents explore, hypothesize, and propose; typed structure and deterministic gates determine what ships. This separation ensures that safety properties (no regression, no unaudited edits) hold regardless of LLM subagent failure modes.
设计原则。语言模型子智能体负责探索、提出假设并给出方案；类型化结构与确定性门控决定最终发版内容。这样的分离确保安全性质（不回归、不未经审计的修改）在无论语言模型子智能体的失败模式如何时都能成立。


### 4.4 The Adaptation Loop
### 4.4 适应循环


Algorithm 1 formalizes the adaptation loop (each iteration corresponds to one "round" in Section 6). Starting from an initial harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{0}$ ,each iteration executes the current harness on an adaptation batch and selectively invokes the four stages: the Digester, Planner, and Evolver each gate on a continuation condition (sufficient actionability, non-empty landscape, and at least one type-safe candidate, respectively), while the Critic and deterministic gate are mandatory for any candidate that reaches them. A round commits a new harness only when a candidate clears all acceptance checks.
算法 1 将适应循环形式化（每次迭代对应第 6 节中的一个“轮次”）。从初始 harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{0}$ 开始，每次迭代都在一个适应批次上运行当前 harness，并有选择地调用四个阶段：Digester、Planner 和 Evolver 各自由一个继续条件把关（分别是足够的可操作性、非空的 landscape，以及至少一个类型安全的候选项），而 Critic 和确定性 gate 对任何到达它们的候选项都是必经的。只有当某个候选项通过所有接纳检查时，一个轮次才会提交新的 harness。


### 4.5 Variant Isolation via Ensemble Routing
### 4.5 通过集成路由实现变体隔离


The adaptation loop (Section 4.4) maintains a single harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ . When tasks require conflicting behaviors,an edit that improves one subset may regress another; the seesaw constraint rejects it, protecting stability but discarding a locally beneficial change. Variant isolation lifts this limitation by maintaining up to $K$ harness variants $\left\{  {{\mathcal{H}}_{t}^{\left( 1\right) },\ldots ,{\mathcal{H}}_{t}^{\left( {V}_{t}\right) }}\right\}  \left( {{V}_{t} \leq  K}\right)$ and routing each task to the variant with the highest estimated success rate on that task's cluster across prior rounds. We term this mechanism Ensemble routing.
适应循环（第 4.4 节）维护单一的 harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$。当任务需要相互冲突的行为时，改进某一子集的编辑可能会使另一部分退化；摆锤约束会拒绝它，既保护了稳定性，也舍弃了局部有益的更改。变体隔离通过最多维护 $K$ 个 harness 变体 $\left\{  {{\mathcal{H}}_{t}^{\left( 1\right) },\ldots ,{\mathcal{H}}_{t}^{\left( {V}_{t}\right) }}\right\}  \left( {{V}_{t} \leq  K}\right)$ 并将每个任务路由到在该任务簇上、基于先前轮次估计成功率最高的变体，从而突破这一限制。我们将这一机制称为集成路由。


The gating layer distinguishes two outcomes per candidate: (1) the edit improves some tasks without regressing any, in which case it is applied to its target variant; or (2) it improves a subset while regressing others, in which case the system forks a new variant rather than rejecting the edit outright (retiring the lowest-performing variant if the pool is full). Once multiple variants exist, the seesaw constraint is scoped per-variant: a candidate targeting variant $k$ is tested only against tasks routed to $k$ ,so improvements to one cluster cannot regress another. This design predicts three properties validated in Section 6.3: (1) non-degrading aggregate trajectory (peak = final), (2) sustained exploration across more rounds, and (3) lower total token consumption.
门控层会为每个候选编辑区分两种结果：(1) 该编辑在不使任何任务退化的情况下改进了部分任务，此时将其应用于目标变体；或 (2) 它改进了某个子集，同时使其他任务退化，此时系统会创建一个新的变体，而不是直接拒绝该编辑（若池已满，则退役表现最差的变体）。一旦存在多个变体，摆锤约束就按变体分别适用：针对变体 $k$ 的候选项只会在路由到 $k$ 的任务上进行测试，因此对一个簇的改进不会使另一个簇退化。该设计预测了第 6.3 节验证的三个特性：(1) 总体轨迹不退化（峰值 = 最终值），(2) 在更多轮次中持续探索，以及 (3) 更低的总 token 消耗。


## 5 Harness-Model Co-Evolution
## 5 Harness-Model 协同进化


Sections 3 and 4 show that evolving the harness alone, with the foundation model held fixed, already delivers substantial gains, and that these gains are largest for weaker, smaller task agents, whose behavioral gaps a better harness most readily closes. Co-evolution does not displace that route; it extends it along a second axis. For a capability-limited small model, harness evolution eventually meets a scaffolding ceiling: once the harness exposes the right tools, context, and control flow, the binding constraint becomes whether the frozen model can actually exploit them, and no harness edit can supply reasoning capacity the model itself lacks.
第 3 和 4 节表明，仅仅在基础模型保持不变的情况下进化 harness，已经能带来显著收益，而且这些收益在较弱、更小的任务智能体上最大；更好的 harness 最容易弥合它们的行为差距。协同进化并不取代这条路径；它沿着第二个维度加以拓展。对能力受限的小模型而言，harness 演化最终会触及搭建（scaffolding）的上限：一旦 harness 暴露出正确的工具、上下文和控制流，约束就变成了冻结的模型是否真的能够利用它们——而 harness 的任何修改都无法补足模型自身缺乏的推理能力。


Symmetrically, training the model under a fixed harness meets a training-signal ceiling: newly acquired capabilities go unexercised when the scaffold never surfaces the context, tools, or control flow that elicit them. The model is the agent's cognitive core, supplying reasoning and planning, while the harness is its executive apparatus, determining what the model perceives, what it can invoke, and what constrains its execution. A sharper apparatus cannot compensate for a weak core, nor a stronger core for an apparatus that never calls on it. Co-evolution targets precisely this bottleneck: by training the model within the same loop that evolves its harness, the agent improves along both axes simultaneously, breaking the ceiling that either improvement alone would leave in place. The principle of jointly evolving complementary capability components also appears in other settings: ${\mathrm{K}}^{2}$ Agent [40] co-evolves know-what (declarative knowledge) and know-how (procedural skill) for hierarchical mobile device control.
对称地，在固定 harness 下训练模型也会触及训练信号上限：当脚手架从未呈现出能触发这些能力所需的上下文、工具或控制流时，新获得的能力就无法被使用。模型是智能体的认知核心，负责推理与规划；而 harness 是它的执行装置，决定模型会感知什么、能够调用什么，以及什么会约束它的执行。更锐利的装置无法弥补薄弱的核心，同样，一个更强的核心也无法弥补永远不去调用它的装置。协同进化正是瞄准这个瓶颈：通过在同一个循环中训练模型、同时演化它的 harness，智能体在两个轴上同步提升，打破单独改进任一方时留下的上限。共同进化互补能力组件的原则也出现在其他场景中：${\mathrm{K}}^{2}$ Agent [40] 为层级移动设备控制协同进化了“知道什么”（声明式知识）与“知道怎么做”（程序技能）。


Figure 3 illustrates the co-evolution mechanism. Rather than alternating between independent harness-evolution and model-training phases, HarnessX runs both within a single iteration over a shared replay buffer. We formalize the iteration (Section 5.1), describe the two optimization substrates (Section 5.2), specify the model training objective via cross-harness GRPO (Section 5.3), and characterize off-policy training over the shared buffer, the property that lets model RL run at no additional rollout cost (Section 5.4).
图 3 展示协同进化机制。HarnessX 并不是在独立的 harness 演化阶段与模型训练阶段之间交替运行，而是在对共享重放缓冲区的单次迭代中同时完成两者。我们在第 5.1 节形式化该迭代，在第 5.2 节描述两种优化底座；通过跨 harness 的 GRPO（第 5.3 节）给出模型训练目标，并在第 5.4 节刻画在共享缓冲区上的离策略训练——正是这一性质使得模型 RL 能在不增加额外 rollout 成本的情况下运行。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_11.jpg?x=203&y=219&w=1396&h=547&r=0"/>



Figure 3 The harness-model co-evolution loop. The agent $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t},{\mathcal{H}}_{t}}\right)$ runs the task batch ${B}_{t}$ under a fixed verifier and the observability layer; the resulting traces and rewards $\left( {\tau ,r}\right)$ enter a shared replay buffer $\mathcal{B}$ ,where cross-harness grouping pools trajectories of the same task across harness versions and computes group-relative advantages $\widehat{A}$ . The same buffer drives two updates over identical data: AEGIS harness evolution (Digester $\rightarrow$ Planner $\rightarrow$ Evolver $\rightarrow$ Critic,yielding the evolved harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1}$ ) and cross-harness GRPO (group sampling and a clipped GRPO objective, yielding the updated model ${\mathcal{M}}_{t + 1}$ ); both feed the next iteration.
图 3 harness-模型协同进化循环。智能体 $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t},{\mathcal{H}}_{t}}\right)$ 在固定的验证器与可观测性层下运行任务批次 ${B}_{t}$；由此产生的轨迹与奖励 $\left( {\tau ,r}\right)$ 进入共享重放缓冲区 $\mathcal{B}$。其中，跨 harness 的分组会在不同 harness 版本的同一任务轨迹之间进行聚合，并计算组相对优势 $\widehat{A}$。同一个缓冲区驱动两次对相同数据的更新：AEGIS harness 演化（Digester $\rightarrow$ Planner $\rightarrow$ Evolver $\rightarrow$ Critic，得到演化后的 harness ${\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1}$）以及跨 harness 的 GRPO（按组采样并使用一个裁剪的 GRPO 目标，得到更新后的模型 ${\mathcal{M}}_{t + 1}$）；两者共同喂给下一次迭代。


### 5.1 The Co-evolution Iteration
### 5.1 协同进化迭代


Co-evolution operates over the pair $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t},{\mathcal{H}}_{t}}\right)$ ,where ${\mathcal{M}}_{t}$ denotes trainable model parameters (relaxing the frozen-model assumption of Section 4) and ${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ denotes the harness configuration at iteration $t$ . The system maintains a fixed-capacity replay buffer $\mathcal{B}$ with first-in-first-out eviction. Each iteration proceeds as:
协同进化作用于一对 $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t},{\mathcal{H}}_{t}}\right)$，其中 ${\mathcal{M}}_{t}$ 表示可训练的模型参数（放宽第 4 节中冻结模型的假设），${\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ 表示迭代 $t$ 的工具架构配置。系统维护一个固定容量的回放缓冲区 $\mathcal{B}$，采用先进先出淘汰。每次迭代按以下步骤进行：


1. Rollout. Run $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t},{\mathcal{H}}_{t}}\right)$ on the adaptation batch ${B}_{t}$ ; the observability layer records each episode as a complete trace ${\tau }_{i}$ ,capturing every model turn,tool call,and tool result.
1. 推进。对适应批次 ${B}_{t}$ 运行 $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t},{\mathcal{H}}_{t}}\right)$；可观测性层将每个回合记录为完整轨迹 ${\tau }_{i}$，捕获每一次模型交互、工具调用以及工具结果。


2. Verification. A fixed verifier scores each trace into a scalar reward ${r}_{i}$ . Holding the verifier fixed keeps rewards comparable across harness versions, which the cross-harness advantage (Eq. 3) requires.
2. 验证。固定的验证器会将每条轨迹评为标量奖励 ${r}_{i}$。保持验证器不变能让不同工具架构版本之间的奖励保持可比性，而跨工具架构优势（式 3）所需的正是这一点。


3. Buffer insertion. Append each scored trace to the shared buffer $\mathcal{B}$ together with the harness version that produced it,so successive rounds accumulate rather than overwrite; FIFO eviction keeps $\mathcal{B}$ restricted to recent rounds.
3. 缓冲区插入。将每条已评分的轨迹连同产生它的工具架构版本 $\mathcal{B}$ 一同追加到共享缓冲区；因此后续轮次会累积而非覆盖；FIFO 淘汰保证 $\mathcal{B}$ 只保留最近几轮。


4. Harness evolution $\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  \operatorname{AEGIS}\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t},\mathcal{B}}\right) }\right.$ ,non-parametric,Section 4). The meta-agent reads the buffered traces as evidence of where the scaffold fails, proposes one discrete structural edit, and admits it only if the Critic and gating layer validate it.
4. 工具架构进化 $\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  \operatorname{AEGIS}\left( {{\mathcal{H}}_{t},\mathcal{B}}\right) }\right.$ ，非参数型，见第 4 节）。元智能体读取缓冲区中的轨迹作为脚手架失败位置的证据，提出一次离散的结构编辑，并仅当 Critic 与门控层通过验证时才接纳它。


5. Behavior log-probabilities. For the traces just added this round, run a forward pass under the generating model ${\mathcal{M}}_{t}$ to obtain the token-level log-probabilities ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}\left( {\tau }_{i}\right)$ and cache them for use in the GRPO loss; trajectories from earlier rounds reuse the values cached at their own insertion (Section 5.4).
5. 行为对数概率。针对本轮刚加入的那些轨迹，在生成模型 ${\mathcal{M}}_{t}$ 下做一次前向计算，得到令牌级对数概率 ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}\left( {\tau }_{i}\right)$，并缓存以用于 GRPO 损失；来自更早轮次的轨迹则重用其各自插入时缓存的值（第 5.4 节）。


6. GRPO update $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  \operatorname{GRPO}\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t},\mathcal{B}}\right) }\right.$ ,parametric,Section 5.3). Partition traces into per-task groups spanning harness versions, assign each a group-relative advantage, and take a clipped policy-gradient step with a KL anchor to the fixed reference.
6. GRPO 更新 $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t + 1} \leftarrow  \operatorname{GRPO}\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t},\mathcal{B}}\right) }\right.$ ，参数型，见第 5.3 节）。把轨迹按跨越不同工具架构版本的每个任务分组，为每组分配组相对优势，并带 KL 锚定到固定参考，执行一步截断的策略梯度更新。


7. Advance. Return to step 1 with the evolved pair $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t + 1},{\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1}}\right)$ .
7. 前进。用已进化的一对 $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{t + 1},{\mathcal{H}}_{t + 1}}\right)$ 回到步骤 1。


Every trace serves as both AEGIS diagnostic evidence and GRPO training signal. The harness evolution (step 4) and model update (steps 5-6) read the same buffer but neither conditions on the other's output within the same iteration; both must complete before the next rollout begins.
每条轨迹既是 AEGIS 诊断证据，也是 GRPO 训练信号。工具架构进化（第 4 步）与模型更新（第 5-6 步）读取同一个缓冲区，但在同一迭代内均不基于对方的输出作条件化；两者都必须在下一次推进开始前完成。


### 5.2 Optimization Substrates
### 5.2 优化底座


Harness side (non-parametric optimization). Harness evolution proceeds as in Section 4, drawing on the replay buffer $\mathcal{B}$ for trace evidence. The principal difference from standalone AEGIS is that $\mathcal{B}$ contains trajectories from multiple model checkpoints ${\mathcal{M}}_{0},{\mathcal{M}}_{1},\ldots ,{\mathcal{M}}_{t}$ ,exposing the Digester to behavioral variation from both model updates and harness edits.
Harness 端（非参数优化）。Harness 的演化沿用第 4 节的方法，借助回放缓冲区 $\mathcal{B}$ 来提供轨迹证据。与独立的 AEGIS 的主要区别在于，$\mathcal{B}$ 包含来自多个模型检查点 ${\mathcal{M}}_{0},{\mathcal{M}}_{1},\ldots ,{\mathcal{M}}_{t}$ 的轨迹，从而使 Digester 能够接触到来自模型更新与 harness 编辑两方面的行为差异。


Model side (parametric optimization via GRPO). The key design choice is the cross-harness grouping criterion (formalized in Section 5.3): all trajectories sharing a task identifier form one GRPO group regardless of which harness or model checkpoint produced them, so that within-group variation reflects strategy differences rather than sampling noise alone.
模型端（通过 GRPO 进行参数优化）。关键设计选择是跨 Harness 的分组准则（在第 5.3 节形式化）：所有共享任务标识符的轨迹组成一个 GRPO 组，而不管它们由哪个 harness 或模型检查点生成；因此，组内差异反映的是策略差异，而不仅仅是采样噪声。


Complementarity. The harness update makes discrete structural changes (adding a tool, replacing a control processor, restructuring the prompt) that cannot be expressed as parameter updates. The model update makes fine-grained behavioral adjustments (when to invoke which tool, how to phrase a query, when to terminate) that depend on high-dimensional in-context state and cannot be captured by symbolic specification. The harness defines coarse-grained strategy architecture; the model learns to exploit it.
互补性。Harness 更新会带来离散的结构性变化（添加工具、更换控制处理器、重构提示），这些变化无法用参数更新来表达。模型更新会做更细粒度的行为调整（何时调用哪种工具、如何措辞查询、何时终止），这些依赖高维的上下文状态，无法被符号化规范捕捉。Harness 定义粗粒度的策略架构；模型则学会加以利用。


### 5.3 Model Training via Cross-Harness GRPO
### 5.3 通过跨 Harness 的 GRPO 进行模型训练


We adopt Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) [33]. Formally, each trajectory in the buffer is generated as:
我们采用组相对策略优化（GRPO）[33]。形式上，缓冲区中的每条轨迹生成如下：


$$
{\tau }_{i} \sim  \operatorname{Agent}\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{k},{\mathcal{H}}_{k},{x}_{i}}\right) ,\;k \in  \{ 0,1,\ldots ,t\} , \tag{1}
$$



where $i$ is the $\left( {x,\tau }\right)$ index in the buffer $\mathcal{B},{\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ and ${\mathcal{H}}_{k}$ are the model checkpoint and harness used to roll out task ${x}_{i}$ into trajectory ${\tau }_{i}$ . Because FIFO eviction bounds the buffer to recent iterations,buffered trajectories come from model versions close to the current policy. Yet they differ markedly in strategy (tool selection, prompt structure,control-flow logic),a diversity that stems from the successive harness versions ${\mathcal{H}}_{0},\ldots ,{\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ . Unlike single-policy RL, where within-group variation reduces to stochastic sampling, here harness identity dominates that variation, which makes the cross-harness grouping criterion (Eq. 2) essential for meaningful advantage estimation.
其中 $i$ 是缓冲区 $\mathcal{B},{\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ 中的 $\left( {x,\tau }\right)$ 索引，${\mathcal{H}}_{k}$ 分别是用于将任务 ${x}_{i}$ 展开为轨迹 ${\tau }_{i}$ 的模型检查点与所用的 harness。由于 FIFO 淘汰机制将缓冲区限制在最近的迭代范围内，缓冲得到的轨迹来自与当前策略相近的模型版本。然而它们在策略上差异显著（工具选择、提示结构、控制流逻辑），这种多样性源自连续的 harness 版本 ${\mathcal{H}}_{0},\ldots ,{\mathcal{H}}_{t}$。与单策略 RL 不同，在单一组内的差异在此仅会简化为随机采样；而这里 harness 的身份决定了这种差异，因此交叉-harness 分组准则（式 2）对于有意义的优势估计至关重要。


Formally,for a task $x$ ,the trajectory group collects all traces of $x$ regardless of which $\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{k},{\mathcal{H}}_{k}}\right)$ pair produced them:
形式上，对于任务$x$，轨迹组会收集所有$x$的轨迹，而不论是由哪一对$\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{k},{\mathcal{H}}_{k}}\right)$生成的：


$$
{\mathcal{G}}_{x} = \left\{  {{\tau }_{i} \in  \mathcal{B} \mid  \operatorname{task}\left( {\tau }_{i}\right)  = x}\right\}   = \mathop{\bigcup }\limits_{k}\left\{  {\tau  \sim  \operatorname{Agent}\left( {{\mathcal{M}}_{k},{\mathcal{H}}_{k},x}\right) }\right\}  . \tag{2}
$$



The model therefore receives gradient signal from inter-strategy reward contrasts, rather than from stochastic variation within a fixed strategy alone, which enables it to internalize strategies that succeeded across harness versions.
因此，模型接收到的是来自不同策略间奖励对比的梯度信号，而非仅来自固定策略内部随机变化的信号，这使其能够内化在各个 harness 版本中都表现成功的策略。


Task-level alignment, not action-level. Cross-harness GRPO performs task-level alignment: trajectories from different harness versions are grouped by task identity and compared by verifier reward alone. No action-level alignment is required, so harness versions with incompatible action spaces (different tool schemas, different prompt structures, different control-flow processors) coexist in the same group without conflict. When computing the policy gradient,each trajectory ${\tau }_{i}$ is replayed under the harness version ${\mathcal{H}}_{k}$ that produced it: the model’s log-probabilities ${\pi }_{\theta }\left( {{\tau }_{i} \mid  x}\right)$ are evaluated against the prompt,tool schema,and observation context that ${\mathcal{H}}_{k}$ would have constructed at each turn. The GRPO gradient thus operates entirely on model output tokens conditioned on harness-specific context, rather than on harness structural actions or environment transitions. This design decouples harness evolution (which may freely alter the action space across versions) from model training (which only requires token-level log-probabilities under each trajectory's own harness context).
按任务对齐，而非按动作对齐。跨 harness 的 GRPO 执行的是任务级对齐：来自不同 harness 版本的轨迹按任务身份分组，仅根据验证器奖励进行比较。无需动作级对齐，因此具有不兼容动作空间的 harness 版本（不同的工具模式、不同的提示结构、不同的控制流处理器）可以无冲突地共存于同一组中。在计算策略梯度时，每条轨迹${\tau }_{i}$都会在生成它的 harness 版本${\mathcal{H}}_{k}$下重新回放：模型的对数概率${\pi }_{\theta }\left( {{\tau }_{i} \mid  x}\right)$会根据${\mathcal{H}}_{k}$在每一步构建的提示、工具模式和观测上下文来评估。因而，GRPO 梯度完全作用于在各自 harness 上下文条件下的模型输出 token，而非 harness 的结构性动作或环境转移。该设计将 harness 演化（可在不同版本间自由改变动作空间）与模型训练（只需在各轨迹自身的 harness 上下文下计算 token 级对数概率）解耦。


The group-relative advantage is:
组相对优势为：


$$
\widehat{A}\left( {\tau }_{i}\right)  = \frac{{r}_{i} - \mu \left( {\mathcal{G}}_{x}\right) }{\sigma \left( {\mathcal{G}}_{x}\right)  + \epsilon }, \tag{3}
$$



where ${r}_{i}$ is the reward for trajectory ${\tau }_{i}$ ,and $\mu \left( {\mathcal{G}}_{x}\right) ,\sigma \left( {\mathcal{G}}_{x}\right)$ are the within-group reward mean and standard deviation. The evolving harness acts as a structured exploration operator for the model's RL: each new version injects a distinct mode of behavior into the task's sampling distribution, and the advantage in Eq. 3 commits the model toward whichever modes the verifier scores highest. The exploration breadth that single-policy sampling cannot provide is thus supplied by the evolving scaffold itself.
其中${r}_{i}$是轨迹${\tau }_{i}$的奖励，$\mu \left( {\mathcal{G}}_{x}\right) ,\sigma \left( {\mathcal{G}}_{x}\right)$是组内奖励均值和标准差。演化中的 harness 充当模型 RL 的结构化探索算子：每个新版本都会向任务的采样分布注入一种不同的行为模式，而式 3 中的优势则推动模型偏向验证器评分最高的那些模式。单策略采样无法提供的探索广度，因此由不断演化的支架本身提供。


The policy objective to maximize is:
要最大化的策略目标为：


$$
{\mathcal{J}}_{\mathrm{{GRPO}}}\left( \theta \right)  = {\mathbb{E}}_{x,{\tau }_{i} \sim  \mathcal{B}}\left\lbrack  {\min \left( {{\rho }_{i}\left( \theta \right) \widehat{A}\left( {\tau }_{i}\right) ,\operatorname{clip}\left( {{\rho }_{i}\left( \theta \right) ,1 - {\epsilon }_{c},1 + {\epsilon }_{c}}\right) \widehat{A}\left( {\tau }_{i}\right) }\right) }\right\rbrack   - \beta {D}_{\mathrm{{KL}}}\left( {{\pi }_{\theta }\parallel {\pi }_{\text{ ref }}}\right) , \tag{4}
$$



where
其中


$$
{\rho }_{i}\left( \theta \right)  = \frac{{\pi }_{\theta }\left( {{\tau }_{i} \mid  x}\right) }{{\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}\left( {{\tau }_{i} \mid  x}\right) },\;{\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}} = {\mathcal{M}}_{d}, \tag{5}
$$



is the importance-sampling ratio between the current policy ${\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ and the checkpoint ${\mathcal{M}}_{d}$ that generated ${\tau }_{i}$ (Eq. 1), ${\epsilon }_{c}$ is the clipping threshold,and $\beta {D}_{\mathrm{{KL}}}\left( {{\pi }_{\theta }\parallel {\pi }_{\mathrm{{ref}}}}\right)$ penalizes divergence from the fixed reference model ${\pi }_{\text{ ref }}$ . The behavior policy ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ in the ratio and the reference policy ${\pi }_{\text{ ref }}$ in the KL term are distinct: ${\pi }_{\text{ ref }} = {\mathcal{M}}_{0}$ is fixed throughout training,while ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ varies per trajectory and must be recovered from the buffer (Section 5.4).
是当前策略${\mathcal{M}}_{k}$与生成${\mathcal{M}}_{d}$（式 1）的检查点${\tau }_{i}$之间的重要性采样比率，${\epsilon }_{c}$是裁剪阈值，$\beta {D}_{\mathrm{{KL}}}\left( {{\pi }_{\theta }\parallel {\pi }_{\mathrm{{ref}}}}\right)$用于惩罚与固定参考模型${\pi }_{\text{ ref }}$的偏离。比率中的行为策略${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$与 KL 项中的参考策略${\pi }_{\text{ ref }}$是不同的：${\pi }_{\text{ ref }} = {\mathcal{M}}_{0}$在整个训练过程中保持固定，而${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$则随每条轨迹变化，必须从缓冲区中恢复（第 5.4 节）。


### 5.4 Off-Policy Training over a Mixed-Policy Buffer
### 5.4 在混合策略缓冲区上进行离策略训练


The replay buffer is intrinsically off-policy: at iteration $t$ it holds trajectories generated by checkpoints ${\mathcal{M}}_{0},{\mathcal{M}}_{1},\ldots ,{\mathcal{M}}_{t}$ under harnesses ${\mathcal{H}}_{0},{\mathcal{H}}_{1},\ldots ,{\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ (Eq. 1),so the buffer distribution does not match the policy ${\pi }_{\theta }$ under update. Recovering ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ for each buffered trajectory is the central off-policy challenge.
回放缓冲区本质上是离策略的：在迭代 $t$ 时，它保存了检查点 ${\mathcal{M}}_{0},{\mathcal{M}}_{1},\ldots ,{\mathcal{M}}_{t}$ 在支架 ${\mathcal{H}}_{0},{\mathcal{H}}_{1},\ldots ,{\mathcal{H}}_{t}$ 下生成的轨迹（式 1），因此缓冲区分布与更新时的策略 ${\pi }_{\theta }$ 不匹配。为每条缓冲轨迹恢复 ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ 是核心的离策略难点。


Behavior policy ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ . The importance ratio (Eq. 5) corrects the gap between ${\pi }_{\theta }$ and the checkpoint ${\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ that produced ${\tau }_{i}$ . Since ${\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ varies across the buffer, ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}\left( {\tau }_{i}\right)$ cannot be recovered from any single model: we materialize it at buffer insertion via one forward pass under ${\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ ,cache the token-level log-probabilities on disk, and reuse them at every gradient step. This decouples the cached behavior log-probabilities from the current log-probabilities ${\pi }_{\theta }\left( {\tau }_{i}\right)$ recomputed each step.
行为策略 ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ 。重要性比（式 5）用于修正由 ${\pi }_{\theta }$ 与产生 ${\tau }_{i}$ 的检查点 ${\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ 之间的差距。由于 ${\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ 在缓冲区中会变化，${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}\left( {\tau }_{i}\right)$ 无法从任意单一模型中恢复：我们在缓冲区插入时通过在 ${\mathcal{M}}_{k}$ 下进行一次前向传递来将其物化，在磁盘上缓存令牌级别的对数概率，并在每个梯度步骤中重复使用。这样就将缓存的行为对数概率与每一步重新计算得到的当前对数概率 ${\pi }_{\theta }\left( {\tau }_{i}\right)$ 解耦开来。


Bounded off-policy bias. FIFO eviction caps the buffer at $C$ trajectories; with $s$ samples per round the maximum model-version lag is $\lfloor C/s\rfloor$ rounds,so every cached ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ originates within a bounded window of ${\pi }_{\theta }$ and the policy that generated a trajectory never differs greatly from the one being updated. The same window bounds harness staleness, so the cross-harness groups (Eq. 2) mix only recent scaffold versions, and the model is never trained predominantly against an obsolete harness.
限制离策略偏差。FIFO 淘汰会将缓冲区限制在 $C$ 条轨迹；每轮 $s$ 个样本下，最大模型版本滞后为 $\lfloor C/s\rfloor$ 轮，因此每一条缓存的 ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ 都来自 ${\pi }_{\theta }$ 所限定的窗口内，生成该轨迹的策略与被更新的策略从未相差太多。同样的窗口也限制了支架的陈旧性，因此跨支架分组（式 2）只混合最近的支架版本，模型从不会主要在一个过时的支架上进行训练。


Replay reuse at no added rollout cost. The dominant cost of agentic RL is the rollout (executing the agent in the environment: model decoding, tool calls, and verification), not the gradient update. In co-evolution a single round of exploration produces one set of trajectories that serves both updates: the same traces drive the AEGIS harness update (Section 4) and, through the shared buffer (Section 5.1), the cross-harness GRPO model update. GRPO consumes these trajectories by replay and issues no rollouts of its own. The marginal cost of adding the model update is therefore confined to (i) one cached forward pass per trajectory to record ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ and (ii) the gradient steps themselves,both of which are rollout-free. No trajectory is generated solely to train the model. Joint optimization is therefore economical: it buys model improvement for the price of offline training compute alone, without any rollouts beyond those harness evolution already performs.
回放复用且不增加采样成本。智能体式 RL 的主要成本来自回放过程本身（在环境中执行智能体：模型解码、工具调用与验证），而不是梯度更新。在协同演化中，一轮探索会产生一组轨迹，同时服务于两次更新：同一份轨迹驱动 AEGIS 支架更新（第 4 节），并通过共享缓冲区（第 5.1 节）驱动跨支架的 GRPO 模型更新。GRPO 通过回放消费这些轨迹，并且不进行自身的额外回合采样。因此，添加模型更新所带来的边际成本仅限于 (i) 每条轨迹一次缓存前向传递以记录 ${\pi }_{{\theta }_{\text{ old }}}$ 以及 (ii) 其后的梯度步骤本身——两者都不需要额外采样。不会为了训练模型而单独生成轨迹。因此联合优化是划算的：它以离线训练计算本身为代价换取模型改进，而不需要除支架演化过程已经执行的那些之外的额外回合采样。


## 6 Experiments
## 6 实验


We evaluate HarnessX along five axes: overall effectiveness across benchmarks and model families (Section 6.2), the impact of variant-management strategies on stability (Section 6.3), the relative contribution of evolver architecture versus infrastructure (Section 6.4), gains from joint model-harness co-evolution (Section 6.5), and empirical confirmation of the predicted failure modes (Section 6.6).
我们从五个维度评估 HarnessX：在基准测试与模型家族上的总体有效性（第 6.2 节）、变体管理策略对稳定性的影响（第 6.3 节）、进化器架构相对于基础设施的相对贡献（第 6.4 节）、联合模型-样机协同进化带来的收益（第 6.5 节），以及对预测失效模式的实证验证（第 6.6 节）。


### 6.1 Experimental Setup
### 6.1 实验设置


Benchmarks. As summarized in Table 3, we evaluate on five benchmarks spanning multi-step retrieval, embodied planning, web interaction, multi-turn dialogue, and software engineering. Unless otherwise noted, each experiment runs for up to $T = {15}$ evolution rounds with early stopping after $P = 3$ consecutive rounds without a shipped edit. The full task set is evaluated every round (no subsampling). The meta-agent token budget varies by benchmark (100M-175M total) but is held constant across task agents within a benchmark.
基准测试。如表 3 所述，我们在五个基准上评估，覆盖多步检索、具身规划、网页交互、多轮对话和软件工程。除非另有说明，每次实验最多运行 $T = {15}$ 轮演化；若连续 $P = 3$ 轮都没有发布编辑内容，则提前停止。完整任务集在每一轮都会评估（不做抽样）。元智能体的令牌预算随基准而变化（总计 100M-175M），但在同一基准内，对所有任务智能体保持不变。


Table 3 Benchmark characteristics.
表 3 基准特性。


<table><tr><td>Benchmark</td><td>Domain</td><td>Sampled Tasks</td><td>Verifier</td></tr><tr><td>GAIA (Level 1-3)</td><td>Multi-step retrieval</td><td>103</td><td>Exact match</td></tr><tr><td>ALFWorld</td><td>Embodied planning</td><td>134</td><td>Goal completion</td></tr><tr><td>WebShop</td><td>Web interaction</td><td>100</td><td>Attribute match</td></tr><tr><td>${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench</td><td>Multi-turn dialogue</td><td>3 domains</td><td>Rule compliance</td></tr><tr><td>SWE-bench Verified</td><td>Software engineering</td><td>55</td><td>Patch resolution</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td>基准</td><td>领域</td><td>采样任务</td><td>验证器</td></tr><tr><td>GAIA（1-3级）</td><td>多步检索</td><td>103</td><td>精确匹配</td></tr><tr><td>ALFWorld</td><td>具身规划</td><td>134</td><td>目标完成</td></tr><tr><td>WebShop</td><td>网页交互</td><td>100</td><td>属性匹配</td></tr><tr><td>${\tau }^{3}$-Bench</td><td>多轮对话</td><td>3个领域</td><td>规则遵循</td></tr><tr><td>SWE-bench Verified</td><td>软件工程</td><td>55</td><td>补丁修复</td></tr></tbody></table>


Models. We distinguish two roles: the meta-agent (Claude Opus 4.6 unless otherwise noted) drives the AEGIS evolution loop; the task agent runs under the evolved harness to solve benchmark tasks. Task agents span three families (Claude Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5.4, and Qwen3.5-9B) to test whether a single meta-agent can evolve effective harnesses across model families.
模型。我们区分两种角色：元智能体（除非另有说明为 Claude Opus 4.6）驱动 AEGIS 演化循环；任务智能体在已演化的训练框架之上运行，用于完成基准任务。任务智能体覆盖三类模型（Claude Sonnet 4.6、GPT-5.4 和 Qwen3.5-9B），用于检验单一元智能体能否在不同模型家族中演化出有效的训练框架。


Baselines. (1) Static Harness: a HarnessX configuration constructed from published benchmark-specific prompts and tool definitions, held fixed across all rounds. (2) Claude Code SDK (CC SDK) ${}^{1}$ : a single-agent evolver (one LLM session per round) that replaces the four-stage pipeline while retaining the same infrastructure and round budget, isolating AEGIS's multi-stage architecture from the shared infrastructure (Section 6.4). This baseline also serves as a proxy for monolithic evolvers such as SICA [31].
基线。(1) 静态训练框架：由已发布的面向基准的提示词与工具定义构建的 HarnessX 配置，在所有轮次中保持不变。(2) Claude Code SDK（CC SDK）${}^{1}$：单智能体演化器（每轮一次 LLM 会话），在保留相同基础设施与轮次预算的同时，替代四阶段流水线；从而将 AEGIS 的多阶段架构与共享基础设施隔离开（第 6.4 节）。该基线也可作为如 SICA [31] 这类整体式演化器的代理。


Metrics. Task success rate (%) under the benchmark-specific verifier. Each task receives two independent attempts per round (pass@2: solved if either succeeds), reducing sampling noise while preserving a binary per-task signal for the seesaw constraint (at the cost of masking sub-threshold success-probability drift; Section 6.3).
指标。在基准专用验证器下的任务成功率（%）。每个任务在每轮获得两次独立尝试（pass@2：任一成功则视为解题），从而降低采样噪声，同时为 seesaw 约束保留每任务的二元信号（代价是会掩蔽低于阈值的成功概率漂移；第 6.3 节）。


Scope. All reported gains are measured on the same task set used for evolution; held-out generalization to unseen tasks is not evaluated in this work.
范围。所有报告的增益均在用于演化的同一任务集上测得；本文不评估对未见任务的泛化能力。


### 6.2 Main Results
### 6.2 主要结果


Table 4 and Figure 4 report pass@2 success rates before and after harness evolution. AEGIS improves 14 of 15 model-benchmark configurations, with an average gain of +14.5% (up to +44.0%). The single stagnating configuration (GAIA, GPT-5.4, Δ=0.0) reflects a fundamental limitation of single-harness evolution on heterogeneous task sets; Section 6.3 shows that variant isolation resolves this. One configuration regressed mid-run $\left( {{\tau }^{3}\text{ -Bench Telecom, } - {14.0}\% }\right.$ at R7) due to accumulated same-type edits,recovering by R9 (Section 6.6).
表4和图4给出了基准性能在采纳前后（harness evolution）的pass@2成功率。AEGIS在15种模型-基准配置中的14种上均提升，平均增益为+14.5%（最高+44.0%）。唯一停滞的配置（GAIA，GPT-5.4，Δ=0.0）反映了在异构任务集合上进行单一harness演化的根本性限制；第6.3节表明，变体隔离能够解决这一问题。另有一个配置在运行中途$\left( {{\tau }^{3}\text{ -Bench Telecom, } - {14.0}\% }\right.$（在R7）出现回退，原因是同类型编辑的累计；到R9恢复（第6.6节）。


Overall performance. Evolution improves 14 of 15 configurations. Gains range from +11.2% to +44.0% on ALFWorld, +13.0% to +18.0% on WebShop, and +10.9% to +18.2% on SWE-bench Verified. On GAIA, Sonnet 4.6 (+9.7%) and Qwen3.5-9B (+17.1%) improve,while GPT-5.4 stagnates ( $\Delta  = {0.0}$ ; resolving its failures demands mutually conflicting edits that no single-harness strategy can accommodate). On ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench, GPT-5.4 gains most (+14.5%) while Qwen3.5-9B gains only +1.1% due to its near-ceiling 93.5% baseline.
整体性能。演化使15种配置中的14种得到提升。在ALFWorld上增益范围为+11.2%到+44.0%，在WebShop上为+13.0%到+18.0%，在SWE-bench Verified上为+10.9%到+18.2%。在GAIA上，Sonnet 4.6（+9.7%）和Qwen3.5-9B（+17.1%）都有改进，而GPT-5.4停滞（ $\Delta  = {0.0}$ ；要修复其失败需要彼此冲突的编辑，而单一harness策略无法兼顾。在${\tau }^{3}$-Bench上，GPT-5.4增益最大（+14.5%），而Qwen3.5-9B仅提升+1.1%，因为其基线接近上限93.5%。


Inverse scaling with baseline performance. Across benchmarks, the weakest task agent (Qwen3.5-9B) consistently gains most: +44.0% on ALFWorld (baseline 53.0%), +17.1% on GAIA (baseline 20.3%), and +18.2% on SWE-bench Verified (baseline 23.6%). Stronger models (Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5.4) gain less on
与基线性能的反向缩放关系。跨各基准来看，最弱的任务代理（Qwen3.5-9B）始终提升最大：在ALFWorld上为+44.0%（基线53.0%）；在GAIA上为+17.1%（基线20.3%）；在SWE-bench Verified上为+18.2%（基线23.6%）。更强的模型（Sonnet 4.6、GPT-5.4）在

表4 主要结果（pass@2成功率，%）。Evolved=达到的峰值准确率。“_”表示领域平均结果，即不存在适用于单一峰值轮次的情况。
