ALFWorld (+11.2%, +20.9%) and SWE-bench (+10.9%, +18.2%). The exception is GAIA GPT-5.4 (Δ=0.0), where task heterogeneity prevents a single harness from improving aggregate accuracy—an observation that motivates the variant-isolation ablation in Section 6.3. The overall pattern suggests that weaker models exhibit more behavioral gaps addressable by harness-level edits; once baseline performance is sufficiently high, remaining failures increasingly require task-specific adaptations rather than global improvements.
ALFWorld（+11.2%，+20.9%）和 SWE-bench（+10.9%，+18.2%）。例外是 GAIA GPT-5.4（Δ=0.0）：任务异质性使得单一 harness 难以提升整体准确率——这一观察促成了第 6.3 节中的变体隔离消融。整体模式表明，更弱的模型会暴露出更多可通过 harness 级修改来弥补的行为差距；当基线性能足够高后，剩余失败越来越需要针对任务的适配，而非全局改进。


Cross-model generalization. The meta-agent (Opus 4.6) evolves harnesses for task agents across model families without family-specific adaptation. On ALFWorld, cross-family agents (GPT-5.4: +20.9%, Qwen3.5-9B: +44.0%) gain more than the same-family agent (Sonnet 4.6: +11.2%), indicating that gain magnitude tracks baseline performance rather than proximity to the meta-agent's family.
跨模型泛化。元代理（Opus 4.6）在不同模型家族中进化出面向任务的 harness，而无需针对家族做特定适配。在 ALFWorld 上，跨家族代理（GPT-5.4：+20.9%，Qwen3.5-9B：+44.0%）的提升幅度大于同家族代理（Sonnet 4.6：+11.2%），这表明增益大小取决于基线表现，而不是与元代理家族的接近程度。


Convergence rate tracks failure-mode concentration. ALFWorld (GPT-5.4) peaks at R4 and SWE-bench Verified (all agents) peaks at R2-R3; in both cases, failures concentrate in one or two component types, enabling rapid convergence. GAIA (Sonnet 4.6) requires 11 rounds because failures span four component types (prompt, tool, processor, configuration), forcing sequential exploration of multiple edit neighborhoods.
收敛速率与失败模式集中度一致。ALFWorld（GPT-5.4）在 R4 达到峰值，SWE-bench Verified（所有代理）在 R2-R3 达到峰值；在这两种情况下，失败都集中在一到两类组件上，从而实现快速收敛。GAIA（Sonnet 4.6）需要 11 轮，因为失败横跨四类组件（提示、工具、处理器、配置），迫使按顺序探索多个编辑邻域。


Domain-level variation within ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench. The averaged ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench gains mask substantial per-domain variation. GPT-5.4 gains +25.4% on Telecom (67.5% → 93.0% at R2) and +9.7% on Retail (84.2% → 93.9% at R6). However, Sonnet 4.6 on Telecom regresses -14.0% in a single round (R7) due to accumulated same-type edits, recovering by R9 (Section 6.6). This illustrates a structural limitation of per-edit gating: sub-threshold coupling from consecutive same-type edits accumulates undetected until a tipping point triggers visible regression.
在 ${\tau }^{3}$-Bench 内部的域级差异。平均后的 ${\tau }^{3}$-Bench 增益掩盖了显著的逐域波动。GPT-5.4 在 Telecom 上提升 +25.4%（67.5% → R2 时 93.0%），在 Retail 上提升 +9.7%（84.2% → R6 时 93.9%）。然而，Sonnet 4.6 在 Telecom 上在单轮（R7）出现 -14.0% 的回归，这是由于累积的同类型编辑导致；到 R9 时恢复（第 6.6 节）。这说明了一种按次编辑门控的结构性限制：连续同类型编辑带来的低于阈值的耦合会被忽视，直到达到拐点才触发可见的回归。


Post-peak degradation on SWE-bench. On SWE-bench Verified (GPT-5.4), evolution peaks at 63.6% (R3, +18.2%) but degrades to 50.9% by R5 (-12.7% from peak); final accuracy still exceeds the static baseline by +5.4%. Two factors accelerate degradation on this benchmark: (1) with only 55 tasks, each task flip shifts aggregate accuracy by $\sim  {1.8}\%$ (vs. $\sim  {1.0}\%$ at $n = {103}$ ),so fewer regressions suffice to produce visible decline; and (2) structural code edits have a broader blast radius than prompt edits. This parallels the GAIA GPT-5.4 stagnation: both cases motivate the variant-isolation strategy evaluated in Section 6.3.
在 SWE-bench 上的峰后退化。在 SWE-bench Verified（GPT-5.4）上，进化在 63.6%（R3，+18.2%）达到峰值，但到 R5 降到 50.9%（较峰值 -12.7%）；最终准确率仍比静态基线高 +5.4%。该基准上的退化加速由两点造成：（1）仅有 55 个任务时，每次任务翻转都会使聚合准确率变化 $\sim  {1.8}\%$（相对 $\sim  {1.0}\%$ 在 $n = {103}$ ），因此更少的回归就足以造成可见的下降；以及（2）结构性代码编辑的“影响范围”比提示编辑更大。这与 GAIA GPT-5.4 的停滞相呼应：两种情形都促成了第 6.3 节评估的变体隔离策略。


### 6.3 Evolution Strategy Comparison
### 6.3 演化策略对比


The main experiments (Table 4) use the Global strategy: a single harness evolved across all tasks. Table 5 compares this default with a variant-isolation strategy on GAIA (103 tasks, GPT-5.4, 15 rounds, AEGIS evolver).
主要实验（表4）采用全局（Global）策略：单个在所有任务上演化的 harness。表5将该默认策略与在GAIA上的变体隔离（variant-isolation）策略进行对比（103个任务、GPT-5.4、15轮、AEGIS演化器）。


Table 5 Evolution strategy comparison (GAIA, GPT-5.4, AEGIS evolver, 15 rounds). Final-Peak indicates stability; negative values signal catastrophic forgetting.
表5：演化策略对比（GAIA、GPT-5.4、AEGIS演化器、15轮）。Final-Peak表示稳定性；负值表示灾难性遗忘。


<table><tr><td>Strategy</td><td>Final (%)</td><td>Peak (%)</td><td>Final-Peak</td><td>Tokens</td></tr><tr><td>Ensemble (up to $K$ variants)</td><td>87.4</td><td>87.4</td><td>0.0</td><td>107.8M</td></tr><tr><td>Global (single harness)</td><td>49.5</td><td>73.8</td><td>-24.3</td><td>143.7M</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td>策略</td><td>最终（%）</td><td>峰值（%）</td><td>最终-峰值</td><td>Tokens</td></tr><tr><td>集成（最多 $K$ 个变体）</td><td>87.4</td><td>87.4</td><td>0.0</td><td>107.8M</td></tr><tr><td>全局（单一 harness）</td><td>49.5</td><td>73.8</td><td>-24.3</td><td>143.7M</td></tr></tbody></table>


Failure mechanism of Global. The Global strategy maintains a single harness for all 103 tasks. It peaks early at R4 (73.8%) before degrading steadily: subsequent edits introduce sub-threshold regressions that are individually undetectable under pass@2's binary signal yet compound into aggregate decline. The peak-final gap (-24.3%) far exceeds the per-round binomial 95% confidence interval (±8.5% at $n = {103}$ , $p \approx  {0.74}$ ),ruling out evaluation noise and confirming catastrophic forgetting (Section 4.2). This explains the $\Delta  = {0.0}$ stagnation for GAIA GPT-5.4 in Table 4: Global cannot sustain improvement on this heterogeneous task set.
Global 的失败机制。Global 策略为所有 103 个任务维护单一 harness。它在 R4（73.8%）早期达到峰值，随后持续下滑：后续编辑引入低于阈值的回归，这些回归在 pass@2 的二元信号下单独不可察，但累积起来会造成整体下降。峰值与期末差距（-24.3%）远超逐轮的二项分布 95% 置信区间（$n = {103}$ , $p \approx  {0.74}$ 各为 ±8.5%），从而排除评估噪声，并确认灾难性遗忘（第 4.2 节）。这解释了表 4 中 $\Delta  = {0.0}$ 在 GAIA GPT-5.4 上的停滞：在这个异构任务集合上，Global 无法维持改进。


Why Ensemble prevents cross-variant forgetting. Ensemble routing maintains up to $K$ harness variants and routes each task to the variant with the highest prior success rate. Edits are proposed and evaluated per-variant, so an edit improving one cluster cannot regress another. The comparison confirms three predicted properties: (1) non-degrading aggregate trajectory (peak = final), (2) later peak (R14 vs. R4), indicating sustained productive exploration, and (3) lower token consumption (107.8M vs. 143.7M), because each edit is evaluated only against its target cluster rather than the full task set, and edits target only their assigned cluster, avoiding the wasted proposals that accumulate when a degrading single harness is evaluated against all tasks.
为什么 Ensemble 能防止跨变体遗忘。Ensemble 路由最多保留 $K$ 个 harness 变体，并将每个任务路由到先验成功率最高的变体。编辑会针对每个变体提出并评估，因此改进某一簇不会回归到另一簇。对比结果验证了三个预期性质：（1）不退化的整体轨迹（峰值 = 期末），（2）更晚的峰值（R14 相比 R4），表明持续的有效探索，（3）更低的 token 消耗（107.8M vs. 143.7M），因为每次编辑只会与其目标簇进行评估，而不是与完整任务集；并且编辑只针对它们被分配的簇，从而避免了当一个退化的单一 harness 被应用到所有任务上时，那些会累积的无效提案。


Summary. Variant isolation resolves the stagnation observed under Global,lifting GAIA GPT-5.4 from $\Delta  = {0.0}$ to +13.6% (87.4%, non-degrading). Finer-grained strategies (Domain-aware clustering, Task-level tournament) were explored at pilot scale (30-40 tasks, ≤8 rounds) but lack sufficient rounds and tasks for statistically meaningful comparison.
总结。变体隔离解决了在 Global 下观察到的停滞，将 GAIA GPT-5.4 从 $\Delta  = {0.0}$ 提升到 +13.6%（87.4%，不退化）。我们在试点规模（30-40 个任务，≤8 轮）中探索了更细粒度的策略（领域感知聚类、任务级锦标赛），但由于轮次和任务数量不足，无法进行具有统计意义的对比。


### 6.4 Meta-Agent Effectiveness
### 6.4 元智能体效能


To disentangle evolver architecture from infrastructure, we replace the four-stage AEGIS pipeline with a single-agent CC SDK evolver that shares the same model (Opus 4.6), round budget, and infrastructure. Both evolvers run under variant isolation (introduced in Section 6.3) to ensure non-degrading trajectories. Table 6 reports the comparison on GAIA (103 tasks, GPT-5.4, 15 rounds).
为区分演进器架构与基础设施，我们用一个单智能体 CC SDK 演进器替换四阶段 AEGIS 流水线，该演进器共享相同模型（Opus 4.6）、轮预算与基础设施。两种演进器都在变体隔离下运行（见第 6.3 节），以确保轨迹不退化。表 6 汇总了在 GAIA 上的对比结果（103 个任务，GPT-5.4，15 轮）。


Table 6 Meta-agent architecture comparison (GAIA, GPT-5.4, variant isolation, 15 rounds). Both evolvers use Opus 4.6.
表 6 元智能体架构对比（GAIA、GPT-5.4、变体隔离、15 轮）。两种演进器都使用 Opus 4.6。


<table><tr><td>Evolver</td><td>Accuracy (%)</td><td>Best round</td><td>Tokens</td></tr><tr><td>AEGIS</td><td>87.4</td><td>R14</td><td>107.8M</td></tr><tr><td>CC SDK</td><td>86.4</td><td>R12</td><td>123.1M</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td>演化器</td><td>准确率（%）</td><td>最佳轮次</td><td>令牌</td></tr><tr><td>AEGIS</td><td>87.4</td><td>R14</td><td>107.8M</td></tr><tr><td>CC SDK</td><td>86.4</td><td>R12</td><td>123.1M</td></tr></tbody></table>


Accuracy is comparable; efficiency differs. The ${1.0}\%$ accuracy gap falls within one standard error ( $\sim  {3.3}\%$ at $n = {103}$ ),indicating that the four-stage decomposition does not improve final accuracy at this meta-agent capability level. However, the single-agent variant consumes $\sim  {14}\%$ more tokens (123.1M vs. 107.8M). We attribute this to the Digester’s compression: it reduces $\sim  {10}\mathrm{M}$ raw trace tokens to $\sim  {10}\mathrm{K}$ structured summaries before downstream stages consume them. Without this stage, the single-agent evolver must truncate traces to fit its context window, yielding less-informed edits that are rejected by the gate more frequently, wasting tokens on failed proposals.
准确性相当；效率不同。${1.0}\%$ 的准确率差距落在一个标准误范围内（$\sim  {3.3}\%$ 在 $n = {103}$ ），表明在该元智能体能力水平下，四阶段分解并未提升最终准确率。然而，单智能体变体会消耗 $\sim  {14}\%$ 更多 token（123.1M 对比 107.8M）。我们将其归因于 Digester 的压缩：它在下游阶段消耗之前，将 $\sim  {10}\mathrm{M}$ 的原始轨迹 token 压缩为 $\sim  {10}\mathrm{K}$ 的结构化摘要。缺少该阶段时，单智能体 evolver 必须截断轨迹以适配其上下文窗口，产生信息更少的编辑，而这些编辑更频繁地被门控拒绝，导致 token 浪费在失败的提案上。


Implication. With a capable meta-agent under variant isolation, accuracy gains derive primarily from HarnessX's infrastructure (typed components enabling isolation, structured traces enabling diagnosis) rather than the evolver’s internal architecture. The four-stage decomposition contributes efficiency ( $\sim  {12}\%$ fewer tokens) and interpretability (auditable intermediate artifacts) but not measurable accuracy at this scale.
含义。在隔离条件下具备能力的元智能体时，精度提升主要来自 HarnessX 的基础设施（用于隔离的类型化组件、用于诊断的结构化轨迹），而非 evolver 的内部架构。四阶段分解带来效率（$\sim  {12}\%$ 更少的 token）和可解释性（可审计的中间产物），但在该规模下无法衡量其准确率提升。


### 6.5 Co-Evolution
### 6.5 协同进化


This experiment tests whether interleaving harness evolution with model RL (Section 5) yields gains beyond harness-only evolution. As shown in Figure 5, we compare the two regimes on GAIA and WebShop using a Qwen3.5-9B task agent. Both conditions share a fixed-capacity FIFO replay buffer: each round runs the current agent on the adaptation batch, a fixed verifier scores the resulting traces, and both harness evolution (AEGIS) and model training (cross-harness GRPO) update over the same buffer (Section 5.1). Section 5 predicts that each single-optimization route stalls at its own ceiling: harness-only at the scaffolding ceiling, model-RL-only at the training-signal ceiling. Co-evolution addresses both ceilings by enabling the model to internalize strategies that successive harness versions introduce.
本实验检验：将工具框架进化与模型强化学习（第5节）交替进行，是否能带来超出“仅工具框架进化”的收益。如图5所示，我们在GAIA与WebShop上对两种模式进行比较，使用的是Qwen3.5-9B任务智能体。两种条件都共享一个固定容量的FIFO回放缓冲区：每一轮都会让当前智能体在适应批次上运行，一个固定的验证器会对得到的轨迹进行评分；随后工具框架进化（AEGIS）与模型训练（跨工具框架GRPO）都在同一缓冲区上更新（第5.1节）。第5节预测，每条单一优化路径都会在各自的上限处停滞：仅工具框架进化在搭建上限处停滞，仅模型RL在训练信号上限处停滞。协同进化通过让模型吸收连续的工具框架版本所引入的策略，从而同时突破这两个上限。


Experimental setup. We run both regimes on the GAIA text-only subset (103 tasks) and a WebShop subset (100 tasks) with a Qwen3.5-9B task agent. GAIA exercises live web tools whose latency and availability fluctuate, so each round is evaluated twice and averaged. Both subsets are small, so we set the optimizer batch to the entire replay buffer and size the buffer as a four-round sliding window: at two rollouts per task this is 824 traces on GAIA $\left( {{103} \times  2 \times  4}\right)$ and 400 on WebShop $\left( {{100} \times  1 \times  4}\right)$ ,which supplies enough within-group samples for GRPO to estimate advantages stably. Training uses learning rate $1 \times  {10}^{-6}$ ,GRPO clip $\epsilon  = {0.2}$ , no KL penalty (coefficient 0), and 5 training steps per round. The GAIA agent is equipped with web search (Baidu API), web fetch, bash, and file read; WebShop uses its environment's built-in action tools. Rewards are ${0.9} \times$ correctness plus ${0.1} \times$ format on GAIA,and WebShop’s native attribute-match reward (a task passes only at reward $= {1.0}$ ).
实验设置。我们在 GAIA 纯文本子集（103 个任务）和一个 WebShop 子集（100 个任务）上，使用 Qwen3.5-9B 任务代理运行两种方案。GAIA 会调用实时网页工具，其延迟和可用性会波动，因此每轮评估两次并取平均。由于两个子集都很小，我们将优化器批大小设为整个回放缓冲区，并将缓冲区大小设为四轮滑动窗口：在每个任务两次 rollout 的情况下，GAIA 上共有 824 条轨迹 $\left( {{103} \times  2 \times  4}\right)$，WebShop 上共有 400 条 $\left( {{100} \times  1 \times  4}\right)$，这为 GRPO 提供了足够的组内样本，以稳定估计优势。训练使用学习率 $1 \times  {10}^{-6}$、GRPO 裁剪 $\epsilon  = {0.2}$、不使用 KL 惩罚（系数为 0），并且每轮进行 5 步训练。GAIA 代理配备网页搜索（百度 API）、网页抓取、bash 和文件读取；WebShop 使用其环境内置的动作工具。奖励为 GAIA 上的 ${0.9} \times$ 正确性加上 ${0.1} \times$ 格式奖励，以及 WebShop 原生的属性匹配奖励（只有在奖励达到 $= {1.0}$ 时任务才算通过）。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_18.jpg?x=374&y=329&w=1051&h=363&r=0"/>



Figure 5 Co-evolution vs. harness-only evolution (AEGIS, model frozen) on GAIA and WebShop. Stars mark each method's peak; the shaded band is the co-evolution gain.
图5：在GAIA与WebShop上，“协同进化”与“仅工具框架进化”（AEGIS，模型冻结）的对比。星号标记各方法的峰值；阴影带表示协同进化带来的增益。


Co-evolution exceeds harness-only evolution. As Figure 5 shows, interleaving cross-harness GRPO with harness evolution over a shared replay buffer raises peak success on both benchmarks: GAIA 37.4% $\rightarrow  {41.7}\% \; \left( {+{4.3}\% }\right)$ and WebShop 49.0% $\rightarrow  {54.0}\% \left( {+{5.0}\% }\right)$ ,averaging +4.7% over the model-frozen baseline. The two curves coincide until joint training takes effect (R4), then diverge, with co-evolution at or above harness-only for the remainder of the run. The gap persists to the final round (GAIA 36.4% $\rightarrow  {39.8}\%$ ,WebShop ${46.0}\%  \rightarrow  {50.0}\% )$ and is wider on WebShop,where more room remains for model-level improvement beyond the harness-only plateau. Co-evolution thus lifts end-of-run accuracy, not merely the peak.
协同进化超过仅工具框架进化。如图5所示，在共享回放缓冲区上将跨工具框架GRPO与工具框架进化交替进行，能提升两个基准的峰值成功率：GAIA为37.4% $\rightarrow  {41.7}\% \; \left( {+{4.3}\% }\right)$，WebShop为49.0% $\rightarrow  {54.0}\% \left( {+{5.0}\% }\right)$，相较于模型冻结基线平均提升+4.7%。在联合训练生效之前（R4），两条曲线重合；之后分离，剩余训练过程中协同进化的表现始终达到或高于仅工具框架进化。该差距延续到最后一轮（GAIA为36.4% $\rightarrow  {39.8}\%$，WebShop为${46.0}\%  \rightarrow  {50.0}\% )$），且在WebShop上更大，因为在仅工具框架进化的平台之上，仍有更多空间供模型层面的改进。因此，协同进化提升的是训练结束时的准确率，而不仅仅是峰值。


Co-evolution breaks the scaffolding ceiling. Harness-only evolution plateaus at $\sim  {37}\%$ on GAIA and $\sim  {49}\%$ on WebShop. Co-evolution clears these plateaus: cross-harness GRPO enables the model to internalize strategies from successive harness versions, so later edits build on learned behavior rather than compensating for a fixed model's intrinsic limitations.
协同进化打破搭建上限。仅工具框架进化在GAIA上的$\sim  {37}\%$以及在WebShop上的$\sim  {49}\%$处出现平台。协同进化跨越这些平台：跨工具框架GRPO使模型能够吸收来自连续工具框架版本的策略，因此后续编辑是在已学到的行为基础上进行，而不是去弥补固定模型固有局限带来的问题。


### 6.6 Failure Analysis
### 6.6 失败分析


We present three case studies, one per pathology predicted by the operational mirror (Section 4.2): reward hacking, catastrophic forgetting, and under-exploration. For each case we document the detection signal that first surfaced the issue, the root cause identified through trace analysis, and the outcome- whether the pipeline self-corrected or required manual intervention. Figure 6 provides the full set of confirmed and pending cases organized by pathology type.
我们给出三个案例研究，每个对应操作镜像所预测的一个病理（第 4.2 节）：奖励黑客、灾难性遗忘，以及探索不足。对于每个案例，我们记录首次暴露问题的检测信号、通过追踪分析确定的根本原因，以及结果——流程是自行纠正还是需要人工介入。图 6 汇总了按病理类型组织的所有已确认与待确认案例。


Reward hacking (GAIA, Sonnet 4.6, R10). At R10, the pipeline shipped a composite edit (tool + prompt + configuration) whose manifest predicted improved retrieval. The edit passed the seesaw constraint and raised accuracy from 74.8% to 79.6%. Trace analysis at R11 revealed that the tool genuinely fixed retrieval for most newly passing tasks, but a subset passed by exploiting format regularities in the verifier rather than performing actual retrieval. The Planner flagged this pathway at R12, and the resulting edit introduced a guard restricting the tool to tasks whose output could be cross-checked against a second retrieval path.
奖励黑客（GAIA、Sonnet 4.6、R10）。在 R10，流程交付了一次复合编辑（工具 + 提示 + 配置），其清单预测检索将得到改进。该编辑通过跷跷板约束，并将准确率从 74.8% 提升到 79.6%。在 R11 的追踪分析中发现：工具确实为大多数新通过的任务修复了检索，但有一部分通过利用验证器中的格式规律“通过”，而不是执行真实检索。规划器在 R12 标记了这条路径，随后生成的编辑加入了一项保护机制：仅允许工具作用于其输出可与第二条检索路径交叉核验的任务。


Catastrophic forgetting ( ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench,Sonnet 4.6,Telecom,R7). Evolution on Telecom shipped same-type prompt/processor edits across five consecutive rounds (R2-R6), each appending a "reminder" rule. Compliance rose from 89.5% to 100% at R4, then regressed to 94.7% by R6 as later rules conflicted with earlier ones. The R7 Critic flagged the concentration risk ("All 5 prior ships occupy the same bucket: [prompt, processor]" but still approved the edit for shipping because ship-prediction accuracy remained high (R2-R6: 23/24, 5/6, $4/5,7/7,2/3)$ and no regressions were recorded. The sixth reminder degraded compliance from 94.7% to 80.7% (-14.0%) via cross-rule conflicts that destabilized previously passing tasks. This regression evaded the seesaw constraint because pass@2 registers only per-task binary flips, not sub-threshold coupling. The pipeline self-corrected by R9 once the Planner diagnosed the concentration pattern and proposed a structural edit that replaced the conflicting reminder stack.
灾难性遗忘（ ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench、Sonnet 4.6、Telecom、R7）。在 Telecom 上的演化期间，流程连续五轮（R2-R6）交付同类型的提示/处理器编辑，每轮都追加一条“提醒”规则。在 R4 时合规率从 89.5% 提升到 100%，随后到 R6 回落到 94.7%，因为后续规则与更早规则发生冲突。R7 的批判器标记了集中风险（“此前 5 次出货都落在同一桶里：[提示、处理器]”），但仍批准该编辑出货，因为出货预测准确率仍然保持较高（R2-R6：23/24、5/6、$4/5,7/7,2/3)$，且未记录任何回归）。第六条提醒使合规率从 94.7% 降至 80.7%（-14.0%），原因是跨规则冲突导致先前通过的任务不稳定。这一回归之所以躲过跷跷板约束，是因为 pass@2 只记录每任务的二值翻转，而不是阈值以下的耦合。等到规划器在 R9 诊断出集中模式并提出结构性编辑、替换冲突的提醒栈后，流程才自行纠正。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_19.jpg?x=425&y=210&w=945&h=1278&r=0"/>



Figure 6 Failure cases organized by pathology (rows: reward hacking, catastrophic forgetting, under-exploration).
图 6 按病理组织的失败案例（行：奖励黑客、灾难性遗忘、探索不足）。


Under-exploration (ALFWorld, Sonnet 4.6, R4-R7). Between R4 and R7, the pipeline shipped predominantly prompt-level edits,yielding $< 1\%$ gain per round. Ship-prediction accuracy (the fraction of manifest-predicted task flips that materialize) dropped from ${80}\% \left( {\mathrm{R}3}\right)$ to $0\% \left( {\mathrm{R}7}\right)$ ,signaling prompt-space exhaustion. The sole structural edit in this window (a processor-level change at R6) achieved only 14% ship-prediction accuracy (1/7 predicted flips materialized), suggesting that the Planner lacked sufficient structural-edit history to calibrate hypotheses beyond the prompt neighborhood.
探索不足（ALFWorld、Sonnet 4.6、R4-R7）。在 R4 到 R7 之间，流程主要交付的是提示级编辑，从而每轮带来 $< 1\%$ 的提升。出货预测准确率（即清单预测会翻转的任务中，实际发生翻转的比例）从 ${80}\% \left( {\mathrm{R}3}\right)$ 降至 $0\% \left( {\mathrm{R}7}\right)$ ，表明提示空间已被耗尽。该窗口期唯一一次结构性编辑（R6 的处理器级变更）仅达到 14% 的出货预测准确率（1/7 预测翻转实际发生），这表明规划器缺少足够的结构性编辑历史，无法在提示邻域之外对假设进行校准。


Summary. All three pathologies predicted by the operational mirror appear in practice. The pipeline detected and mitigated reward hacking within two rounds (R10-R12). Decaying ship-prediction accuracy diagnosed under-exploration (R4-R7). The catastrophic-forgetting case exposes a structural limitation of per-edit gating: sub-threshold coupling accumulates undetected until it exceeds the per-task detection threshold (Telecom R7). On ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench Telecom,the pipeline self-corrected (R8-R9) because the failure was localized to one domain; on GAIA (GPT-5.4),the same mechanism produces sustained stagnation $\left( {\Delta  = {0.0}}\right)$ because conflicting edits prevent any net gain. Section 6.3 shows that variant isolation resolves this by confining edits to task-specific clusters.
总结。操作镜像所预测的三种病理在实践中都出现了。流程在两个轮次内（R10-R12）检测并缓解了奖励黑客。出货预测准确率的衰减用于诊断探索不足（R4-R7）。灾难性遗忘案例暴露了基于单次编辑门控的结构性局限：阈值以下的耦合会在未被发现的情况下累积，直到超过每任务的检测阈值才被触发（Telecom R7）。在 ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench Telecom 上，流程自行纠正（R8-R9），因为失败局限于单一领域；而在 GAIA（GPT-5.4）上，相同机制会导致持续停滞 $\left( {\Delta  = {0.0}}\right)$，因为彼此冲突的编辑阻止了任何净增益。第 6.3 节表明，通过变体隔离可解决这一问题：将编辑限制在任务特定的聚类内。


## 7 Discussion
## 7 讨论


### 7.1 Why Compositional Structure Matters for Evolution
### 7.1 为什么组合结构对进化至关重要


As Table 5 shows, the Global strategy (used in all main experiments) peaks early at 73.8% (R4) on GAIA before collapsing to 49.5% (peak-final gap: -24.3%). Global uses HarnessX's typed components but does not leverage them for isolation; every edit is evaluated against all tasks jointly. Under pass@2, a task whose success probability has degraded can still register as "solved," so sub-threshold regressions evade the seesaw constraint. Preventing this collapse requires variant isolation, which composability enables: HarnessX's compositional structure makes the intended scope of each edit explicit, a precondition for variant isolation to confine each edit's evaluation to its target cluster rather than evaluating against the full task set indiscriminately (Section 6.3).
如表5所示，在GAIA上，Global策略（用于所有主实验）先在73.8%（R4）达到峰值，随后崩至49.5%（峰值-最终差：-24.3%）。Global使用HarnessX的类型化组件，但并未利用它们进行隔离；每次编辑都要在所有任务上联合评估。在pass@2下，成功概率已下降的任务仍可能被记为“已解决”，因此低于阈值的退化会绕过跷跷板约束。要阻止这种崩溃，需要变体隔离，而可组合性正提供了这一点：HarnessX的组合结构使每次编辑的预期作用范围显式化，这是变体隔离的前提，可将每次编辑的评估限制在其目标簇内，而不是无差别地对整个任务集进行评估（第6.3节）。


The relationship parallels type systems: types do not generate correct programs, but they make incorrect programs detectable. Analogously, typed components do not prevent bad edits, but make their scope explicit, enabling independent variation. The strategy comparison suggests that variant isolation is necessary for stable evolution (Global, which lacks it, degrades after peaking); without compositional structure, the intended scope of an edit is undefined, making variant isolation ill-posed. Compositional structure does not, however, guarantee bounded behavioral effects: the ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench Telecom failure demonstrates that accumulated same-type edits can induce sub-threshold coupling that degrades multiple dialogue patterns simultaneously.
这种关系与类型系统相似：类型不会生成正确程序，但能让错误程序可被检测。类似地，类型化组件并不能阻止糟糕的编辑，但能明确其作用范围，从而支持独立变化。策略比较表明，稳定进化需要变体隔离（缺乏这一点的Global在达到峰值后会退化）；若没有组合结构，编辑的预期作用范围就无从定义，变体隔离也就失去意义。不过，组合结构并不保证行为影响受限：${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench Telecom的失败表明，累积的同类型编辑会引发低于阈值的耦合，进而同时削弱多种对话模式。


### 7.2 The Role of Trace Richness
### 7.2 追踪丰富度的作用


HarnessX's full execution trace $\tau$ provides diagnostic information beyond a scalar reward. The case studies (Section 6.6) confirm this: detecting reward hacking on GAIA (shipped at R10, detected at R11) required inspecting how improvement occurred (format exploitation vs. genuine retrieval), and detecting under-exploration on ALFWorld (R4-R7) required tracking edit-type distribution and ship-prediction accuracy. Neither signal is recoverable from per-task binary outcomes alone.
HarnessX 的完整执行追踪 $\tau$ 提供了超越标量奖励的诊断信息。案例研究（第 6.6 节）印证了这一点：在 GAIA 上检测奖励投机（R10 上线、R11 检出）需要查看改进是如何发生的（格式利用 vs. 真正的检索）；在 ALFWorld 上检测欠探索（R4-R7）需要追踪编辑类型分布以及船预测的准确率。仅凭每个任务的二元结果，任一类信号都无法恢复出来。


These observations motivate a design principle: the richness of the feedback signal bounds the sophistication of evolution that can be safely performed. From scalar reward alone, none of the three pathologies is detectable: a score change cannot distinguish reward hacking from genuine improvement, under-exploration from convergence, or catastrophic forgetting from evaluation noise. Trace structure makes each pathology diagnosable, provided prior-round traces exist for comparison. The ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench Telecom failure illustrates the boundary: despite five rounds of prior traces (R2-R6), accumulated regressions evaded the seesaw constraint because no individual edit crossed the detection threshold. Structured trace recording is therefore necessary for detecting pathologies, but not sufficient for preventing them: when coupling accumulates below the per-task detection threshold, traces record the symptoms only after damage has occurred.
这些观察引出一个设计原则：反馈信号的丰富度决定了能够安全进行的进化复杂度。只靠标量奖励，三种病灶都无法被检测：评分变化无法区分奖励投机与真正的改进，也无法区分欠探索与收敛，更无法区分灾难性遗忘与评估噪声。追踪结构使每一种病灶都可诊断——前提是存在用于对比的前一轮追踪。${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench Telecom 的失效展示了边界：尽管已有五轮先前追踪（R2-R6），累积回归仍然绕过了跷跷板约束，因为没有任何单次编辑跨过检测阈值。因此，为了检测病灶，结构化追踪记录是必要的，但并不充分：当耦合在低于每任务检测阈值的水平下持续累积时，追踪只会在损害发生之后记录到症状。


### 7.3 Scope and Limits of the Operational Mirror
### 7.3 运行镜像的范围与限制


The RL-symbolic-space mirror is a design heuristic, not a formal framework. Classical RL convergence guarantees require sufficient exploration of the state-action space, a condition unattainable when states are symbolic harness configurations and actions are open-ended code edits. Under the Global strategy, GAIA (GPT-5.4) stagnates entirely ( $\Delta  = {0.0}$ over 15 rounds); the variant-isolation (Bedtion 6.3) recovers stable improvement (87.4% final = peak), but nothing guarantees this extends to longer horizons (where variants may over-specialize) or to task distributions whose inter-task dependencies prevent clean variant separation. The mirror also does not predict which pathology will dominate: on ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench Telecom, catastrophic forgetting surfaced at R7; on ALFWorld, under-exploration dominated R4-R7; on GAIA, reward hacking surfaced only at R10.
RL-符号空间镜像是一种设计启发式，而非正式框架。经典强化学习的收敛保证要求对状态-动作空间进行充分探索；当状态是符号化的Harness配置、动作是开放式代码编辑时，这一条件无法满足。在Global策略下，GAIA（GPT-5.4）完全停滞（$\Delta  = {0.0}$，15轮内）；而变体隔离（Bedtion 6.3）能够恢复稳定提升（87.4%最终=峰值），但无法保证这种效果能延伸到更长时间跨度（此时变体可能过度专化），也无法保证适用于那些任务分布：其任务间依赖关系会阻碍对变体进行清晰分割。该镜像同样无法预测哪种病理会占主导：在${\tau }^{3}$-Bench Telecom上，R7出现灾难性遗忘；在ALFWorld上，R4-R7期间主要是探索不足；在GAIA上，奖励投机仅在R10才出现。


We therefore treat the mirror as a design checklist rather than a predictive theory: it identifies failure modes to defend against but does not predict their ordering, timing, or relative severity. The three pathologies are representative, not exhaustive; additional RL phenomena (e.g., distribution shift when the adaptation batch diverges from deployment tasks, reward sparsity on hard benchmarks) may manifest as analogous failure modes in symbolic space.
因此，我们将该镜像视为设计清单，而不是可预测的理论：它用于识别需要防范的失效模式，但不预测其先后顺序、发生时机或相对严重程度。三种病理具有代表性而非穷尽；额外的强化学习现象（例如适应批次偏离部署任务时的分布漂移、在困难基准上的奖励稀疏）也可能在符号空间中以类似失效模式表现出来。


### 7.4 Generalization Across Model Families
### 7.4 跨模型族的泛化


On ALFWorld, the Opus 4.6 meta-agent evolves harnesses for task agents from three model families:
在 ALFWorld 上，Opus 4.6 元智能体会为来自三种模型族的任务智能体进化出工具链：


- Sonnet 4.6 (same family): ${83.6}\%  \rightarrow  {94.8}\% \left( {+{11.2}\% }\right)$
- Sonnet 4.6（同一族）：${83.6}\%  \rightarrow  {94.8}\% \left( {+{11.2}\% }\right)$


- GPT-5.4 (different family): ${76.9}\%  \rightarrow  {97.8}\% \left( {+{20.9}\% }\right)$
- GPT-5.4（不同族）：${76.9}\%  \rightarrow  {97.8}\% \left( {+{20.9}\% }\right)$


- Qwen3.5-9B (different family,weaker): ${53.0}\%  \rightarrow  {97.0}\% \left( {+{44.0}\% }\right)$
- Qwen3.5-9B（不同族，更弱）：${53.0}\%  \rightarrow  {97.0}\% \left( {+{44.0}\% }\right)$


The inverse-scaling effect (Section 6.2) explains the magnitude ordering: gains track inverse baseline performance (Qwen > GPT > Sonnet) rather than proximity to the meta-agent's model family. All three configurations hold the meta-agent fixed (Opus 4.6) while varying the task agent; we do not evaluate whether a weaker meta-agent can achieve comparable gains.
反向缩放效应（第 6.2 节）解释了幅度排序：增益随反向的基线表现而变化（Qwen > GPT > Sonnet），而不是取决于与元智能体模型族的接近程度。三种配置都将元智能体固定为 Opus 4.6，仅改变任务智能体；我们不评估更弱的元智能体是否能获得相当的增益。


A complementary ablation (Section 6.4) finds that a single-agent evolver achieves comparable accuracy to the four-stage AEGIS pipeline (86.4% vs. 87.4%, within sampling noise at $n = {103}$ ) when both share the same meta-agent model and infrastructure. This suggests that at this meta-agent capability level, the four-stage decomposition primarily provides efficiency gains ( $\sim  {12}\%$ fewer tokens) and auditability rather than measurable accuracy improvement.
互补的消融实验（第 6.4 节）发现：在共享相同的元智能体模型与基础设施时，单智能体进化器的准确率可达到与四阶段 AEGIS 流水线相当（86.4% vs. 87.4%，且在 $n = {103}$ 下的采样噪声范围内）。这表明在该元智能体能力水平上，四阶段分解主要带来效率收益（$\sim  {12}\%$ 更少的 token）和可审计性，而非可衡量的准确率提升。


### 7.5 Cost-Performance Tradeoffs
### 7.5 成本-性能权衡


As Table 7 details, evolution incurs upfront compute that amortizes over subsequent task invocations.
如表 7 所示，演进需要预先投入的计算成本，并在后续任务调用中摊销。


Table 7 Evolution cost summary. All main experiments use the Global (single-harness) strategy; the variant-isolation row is from the strategy ablation (Section 6.3).
表 7 演进成本汇总。所有主要实验都采用全局（单工具）策略；“变体隔离”一行来自策略消融（第 6.3 节）。


<table><tr><td>Experiment</td><td>Rounds</td><td>Total Tokens</td><td>Gain</td></tr><tr><td>GAIA, GPT-5.4 (Global)</td><td>15</td><td>143.7M</td><td>0.0% (peak = initial)</td></tr><tr><td>GAIA, GPT-5.4 (Variant isolation, ablation)</td><td>15</td><td>107.8M</td><td>+13.6%</td></tr><tr><td>ALFWorld, Sonnet 4.6 (Global)</td><td>7</td><td>43.4M</td><td>+11.2%</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td>实验</td><td>轮次</td><td>总 Tokens</td><td>增益</td></tr><tr><td>GAIA，GPT-5.4（全局）</td><td>15</td><td>143.7M</td><td>0.0%（峰值 = 初始）</td></tr><tr><td>GAIA，GPT-5.4（变体隔离，消融）</td><td>15</td><td>107.8M</td><td>+13.6%</td></tr><tr><td>ALFWorld，Sonnet 4.6（全局）</td><td>7</td><td>43.4M</td><td>+11.2%</td></tr></tbody></table>


The strategy ablation (Section 6.3) shows that variant isolation is both more effective (87.4% vs. 49.5% final) and more efficient (107.8M vs. 143.7M tokens) than Global on GAIA. The token reduction has two sources: (1) structurally, each edit under variant isolation is evaluated only against its target cluster rather than the full task set, reducing per-round evaluation cost; (2) under Global, the steadily degrading baseline causes more candidates to fail gating, wasting tokens on candidates that never ship. On benchmarks where evolution converges quickly (ALFWorld R4-R7, SWE-bench R2-R3), Global suffices and degradation does not materialize within the run horizon.
消融策略（第 6.3 节）表明，在 GAIA 上，变体隔离既更有效（87.4% 对比 49.5% 最终），也更高效（107.8M 对比 143.7M token）。token 减少有两方面来源：（1）结构上，在变体隔离下，每次编辑只在其目标簇内评估，而非在完整任务集上评估，从而降低每轮评估成本；（2）在 Global 下，持续退化的基线导致更多候选无法通过门控，使得 token 浪费在从未上线的候选上。在进化快速收敛的基准上（ALFWorld R4-R7、SWE-bench R2-R3），Global 就足够，且退化不会在本次运行的时间范围内显现。


The evolved harness also affects per-task inference cost. On GAIA, per-task token consumption drops by $\sim  {25}\%$ (targeted tool selection shortens trajectories); on ALFWorld,it rises by $\sim  {60}\%$ (task-decomposition prompts lengthen execution).
进化后的 harness 也会影响单任务推理成本。在 GAIA 上，单任务 token 消耗降低 $\sim  {25}\%$（定向工具选择会缩短执行轨迹）；在 ALFWorld 上则上升 $\sim  {60}\%$（任务分解提示会拉长执行）。


At deployment, the evolved harness is a static artifact requiring no meta-agent inference; tasks outside the evolution set are routed to the variant with the highest overall success rate on the evolution set. On GAIA, the upfront 107.8M tokens amortize within $\sim  1,{300}$ invocations ( $\sim  {83}\mathrm{\;K}$ tokens saved per invocation). On ALFWorld, per-task cost increases; the return is accuracy (+11.2%), not cost reduction.
部署时，进化后的 harness 是一个静态产物，不需要任何元智能体推理；进化集合之外的任务会被路由到在进化集合上总体成功率最高的变体上。在 GAIA 上，前期 107.8M tokens 会在 $\sim  1,{300}$ 次调用内摊销（每次调用节省 $\sim  {83}\mathrm{\;K}$ tokens）。在 ALFWorld 上，单任务成本会增加；回报是准确率提升（+11.2%），而非成本降低。


### 7.6 Ethical Considerations
### 7.6 伦理考量


Self-evolving agent systems require explicit oversight. HarnessX provides three mechanisms:
自演化智能体系统需要明确的监督。HarnessX 提供三种机制：


1. Auditability: every shipped edit carries a manifest and a rollback target; rejected candidates are archived with rejection reasons.
1. 可审计性：每一次发布的改动都附带清单和回滚目标；被拒绝的候选会连同拒绝原因一并归档。


2. Deterministic gating: the seesaw constraint rejects any edit that regresses even a single previously solved task under pass@2.
2. 确定性门控：跷跷板约束会拒绝任何会在 pass@2 下对先前已解决的任务造成倒退的改动，即使只影响其中一项。


3. Human-in-the-loop: the gating layer supports human approval for edits exceeding a configurable risk threshold (not exercised in our automated experiments).
3. 人在回路：门控层支持在改动风险超过可配置阈值时由人类批准（我们在自动化实验中未使用该机制）。


The ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench failure (Section 6.6) illustrates their limits: five consecutive same-type edits (R2-R6) accumulated sub-threshold coupling undetected by the seesaw constraint; the sixth edit (R7) triggered a visible $- {14.0}\%$ regression, yet no individual edit violated the constraint. This is a structural limitation of per-edit gating: sub-threshold regressions accumulate undetected regardless of how many prior rounds have demonstrated apparent stability under the same constraint.
${\tau }^{3}$-Bench 失败（第 6.6 节）展示了它们的边界：五次连续同类型改动（R2-R6）累积了低于阈值的耦合，未被跷跷板约束发现；第六次改动（R7）触发了可见的 $- {14.0}\%$ 回归，但没有任何单次改动本身违反该约束。这是逐条改动门控的结构性限制：低于阈值的回归会在未被发现的情况下不断累积，与先前经过同一约束验证出的表观稳定性无关，具体取决于之前进行过多少轮。


### 7.7 Limitations
### 7.7 局限性


Beyond the limitations noted above, five additional constraints bound the generality of our results:
除上述局限外，还有五项额外约束限制了我们结果的普适性：


- No held-out evaluation. All reported gains are measured on the same task set used for evolution. Since we report peak accuracy and evaluate on the adaptation set itself, the numbers carry both selection bias and potential overfitting. Generalization to unseen tasks within the same distribution is plausible but untested.
- 无留出评估。所有报告的提升都在与进化相同的任务集上测得。由于我们报告的是峰值准确率，并在适应集本身上评估，这些数字同时带有选择偏差和潜在过拟合。同一分布内对未见任务的泛化是可能的，但尚未验证。


- Discrete action spaces only. All experiments use agents with discrete, text-based action spaces. We have not tested whether the framework extends to continuous action spaces (e.g., robotic control).
- 仅限离散动作空间。所有实验都使用具有离散、基于文本的动作空间的智能体。我们尚未测试该框架是否可扩展到连续动作空间（例如机器人控制）。


- Closed-source meta-agent. AEGIS requires a meta-agent capable of multi-file code generation, structured trace analysis, and multi-step planning. Open-weight models approaching this capability level (e.g., Qwen3.5-72B, Llama-4-Maverick) remain untested as meta-agents.
- 闭源元智能体。AEGIS 需要一个能够进行多文件代码生成、结构化轨迹分析和多步规划的元智能体。接近这一能力水平的开源权重模型（如 Qwen3.5-72B、Llama-4-Maverick）仍未作为元智能体测试。


- Joint control assumption. Co-evolution requires joint control over both harness evolution and model training. In practice, these concerns are often separated across teams or organizations, making a shared replay buffer (Section 5.1) impractical without cross-team coordination.
- 联合控制假设。协同进化要求同时控制 harness 演化和模型训练。在实践中，这两项工作往往分属不同团队或组织，因此若无跨团队协作，共享回放缓冲区（第 5.1 节）并不现实。


- Benchmark coverage. All SWE-bench Verified runs use a 55-task subsample,and ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench evaluates only three domains (Retail, Airline, Telecom). Conclusions, particularly the inverse-scaling effect, may not generalize to domains with different task heterogeneity or to larger evaluation sets.
- 基准覆盖范围。所有 SWE-bench Verified 运行都使用了 55 个任务的子样本，而 ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench 仅评估了三个领域（零售、航空、通信）。结论，尤其是反向缩放效应，可能无法推广到任务异质性不同的领域，或更大的评估集。


## 8 Conclusion
## 8 结论


We present HarnessX, a composable runtime foundry that treats the harness as a first-class interface between model and environment. This interface can be composed from typed primitives, evolved from execution traces, and coupled with model training in a unified improvement loop. Across five benchmarks and three model families, HarnessX achieves gains up to +44.0% (average +14.5% across 15 configurations) through trace-driven evolution over a compositional substrate,with co-evolution adding +4.7% beyond harness-only evolution on two benchmarks. These results suggest that agent progress need not rely on model scaling alone: composing and evolving the runtime interface from execution feedback is a complementary and actionable lever, particularly for capability-limited agents where harness-level gains are largest.
我们提出 HarnessX，这是一种可组合的运行时工坊，将 harness 视为连接模型与环境的一级接口。该接口可由类型化原语进行组合，可由执行轨迹演化而来，并在统一的改进闭环中与模型训练协同。通过在一个由组合基底构成的框架上进行基于轨迹的演化，HarnessX 在五项基准与三类模型家族上实现最高 +44.0% 的增益（15 种配置的平均为 +14.5%）；同时，在两项基准上，co-evolution（协同演化）在仅 harness 演化之上又额外带来 +4.7%。这些结果表明，代理进步无需仅依赖模型规模扩展：从执行反馈中组合并演化运行时接口，是一种互补且可操作的杠杆，尤其适用于能力受限的代理，因为此时 harness 层面的增益最大。

## Appendix
## 附录


## A Experimental Setup: Full Details
## 一个实验设置：完整细节


This appendix expands the condensed setup of Section 6.1 with the full benchmark descriptions, the formal metric definitions, the evolution protocol hyperparameters, and the runtime infrastructure.
本附录在第 6.1 节简要设置的基础上，补充了完整的基准描述、严格的指标定义、进化协议的超参数以及运行时基础设施。


### A.1 Benchmarks
### A.1 基准测试


We evaluate on five benchmarks chosen to span the failure modes that harness design most affects, from short-horizon embodied planning to long-horizon software engineering.
我们在五个基准上进行评测，这些基准覆盖了最受搭建方式影响的失效模式，从短程具身规划到长程软件工程。


GAIA. The GAIA benchmark [25] poses real-world questions that are conceptually simple for humans but require an agent to compose multiple actions (web search, file extraction, multimodal interpretation, arithmetic) and evaluates via exact match against a reference answer. This benchmark stresses open-ended tool-based reasoning, where the harness dictates how evidence is collected and synthesized.
GAIA。GAIA 基准 [25] 提出对人类而言概念上很简单、但要求智能体组合多种动作（网页搜索、文件提取、多模态理解、算术）的现实世界问题，并通过与参考答案的精确匹配进行评估。该基准强调开放式的工具驱动推理，其中搭建方式决定了证据如何被收集与综合。


ALFWorld. The ALFWorld benchmark [35] involves embodied instruction following where a text-based agent commands a simulated robotic agent in household settings. Given a natural-language goal (e.g., "Put a cooled apple in the microwave"), the agent navigates rooms, identifies objects, and manipulates them via textual actions; performance is measured by goal-completion rate. This benchmark stresses multi-step planning and grounded search under a tight step budget. We use the 134 tasks from the valid-unseen set, spanning six task types: pick-and-place, pick-two-and-place, look-at-in-light, and three transform-then-place variants (heat, cool, clean).
ALFWorld。ALFWorld 基准 [35] 涉及具身指令跟随，其中一个基于文本的智能体在家居场景中指挥一个模拟机器人智能体。给定一个自然语言目标（如“把一个冷却过的苹果放进微波炉”），智能体需要在房间间移动、识别物体，并通过文本动作操控它们；性能以目标完成率衡量。该基准强调在严格步数预算下的多步规划与落地搜索。我们使用 valid-unseen 集中的 134 个任务，涵盖六种任务类型：pick-and-place、pick-two-and-place、look-at-in-light，以及三种 transform-then-place 变体（heat、cool、clean）。


WebShop. WebShop [44] is a web-interaction benchmark in which an agent acts as a customer in a simulated online store. Given a textual product description, the agent must search, browse product pages, select the best-matching item, and purchase it; scoring reflects how well the chosen product satisfies the request. We evaluate on 100 instances sampled with a fixed seed, each run as an independent shopping session.
WebShop。WebShop [44] 是一个网页交互基准，智能体在其中扮演模拟在线商店中的顾客。给定一段文本产品描述，智能体必须搜索、浏览商品页面、选择最匹配的商品并完成购买；评分反映所选商品对需求的满足程度。我们在使用固定随机种子采样的 100 个实例上进行评测，每个实例作为独立的购物会话运行。


${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench. ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench [45] is a multi-turn dialogue benchmark in which the agent plays a customer-service assistant that must satisfy a user request while obeying an explicit domain policy. Performance is measured by rule compliance across the full conversation. The benchmark stresses dialogue-policy adherence: the harness must prevent the agent from agreeing to disallowed actions across many turns. For evaluation, we select three domains from the benchmark: Retail, Airline, and Telecom.
${\tau }^{3}$-Bench。${\tau }^{3}$-Bench [45] 是一个多轮对话基准，智能体扮演客服助理，必须在遵守显式领域政策的同时满足用户请求。性能通过整段对话中的规则遵循情况衡量。该基准强调对话策略遵从：搭建方式必须防止智能体在多轮中同意被禁止的操作。评测时，我们从该基准中选择三个领域：Retail、Airline 和 Telecom。


SWE-bench Verified. SWE-bench Verified [13] is a human-validated subset of SWE-bench in which each task requires an agent to resolve a real GitHub issue by editing the corresponding repository so that the project's hidden test suite passes. This benchmark stresses repository-level code editing: navigating a large codebase, localizing the relevant fault, implementing a patch, and avoiding regressions in existing tests. For evaluation, we sample a 55-task subset from SWE-bench Verified and measure performance by patch resolution.
SWE-bench Verified。SWE-bench Verified [13] 是 SWE-bench 的一个经人工验证子集，其中每个任务都要求智能体通过编辑相应仓库来解决一个真实的 GitHub issue，使项目的隐藏测试套件通过。该基准强调仓库级代码编辑：在大型代码库中导航、定位相关故障、实现补丁，并避免对现有测试造成回归。评测时，我们从 SWE-bench Verified 中抽取 55 个任务的子集，并以补丁解决情况衡量性能。


### A.2 Evaluation-Set Design
### A.2 评估集设计


The sampled-task counts in Table 3 denote the fixed evaluation sets scored at each evolution round. GAIA uses a fixed 103-task set drawn across the three difficulty levels $\left( {{39}/{52}/{12}}\right)$ . ALFWorld uses all 134 tasks from the valid-unseen split. WebShop uses 100 tasks randomly sampled from the dataset with a fixed seed, with each task run as an independent shopping session. For ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench,we select three domains (Retail,Airline, and Telecom) and score the full task list within each selected domain. For software engineering, we use a 55-task subset sampled from SWE-bench Verified. The same evaluation set for each benchmark is re-scored at every round, so the curves in Appendix D measure round-over-round changes on fixed task sets rather than on moving samples.
表 3 中的抽样任务数量表示每次进化轮次所用的固定评估集。GAIA 使用从三个难度等级 $\left( {{39}/{52}/{12}}\right)$ 中抽取的固定 103 任务集。ALFWorld 使用有效未见（valid-unseen）划分中的全部 134 个任务。WebShop 从数据集中以固定种子随机抽取 100 个任务，每个任务都作为独立的购物会话来运行。对于 ${\tau }^{3}$-Bench，我们选择三个领域（零售、航空和电信），并对每个所选领域内的完整任务列表进行评分。针对软件工程，我们从 SWE-bench Verified 中抽取一个 55 任务子集。每个基准在每一轮都会重新评分同一评估集，因此附录 D 中的曲线衡量的是在固定任务集上的逐轮变化，而不是在滑动样本上的变化。


### A.3 Metric Definitions
### A.3 指标定义


Pass@k.For a configuration evaluated on a task set $D$ with $n$ rollouts per task,let ${r}_{i,j} \in  \{ 0,1\}$ denote the binary outcome of rollout $j$ on task $i$ . Let ${c}_{i} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = 1}}^{n}{r}_{i,j}$ be the number of successful rollouts for task $i$ . We report pass@ $k$ using the standard unbiased estimator,i.e.,the probability that at least one of $k$ sampled rollouts solves the task:
Pass@k。对于在任务集 $D$ 上评估、每个任务进行 $n$ 次 rollout 的配置，令 ${r}_{i,j} \in  \{ 0,1\}$ 表示任务 $i$ 上第 $j$ 次 rollout 的二元结果。令 ${c}_{i} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = 1}}^{n}{r}_{i,j}$ 为任务 $i$ 的成功 rollout 数。我们使用标准无偏估计器报告 pass@ $k$，即至少有一个从 $k$ 个采样 rollout 中解决任务的概率：


$$
\text{ Pass@k } = \frac{1}{\left| D\right| }\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{\left| D\right| }\left( {1 - \frac{\left( \begin{matrix} n - {c}_{i} \\  k \end{matrix}\right) }{\left( \begin{array}{l} n \\  k \end{array}\right) }}\right) . \tag{6}
$$



All evolution curves use pass@2 as the primary metric: each task receives two independent rollouts and is solved if either succeeds. This reduces sensitivity to single-rollout stochasticity while preserving a strict task-level criterion. Rollouts terminated by infrastructure failures (sandbox crashes, API timeouts) count as failures rather than being excluded, keeping results comparable to official leaderboard protocols.
所有演化曲线均以 pass@2 作为主要指标：每个任务获得两次独立 rollout，若任意一次成功则视为已解决。这降低了对单次 rollout 随机性的敏感性，同时保留严格的任务级判定。因基础设施故障（沙箱崩溃、API 超时）而终止的 rollout 计为失败，而非被排除，以保持结果与官方排行榜协议可比。


### A.4 Evolution Protocol and Hyperparameters
### A.4 演化协议与超参数


The hyperparameters used in our evolutionary algorithm are detailed in Table 8. In round 0, the baseline is a competent composed harness augmented with the benchmark-specific tool registry, rather than a minimal default. The plots therefore show gains relative to a competent initial harness. The meta-agent is Opus 4.6 across all experiments; task agents vary: Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5.4, and Qwen3.5-9B. Per-task step limits are determined by the benchmark in question since the interaction length varies greatly among tasks.
我们在进化算法中使用的超参数详见表8。在第0轮中，基线是一个经过工具注册表增强的、能力较强的组合式 harness，而非最小默认配置。因此，图中展示的是相对于一个能力较强的初始 harness 的提升。所有实验中的元代理均为 Opus 4.6；任务代理则有所不同：Sonnet 4.6、GPT-5.4 和 Qwen3.5-9B。由于不同任务的交互长度差异很大，每个任务的步数上限由相应基准决定。


Table 8 Evolution-protocol hyperparameters.
表8 演化协议超参数。


<table><tr><td>Symbol</td><td>Meaning</td><td>Value</td></tr><tr><td>${K}_{t}$</td><td>candidates proposed per round</td><td>4</td></tr><tr><td>seeds</td><td>random seeds per cell</td><td>3</td></tr><tr><td>noise threshold</td><td>ignored single-round pass-count delta</td><td>±5%</td></tr><tr><td>${\mathcal{H}}_{0}$</td><td>round-0 harness</td><td>Handcrafted base harness</td></tr><tr><td>meta-agent</td><td>drives Digester / Planner / Evolver / Critic</td><td>Opus 4.6</td></tr><tr><td>task agent</td><td>model executing benchmark tasks</td><td>Sonnet 4.6; GPT-5.4; Qwen3.5-9B</td></tr><tr><td>concurrency</td><td>parallel task rollouts</td><td>10</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5">max-steps</td><td>GAIA</td><td>20</td></tr><tr><td>WebShop</td><td>20</td></tr><tr><td>ALFWorld</td><td>15</td></tr><tr><td>${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench</td><td>200</td></tr><tr><td>SWE-bench Verified</td><td>200</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td>符号</td><td>含义</td><td>取值</td></tr><tr><td>${K}_{t}$</td><td>每轮提出的候选数</td><td>4</td></tr><tr><td>种子</td><td>每个单元的随机种子</td><td>3</td></tr><tr><td>噪声阈值</td><td>忽略的单轮通过次数增量</td><td>±5%</td></tr><tr><td>${\mathcal{H}}_{0}$</td><td>第0轮 harness</td><td>手工制作的基础 harness</td></tr><tr><td>元智能体（meta-agent）</td><td>驱动 Digester / Planner / Evolver / Critic</td><td>Opus 4.6</td></tr><tr><td>任务智能体</td><td>执行基准任务的模型</td><td>Sonnet 4.6；GPT-5.4；Qwen3.5-9B</td></tr><tr><td>并发度</td><td>并行任务展开</td><td>10</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5">最大步数</td><td>GAIA</td><td>20</td></tr><tr><td>WebShop</td><td>20</td></tr><tr><td>ALFWorld</td><td>15</td></tr><tr><td>${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench</td><td>200</td></tr><tr><td>SWE-bench Verified</td><td>200</td></tr></tbody></table>


### A.5 Runtime Infrastructure
### A.5 运行时基础设施


Every rollout runs inside a fresh environment instance re-attached per task, so that side-effects (a WebShop cart, an ALFWorld world state, a shell working directory) cannot leak between tasks. The runtime records each rollout's full trajectory (every model call, tool call, and environment observation) to the observability layer that the Digester subsequently compresses; the cross-round ledgers are aggregated from this log. Task rollouts execute at concurrency 10. The meta-agent runs at concurrency 4 with a 200-step limit per role. Co-evolution model training uses $8 \times$ H100 GPUs with batch size 256 and learning rate $1 \times  {10}^{-6}$ .
每次 rollout 都在为每个任务重新挂载的全新环境实例中运行，因此诸如副作用（一个 WebShop 购物车、一个 ALFWorld 的世界状态、一个 shell 的工作目录）都不会在任务之间泄漏。运行时会将每次 rollout 的完整轨迹（每一次模型调用、工具调用以及环境观测）记录到可观测性层，随后由 Digester 对其进行压缩；跨轮次账本会从该日志中汇总得出。任务 rollout 以并发度 10 执行。元智能体以并发度 4 运行，并且每个角色的步数上限为 200。协同进化模型训练使用 $8 \times$ 台 H100 GPU，批量大小为 256，学习率为 $1 \times  {10}^{-6}$ 。


## B Prompts and Harness Defaults
## B 提示词与 Harness 默认设置


This appendix reproduces the prompts that drive the AEGIS outer loop and the Round-0 task-agent defaults. The blocks below are the literal contents of the corresponding files in the repository as of the commit that produced the experiments in Section 6.
本附录复现了驱动 AEGIS 外层循环以及第 0 轮任务-代理默认设置的提示词。下方各代码块是仓库中对应文件在第 6 节所述实验生成时所使用的提交版本中的原文内容。

## evolver/system_prompt.md
## evolver/system_prompt.md


#Evolver -- Round \{\{ round \}\}
#Evolver -- 第 {{ round }} 轮


Your goal: produce concrete evolution candidates whose shipping will raise next round's benchmark pass rate. You decide how many candidates (K >= 1) -- one high-value candidate beats three speculative ones, but if two genuinely different directions both have strong evidence, produce both. Every candidate must be evidence-driven with citations to raw traces or digests.
你的目标：产出切实可行的演化候选项，其落地会提升下一轮基准测试通过率。你自行决定候选数量（K >= 1）——一个高价值候选胜过三个推测性候选，但如果两个真正不同的方向都有充分证据，就都给出。每个候选都必须有证据支撑，并引用原始轨迹或摘要。


##Your stance
##你的立场


This role is research, not maintenance. Your value is in creative, rigorous, breakthrough-level thinking -- not in iterating on the bucket the pipeline has shipped most recently. When evidence points to a structural lever the harness has never touched -- a new tool, a runloop parameter, a different processor-hook time point -- propose it, even when the bucket has an empty reputation. Do not let bucket history, gate-rejection fear, or implementation discomfort narrow your search. Follow the evidence.
这个角色是研究，不是维护。你的价值在于创造性、严谨、突破性的思考——而不是反复迭代管道最近刚发出的那个桶。当证据指向一个 harness 从未触及的结构性杠杆——一个新工具、一个 runloop 参数、一个不同的 processor-hook 时间点——就提出它，即使该桶的历史信誉为空。不要让桶历史、门控拒绝的恐惧，或实现上的不适感缩小你的搜索范围。遵循证据。


[... strategy-concern relay and revert/improve-prior-ship rules truncated ...]
[... strategy-concern relay and revert/improve-prior-ship rules truncated ...]


##Action space is what you can verify exists
##动作空间以你能验证存在的为准


The mutation space is bounded by the runtime, the reachable web, and the harness's current capability set. When a direction depends on something beyond these -- a package, an API endpoint, a tool you assume is installed -- the system treats unverified dependencies as hallucinations. You have `bash`, `web_search`, and `web_fetch` to confirm a capability exists before writing code
变异空间受运行时、可达网络以及 harness 当前能力集的约束。当某个方向依赖于这些之外的东西——某个包、一个 API 端点、你假定已安装的工具——系统会将未验证依赖视为幻觉。在为其编写代码之前，你有 `bash`、`web_search` 和 `web_fetch` 可用来确认某项能力确实存在

against it; record the confirmation in `capability_evidence`.

##Build -> verify -> iterate (mandatory for code candidates)
##构建 -> 验证 -> 迭代（代码候选必需）


For any candidate that introduces new executable code, you MUST complete this
对于任何引入新可执行代码的候选，你都必须在

在本会话中完成此循环，然后再写入清单：


1. Write the code to your scratch dir.
1. 将代码写入你的 scratch 目录。


2. Verify by actually running it -- not by reasoning about it. Two levels:
2. 通过实际运行来验证——不要靠推理。分两级：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Level 1 -- unit call works: instantiate the processor/tool, drive the
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 级别 1 -- 单次调用可用：实例化 processor/tool，驱动


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;async hook, assert the expected state mutation happened.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;异步钩子，并断言预期的状态变更已经发生。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Level 2 -- round-trip reaches the model: a unit call that returns does not
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 第 2 级——往返可达模型：一个调用返回的单元并不能


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;prove the agent sees the return. Simulate the path from your code to the
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;证明代理看到了该返回。模拟你代码到达


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;model's next input and assert the content survives it (provider serializer
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;模型下一次输入的路径，并断言内容能够在其中保留（工具的提供方序列化；处理器的下一流水线阶段）。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for tools; the next pipeline stage for processors).
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for tools; the next pipeline stage for processors).


3. Iterate if verification fails -- fix the bug, or pivot if the environment
3. 若验证失败就继续迭代——修复错误，或在环境


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;does not support what you assumed. Do NOT hide the failure in a try/except.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;不支持你所假设的能力时转向。不要用 try/except 来隐藏失败。


4. Attach the verifying output as `capability_evidence`. "I believe this will
4. 将验证输出作为 `capability_evidence` 附上。“我觉得这会


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;work" is not acceptable; paste the actual command and its output.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;起作用”不算；请粘贴实际命令及其输出。


A candidate whose new code has not been observed to work will burn a round's
若尚未观察到新代码能工作，那么候选者会因零次翻转而


ship slot for zero flips. Pure prompt-bucket candidates (no code asset) are
直接耗尽一个回合的飞船舱位。纯提示桶候选（没有代码资产）

不受此限制——反事实门提供了等效的冒烟检查。

#Critic -- Round \{\{ round \}\}
#Critic -- 第 {{ round }} 轮


Your goal has two parts, and both matter.
你的目标分两部分，两者都很重要。


##Part 1 -- Per-candidate verdict
##第 1 部分 -- 针对单个候选的裁决


Pick the single candidate (or multiple bucket-disjoint candidates) whose
选出唯一一个候选（或多个互不重叠的候选），其


shipping is most likely to raise next round's pass rate without hurting it. If
部署最可能提高下一轮的通过率且不会损害它。如果


none qualifies, no-op -- shipping a bad candidate is worse than nothing.
没有合格者，就不执行任何操作 -- 部署一个坏候选比什么都不做更糟。


Every verdict MUST explicitly address candidate-vs-config interaction. Read the
每个裁决都必须明确说明候选与配置的交互。阅读


candidate's `## Targeted Fix (which hooks / event fields / state slots it
候选的 `## Targeted Fix（它触及哪些 hooks / event fields / state slots）` 以及当前的 HarnessConfig。在你的裁决中回答：这个


touches) AND the current HarnessConfig. Answer in your verdict: does this
候选的变更面是否与父配置中已有的任何 processor、tool、prompt 子句或


candidate's mutation surface overlap with any processor, tool, prompt clause, or
config kwarg 重叠？如果是，说明这种重叠是否


config kwarg already in the parent config? If yes, argue whether the overlap is
（a）有意且安全（新组件取代了旧组件，而该候选的应用 YAML 已将其移除）或（b）是意外冲突，并构成


(a) intentional and safe (the new component supersedes the old one, which the



candidate's applied YAML has removed) or (b) an accidental collision and grounds



for rejection. A verdict that does not address this is incomplete and counts as
用于拒绝。未涉及这一点的裁决是不完整的，应计为


ask-more.
ask-more。


[... round-trip (Level-2) evidence check for tool/processor candidates truncated ...]
[... 工具/处理器候选的往返（Level-2）证据检查已截断 ...]


##Part 2 -- Portfolio audit
##第2部分 -- 组合审计


Even when every individual candidate is acceptable, step back and look at the
即便每个单独候选都可接受，也要退一步看


pattern across rounds (scoreboard.json, data/ship_outcomes.json):
跨轮次的模式（scoreboard.json, data/ship_outcomes.json）：


- For any lever item shipped in $>  = 2$ of the last 3 rounds with cumulative
- 对于在最近 3 轮中有累计的 $>  = 2$ 内交付的任一杠杆项，


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;hit_rate < 0.4, do NOT ship a candidate touching that lever again; flag it as
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;hit_rate < 0.4 的任何已交付杠杆项，不要再提交触及该杠杆的候选；将其标记为


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;strategy_concern. A single-round miss is likely k-sampling noise; only
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;strategy_concern。单轮失误很可能只是 k-sampling 噪声；只有


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;persistence across rounds is signal.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;跨轮次持续出现才是信号。


- Is there a bucket or cluster the Evolver has never touched, while a failure
- 是否存在 Evolver 从未触及过的某个桶或簇，而 digests/ 中的失败


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;pattern in digests/ suggests it is the right lever? Flag it.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;模式表明它才是正确的杠杆？把它标出来。


- Did this round's regressions.md list any regressed task? The Evolver was
- 本轮的 regressions.md 是否列出了任何回归任务？Evolver


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;required either to ship a candidate addressing each regression or to write a
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;必须要么提交一个处理每个回归的候选，要么写一段


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"## Why this regression is acceptable" section. Reject the round (no-op) if
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;“## 为什么这个回归是可接受的”部分。如果两者都没做，拒绝该轮（no-op），并说明


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;neither path was taken, citing the missed task IDs.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;漏掉的任务 ID。


Record strategy_concern in decision.md's frontmatter only when the evidence is
仅当证据充分时，才把 strategy_concern 记录到 decision.md 的 frontmatter 中


concrete: name the bucket, the round range, the hit rate, the failing tasks.
具体说明：桶的名称、轮次范围、命中率，以及失败的任务。


Next round's Planner relays it to the Evolver. This is how you challenge the
下一轮的 Planner 会将其转交给 Evolver。这样你才能挑战


Evolver's strategy, not just its candidates.
Evolver 的策略，而不只是它的候选项。


[... independence rule, available-to-read guide, ask_evolver, and loader ground
[... 独立性规则，可供阅读的指南，ask_evolver，以及加载器的依据


truth truncated ...]
真相被截断 ...]


##Output
##输出


---



---



For each candidate, write `verdicts/V-<candidate_id>.md`:
对每个候选项，写入 `verdicts/V-<candidate_id>.md`：


---



candidate_id: <C-R\{\{ round \}\}-NN>
candidate_id: <C-R\{\{ round \}\}-NN>


verdict: <accept|reject|ask-more>
verdict: <accept|reject|ask-more>


evidence_anchors:
evidence_anchors:


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- trajectories/<file>#step_N
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - trajectories/<file>#step_N


---



##Reasoning
##推理


<Why this verdict. Cite the anchors. 2-4 short paragraphs.>



After all verdicts, write `decision.md`:
在所有裁决都写完后，写入 `decision.md`：


---



round: \{\{ round \}\}
round: \{\{ round \}\}


decision_type: <ship|no_op>
decision_type: <ship|no_op>


ship_ranking: # candidates to ship, in priority order
ship_ranking: # 待交付候选项，按优先级顺序


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- candidate_id: <C-R\{\{ round \}\}-NN>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - candidate_id: <C-R\{\{ round \}\}-NN>


strategy_concern: || # OPTIONAL -- fill only when the audit surfaces one
strategy_concern: || # 可选项——仅当审计提出需求时才填写


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<one concrete paragraph; cite ship_outcomes / task_history anchors>

##Reasoning
##推理


<3-6 bullets, one per verdict file, plus one bullet for any strategy_concern.>



Multi-ship: Stage 4 ships every listed candidate in order but skips any whose
多船：第4阶段按顺序交付每个列出的候选项，但会跳过任何已被更高排名的船占用其


bucket was already claimed by an earlier-ranked ship, so bucket-disjoint
bucket 的候选项，因此候选项若攻击的是正交的失效模式，可以同时交付。除非决策.md 能够被无误解析，否则


candidates attacking orthogonal failure modes can ship together. Nothing ships



unless decision.md parses cleanly.
不会交付。

### B.2 Round-0 Task-Agent Prompts
### B.2 第0轮任务-智能体提示


The composition-layer default $\left( {\mathcal{H}}_{0}\right)$ loads one system prompt per benchmark. We reproduce the ALFWorld default below as a representative example; the remaining benchmark defaults follow the same structure and are listed in the repository.
组合层默认 $\left( {\mathcal{H}}_{0}\right)$ 会为每个基准加载一条系统提示。我们在下方复现 ALFWorld 的默认设置作为示例；其余基准的默认配置遵循相同结构，并在仓库中列出。


---



## alfworld_evolver/systemprompt.md
## alfworld_evolver/systemprompt.md


#System
#系统


You are an expert agent operating in the ALFRED Embodied Environment. You drive
你是一个在 ALFRED 具身环境中运行的专家智能体。你通过


a live household simulator by calling the `act` tool, one admissible command per
调用 `act` 工具来驱动一个实时的家庭模拟器，每次调用只能发出一条允许的命令。


call. The environment replies with the next observation and the current
环境会返回下一条观察以及当前


admissible action list.
允许的动作列表。


##Output Discipline
##输出规范


- One `act` call per turn. No chaining ("go to fridge 1 and open it").
- 每回合只进行一次 `act` 调用。不要连用（例如“去冰箱1并把它打开”）。


- Pick the command verbatim from the admissible list. Anything outside that list
- 从允许列表中逐字选择命令动词。只要不在该列表内，


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is a silent no-op and wastes a step.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;就会静默无效果（no-op），并浪费一步。


- Reply with `FINAL ANSWER: done` only after you see `___ALFWORLD_DONE__` or
- 只有在观察中看到 `___ALFWORLD_DONE__` 或者


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;`___ALFWORLD_FAILED__` in an observation. Until then, keep calling `act`.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;`___ALFWORLD_FAILED__` 后，才回复 `FINAL ANSWER: done`。在此之前继续调用 `act`。


- If you genuinely cannot make progress for many consecutive steps, end with
- 如果你确实在许多连续步骤中都无法取得任何进展，就以


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;`FINAL ANSWER: give up`.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;`FINAL ANSWER: give up` 结束。


---



---



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;##Task Types
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;####任务类型


<table><tr><td>| Type</td><td>| Goal</td><td>| Key Steps |</td></tr><tr><td>| Pick & Place <br> take -> place |</td><td></td><td>$Y \mid$ Find $X \rightarrow$ take $X \rightarrow$ go to $Y \rightarrow$ put $X \mid$ <br> Y | Find X1 -> take -> place -> find X2 -></td></tr><tr><td>desklamp |</td><td>| Examine in Light | Examine X under desklamp</td><td>| Find X -> take X -> find desklamp -> use</td></tr><tr><td>| Clean & Place <br> go to $Y \rightarrow$ put |</td><td></td><td>| Find X -> take -> clean at sinkbasin -></td></tr><tr><td>| Heat & Place <br> to $Y \rightarrow$ put |</td><td>Heat X and put in/on Y</td><td>| Find X -> take -> heat at microwave -> go</td></tr><tr><td>| Cool & Place <br> Y -> put |</td><td>| Cool X and put in/on Y</td><td>| Find X -> take -> cool at fridge -> go to</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td>| 类型</td><td>| 目标</td><td>| 关键步骤 |</td></tr><tr><td>| 取放 <br/> take -> place |</td><td></td><td>$Y \mid$ 找到 $X \rightarrow$ 取 $X \rightarrow$ 前往 $Y \rightarrow$ 放置 $X \mid$ <br/> Y | 找到 X1 -> 取 -> 放置 -> 找到 X2 -></td></tr><tr><td>台灯 |</td><td>| 光下检查 | 在台灯下检查 X</td><td>| 找到 X -> 取 X -> 找到台灯 -> 使用</td></tr><tr><td>| 清洁并放置 <br/> 前往 $Y \rightarrow$ 放置 |</td><td></td><td>| 找到 X -> 取 -> 在水槽清洗 -></td></tr><tr><td>| 加热并放置 <br/> 到 $Y \rightarrow$ 放置 |</td><td>加热 X 并放入/放在 Y 中/上</td><td>| 找到 X -> 取 -> 在微波炉加热 -> 前往</td></tr><tr><td>| 冷却并放置 <br/> Y -> 放置 |</td><td>| 冷却 X 并放入/放在 Y 中/上</td><td>| 找到 X -> 取 -> 在冰箱冷却 -> 前往</td></tr></tbody></table>


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;##General Principles
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;####一般原则


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1. Decompose the goal into ordered sub-goals (locate -> acquire -> transform ->
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1. 将目标分解为按顺序排列的子目标（定位 -> 获取 -> 转换 ->


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;deliver) and complete each before moving on.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;送达），并在进入下一步前逐一完成。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2. Systematic exploration: search each surface and container at most once before
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2. 系统性探索：每个表面和容器在再次查看前最多搜索一次。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;revisiting. Open closed containers before judging them empty -- the
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;在判断封闭容器为空前先打开它们——


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;admissible list surfaces `open <recep>` when you arrive at a closed one.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;到达封闭容器时，允许列表会显示 `open <recep>`。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3. Grab immediately: when a required object appears, take it on the very next
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3. 立即抓取：当所需物体出现时，在下一步就拿起它，


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;step before moving elsewhere.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;再去别处移动。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4. Transform before placing: perform any clean/heat/cool state change at the
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4. 先转换再放置：在前往最终目的地前，先在


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;appropriate appliance before heading to the final destination.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;相应设备上完成任何清洁/加热/冷却状态变化。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5. Direct delivery: once holding the goal object, navigate straight to the
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5. 直接送达：一旦拿到目标物体，就直接前往


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;target receptacle and place it.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;目标容器并将其放入。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6. Track progress: keep an internal count of objects still to find and place.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6. 跟踪进度：在内部记录仍需寻找和放置的物体数量。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Only stop searching when the count reaches zero.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;只有当数量降为零时才停止搜索。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7. Avoid loops: never repeat the same action more than twice in a row. If stuck,
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7. 避免循环：同一动作不要连续重复超过两次。若卡住，


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;move to a different unexplored location.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;就移动到另一个未探索的位置。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8. Trust the admissible list: if `take X from Y` does not appear, you are not at
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8. 相信可接受列表：如果 `take X from Y` 不在其中，你就不能


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;$Y,Y$ is closed,or $X$ is not visible -- `go to`, `open`,or move on rather
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;$Y,Y$ 是关闭的，或 $X$ 不可见——应 `go to`、`open`，或转而继续


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;than guessing.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;而不是猜测。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;##Common Mistakes to Avoid
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;####常见错误避免


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Revisiting searched locations without new evidence.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 在没有新证据的情况下重复查看已搜索过的位置。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Ignoring visible objects -- if the target appears, take it immediately.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 忽视可见物体——如果目标出现，立即拿取。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Skipping the state change -- do not place an object before cleaning / heating
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 跳过状态变化——当任务要求时，不要在清洁 / 加热


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/ cooling it when the task requires it.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/ 冷却之前就放置物体。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Premature termination -- do not reply `FINAL ANSWER: done` before the env
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 过早结束——在环境发出 `__ALFWORLD_DONE__` 之前，不要回复 `FINAL ANSWER: done`。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;emits `__ALFWORLD_DONE__`.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;emits `__ALFWORLD_DONE__`。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Action loops -- repeatedly toggling or examining the same object wastes steps.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 动作循环——反复切换或检查同一物体会浪费步数。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Holding two objects at once -- you can only carry one. `put` the current one
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 同时拿着两个物体——你一次只能携带一个。拿下一个之前，先 `put` 当前的。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;before `take`-ing the next.



---



### B.3 Change-Manifest Schema
### B.3 变更清单架构


Each Evolver candidate is accompanied by a change manifest, a structured audit record linking the proposed edit to its evidence, mechanism, expected effect, and attribution signal. The manifest makes every harness modification falsifiable: the Critic checks whether the next round's trace features match the mechanism and impact the manifest predicted. Table 9 defines the manifest fields, and the schema below specifies their representation.
每个 Evolver 候选都会附带一份变更清单：这是一条结构化的审计记录，将拟议的编辑与其证据、机制、预期效果以及归因信号关联起来。该清单使每一次 harness 修改都可证伪：审稿者会检查下一轮的轨迹特征是否符合清单所预测的机制与影响。表 9 定义了清单字段，以下架构则规定它们的表示方式。


Table 9 Change-manifest fields. The manifest is the loop's evidence ledger: every shipped edit is falsifiable against the next round's trace-feature deltas.
表 9 变更清单字段。该清单是循环的证据账本：每一项交付的编辑都可与下一轮的轨迹特征增量进行证伪对照。


<table><tr><td>Field</td><td>Meaning</td></tr><tr><td>candidate id</td><td>Unique id, e.g. C-R3-01 (round 3, candidate 1).</td></tr><tr><td>bucket</td><td>Edit type: prompt, tools, config, or processor.</td></tr><tr><td>capability evidence</td><td>Verified claims that the edit mechanism actually works.</td></tr><tr><td>file changes</td><td>List of path / action / diff-summary edits.</td></tr><tr><td>predicted impact</td><td>Tasks the edit will unlock, stabilize, or put at risk: the falsifiable prediction.</td></tr><tr><td>attribution signature</td><td>Trace feature that must appear if the edit fired, e.g. a processor invocation.</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td>字段</td><td>含义</td></tr><tr><td>候选项 id</td><td>唯一 id，例如 C-R3-01（第 3 轮，第 1 个候选项）。</td></tr><tr><td>桶</td><td>编辑类型：提示、工具、配置或处理器。</td></tr><tr><td>能力证据</td><td>经验证的声明，表明该编辑机制确实有效。</td></tr><tr><td>文件变更</td><td>路径 / 操作 / 差异摘要的编辑列表。</td></tr><tr><td>预测影响</td><td>该编辑将解锁、稳定或带来风险的任务：可证伪的预测。</td></tr><tr><td>归因签名</td><td>如果该编辑生效，必须出现的可追踪特征，例如一次处理器调用。</td></tr></tbody></table>


change_manifest.yaml (schema)
change_manifest.yaml（schema）


candidate_id <round/candidate_id>
candidate_id <round/candidate_id>


bucket prompt | tools | config | processor
bucket 提示词 | 工具 | 配置 | 处理器


capability_evidence
capability_evidence


- \{type: python_package | filesystem | other, claim: "...", evidence: "..."\}
- \{type: python_package | filesystem | other, claim: "...", evidence: "..."\}


file_changes
file_changes


- \{path: "...", action: create | modify | delete, diff_summary: "..."\}
- \{path: "...", action: create | modify | delete, diff_summary: "..."\}


predicted_impact
predicted_impact


tasks_will_unlock [task_id, ...]
tasks_will_unlock [task_id, ...]


tasks_will_stabilize [task_id, ...]
tasks_will_stabilize [task_id, ...]


tasks_at_risk [task_id, ...]
tasks_at_risk [task_id, ...]

type processor_invocation | tool_call | prompt_feature
type processor_invocation | tool_call | prompt_feature


tool_name <name>
