## C Anatomy of an Evolution Step
## C 演化步骤剖析


To illustrate the AEGIS loop concretely, we walk through one full cycle, from Digester compression through Planner synthesis, Evolver editing, and Critic judgment, to the resulting trace delta. We select round 10 of the GAIA / Sonnet 4.6 run: a composite edit spanning a new tool, a prompt addition, and a configuration change. This multi-component intervention produced the largest single-round gain in that run, making it a richer illustration than a single-lever edit.
为具体说明 AEGIS 循环，我们完整走一遍：从 Digester 压缩，到 Planner 合成、Evolver 编辑，再到 Critic 判断，直至得到 trace 增量。我们选取 GAIA / Sonnet 4.6 运行的第 10 轮：一次复合编辑，涵盖一个新工具、一项提示词追加和一次配置变更。这个多组件干预带来了该次运行中单轮最大的收益，因此比单一杠杆式编辑更能说明问题。


### C.1 Worked Example: GAIA / Sonnet 4.6, Round 10
### C.1 工作示例：GAIA / Sonnet 4.6，第10轮


Failure evidence. Prior to round 10,the success rate stood at 74.8%, having dropped from its peak of 77.7% due to a regression in round 9. The Digester's trace analysis revealed a systematic failure pattern: every Wikipedia fetch in round 10's traces returned zero characters. WebFetch employs a browser if the website requires JavaScript support, but Wikipedia's new frontend fails to load correctly, timing out or returning an empty body. The traces make it plain: within task db4fd70a (number of stations in a rail line), db4fd70a_r0.jsonl#step_0 and #step_1 report that Wikipedia WebFetch fetches return 0 chars; similarly, within f0f46385 (ASEAN members' membership status), three consecutive WebFetch calls return 0 chars; ten separate attempts across the round returned empty responses.
失败证据。在第10轮之前，成功率为74.8%，因第9轮的回归而从77.7%的峰值下降。Digester 的轨迹分析揭示了一个系统性失败模式：第10轮轨迹中的每一次 Wikipedia 抓取都返回了零字符。WebFetch 在网站需要 JavaScript 支持时会使用浏览器，但 Wikipedia 的新前端无法正确加载，导致超时或返回空主体。轨迹清楚表明：在任务 db4fd70a（铁路线上的车站数量）中，db4fd70a_r0.jsonl#step_0 和 #step_1 报告 Wikipedia WebFetch 抓取返回 0 字符；同样，在 f0f46385（东盟成员国的成员资格状态）中，连续三次 WebFetch 调用都返回 0 字符；该轮共有十次独立尝试返回空响应。


Planner synthesis. The Digester grouped the 23 failed tasks by failure mode, surfacing a critical tool-level issue that the round-9 Critic had already flagged: the tools component had not shipped a fix in nine consecutive rounds despite source-access failures appearing since round 1. The Planner received two targets: (1) resolve the persistent tool-level source-access failures, and (2) revert the prompt and budget-processor changes responsible for the round-9 regression.
Planner 综合。Digester 按失败模式对 23 个失败任务进行了分组，暴露出一个关键的工具层问题：第9轮 Critic 早已指出，尽管自第1轮起就出现源访问失败，tools 组件却连续九轮都未交付修复。Planner 收到两个目标：(1) 解决持续存在的工具层源访问失败；(2) 回滚导致第9轮回归的 prompt 和 budget-processor 更改。


Evolver edit. The Evolver suggested C-R10-02, covering three buckets. (i) tools: new WikiTextFetch tool, avoiding the browser altogether by employing the MediaWiki API endpoint; returns complete text of the article, 10,529 chars in case of the rail line, 80,028 for ASEAN. (ii) prompt: a single sentence in the tool usage section instructing the agent to use WikiTextFetch before looking up Wikipedia articles. (iii) config: restore the round-8 baseline configuration, register WikiTextFetch, and remove the problematic budget processor. The manifest's capability evidence includes a Level-2 round-trip check (content serialized as a 10,529-char string by the provider); the attribution signature requires at least one WikiTextFetch call.
Evolver 编辑。Evolver 提议了 C-R10-02，涵盖三类变更。(i) tools：新增 WikiTextFetch 工具，完全绕过浏览器，改用 MediaWiki API 端点；返回文章完整文本，在铁路线案例中为 10,529 字符，在 ASEAN 案例中为 80,028 字符。(ii) prompt：在工具使用部分加入一句话，指示代理在查找 Wikipedia 文章前先使用 WikiTextFetch。(iii) config：恢复第8轮基线配置，注册 WikiTextFetch，并移除有问题的 budget processor。清单的能力证据包含一次 Level-2 往返检查（内容由提供方序列化为 10,529 字符串）；归因签名要求至少一次 WikiTextFetch 调用。

R10/candidates/C-R10-02.md

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;expected_min_calls 1
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;expected_min_calls 1


---



Critic verdict. The Critic approved only C-R10-02, rejecting the competing revert-only candidate C-R10-01. Its rationale covered three aspects. (i) Interaction: C-R10-02 is a strict superset of C-R10-01; both restore the round-8 baseline, so the budget-processor removal is intentional, not an accidental overlap. (ii) Round-trip evidence: the Critic verified Level-2 evidence (tool output arrives as a full string, not a truncation marker) before accepting any tools-bucket candidate. (iii) Portfolio: this is the first tools-bucket ship in ten rounds, and the trace evidence of persistent zero-char returns justifies the intervention that round-9 flagged.
Critic 判定。Critic 仅批准了 C-R10-02，拒绝了竞争性的“仅回退”候选 C-R10-01。其理由涵盖三点。（i）交互：C-R10-02 是 C-R10-01 的严格超集；两者都恢复了回合 8 的基线，因此移除 budget-processor 是有意为之，而不是不小心的重叠。（ii）往返证据：在接受任何 tools-bucket 候选之前，Critic 在验证关卡 2 证据（工具输出以完整字符串返回，而不是截断标记）。（iii）组合：这是十个回合里首次出现 tools-bucket 船，而回溯证据表明回合 9 标记的“持续零字符返回”确实存在，因此证明了当时的干预是合理的。


Delta realized. Post-shipping, the GAIA pass rate increased from 74.8% at R9 to 79.6% at R10 (+4.9pp, five tasks changed to pass), the greatest improvement during the entire run; five of the seven tasks the tool was predicted to affect flipped to pass (hit rate 0.71, the highest for any ship across all 19 runs). The improvement mainly occurred at Levels 2 (+4 tasks) and 3 (+2). Since the tool triggered its target tasks, the attribution condition was satisfied.
Delta 实现。交付后，GAIA 通过率从 R9 的 74.8% 提升到 R10 的 79.6%（+4.9pp，5 个任务从失败变为通过），这是整个运行中提升幅度最大的结果。被预测会受到该工具影响的 7 个任务中有 5 个翻转为通过（命中率 0.71，也是所有 19 轮中最高）。提升主要发生在 Level 2（+4 个任务）和 Level 3（+2）。由于该工具触发了目标任务，归因条件得到满足。


Figure 7 summarizes the same edit as a manifest card: the raw YAML above is what the loop logs, the card is the human-facing reading of it.
图 7 用清单卡的形式总结了同一处编辑：上方那段原始 YAML 就是循环记录的内容，而这张卡则是面向人类的可读版本。


## D Additional Results
## D 额外结果


The rest of this appendix is organized per benchmark. Each subsection is built around one figure of three panels: (a) a breakdown of the failure clusters the adaptation loop had to address, (b) the per-model distribution of harness levers the evolution shipped, and (c) a model-by-lever heatmap of each lever's effectiveness (tasks flipped to pass over tasks predicted). We read the three panels in order: what fails and why, how each model evolves, and whether the evolution closes the failures.
本附录其余内容按基准逐一组织。每个小节围绕一张包含三联图的图展开：（a）适应循环需要处理的失败簇拆解，（b）进化为每个模型交付的运筹杠杆分布，以及（c）各杠杆效力的模型-杠杆热力图（将任务预测为能通过的任务翻转以验证）。我们依次阅读三联图：失败是什么、原因是什么，各模型如何演化，以及演化是否能终结这些失败。


### D.1 GAIA
### D.1 GAIA


GAIA stresses general reasoning under tool use, and is the most lever-diverse benchmark in our suite. Figure 8 gives the three views we use throughout this appendix.
GAIA 强调在使用工具时的通用推理能力，是我们套件中杠杆种类最丰富的基准。图 8 给出了本附录中我们使用的三种视角。


Failure clusters and their causes. Panel (a) summarizes the failure clusters accumulated across the GAIA run. The dominant cluster is blocked-source (39%), where the agent cannot retrieve the required evidence because pages return empty content, require JavaScript rendering that times out, or contain incomplete information. Reasoning failures (33%) follow, covering tasks that require multi-hop inference, disambiguation
失败集及其原因。（a）面板汇总了 GAIA 运行期间累计的失败集。主要失败集是被阻断的源（39%）：智能体无法检索所需证据，因为页面返回空内容，需要 JavaScript 渲染但会超时，或包含不完整信息。推理失败（33%）紧随其后，覆盖需要多跳推断、消歧


C-R10-02 | GAIA / Sonnet 4.6 | round 10 | bucket: tools+prompt+config
C-R10-02 | GAIA / Sonnet 4.6 | 第 10 轮 | bucket: tools+prompt+config


Failure evidence
失败证据


Every Wikipedia WebFetch in the round's trajectories returns 0 chars (10+ calls across db4fd70a, fof46385, 42d4198c); the headless browser fallback times out on Wikipedia's frontend.
本轮轨迹中的每次 Wikipedia WebFetch 都返回 0 个字符（db4fd70a、fof46385、42d4198c 共 10+ 次调用）；在 Wikipedia 前端上，后备的无头浏览器会超时。


Edit
编辑


New WikiTextFetch tool calls the MediaWiki API for plain-text article content (tools); one prompt line routes Wikipedia lookups to it first (prompt); the round-8 baseline is restored and the regressing budget processor removed (config).
新的 WikiTextFetch 工具调用 MediaWiki API 获取纯文本文章内容（tools）；第一行提示将维基百科查询先路由到它（prompt）；恢复第 8 轮基线，并移除了会回归的预算处理器（config）。


Predicted fixes
预测修复


Unlock db4fd70a, f0f46385, 983bba7c, 08f3a05f, 5e2a91b0; stabilize 4b6bb5f7, 42d4198c.
解锁 db4fd70a、f0f46385、983bba7c、08f3a05f、5e2a91b0；稳定 4b6bb5f7、42d4198c。


Attribution signature
归因签名


tool_call on WikiTextFetch, ≥ 1 call; verified against the next round's trace.
对 WikiTextFetch 的 tool_call，≥ 1 次；已与下一轮的追踪记录核验。


Figure 7 Change manifest for C-R10-02 rendered as a manifest card, the human-facing counterpart of the logged YAML above.
图 7：针对 C-R10-02 的变更清单被渲染成清单卡片，即上方记录的 YAML 的面向人工的对应物。


of similar entities, numerical computation, or precise interpretation of underspecified queries. Figure/visual failures (11%) arise when the answer depends on information embedded in images, maps, or diagrams that text extraction alone cannot capture. Document/table parsing failures (11%) occur when evidence is locked in PDFs, structured tables, or semi-structured formats and the agent either misparses the layout or overlooks relevant cells. Scope ambiguity (6%) covers queries with multiple valid interpretations, where the agent answers a related but incorrect reading. Together, these clusters indicate that GAIA failures concentrate in evidence retrieval, multi-step reasoning, visual grounding, structured-document extraction, and query disambiguation.
以及类似实体、数值计算，或对信息不足查询的精确解读。当答案依赖于嵌入在图片、地图或图表中的信息，而仅靠文本抽取无法捕获时，就会出现图/视觉失败（11%）。当证据被锁在 PDF、结构化表格或半结构化格式中，且智能体要么误解析版式、要么忽略相关单元格时，会发生文档/表格解析失败（11%）。范围歧义（6%）涵盖对存在多种有效理解的查询：智能体给出的是相关但不正确的解读。合起来看，这些失败表明 GAIA 的故障主要集中在证据检索、多步推理、视觉落地、结构化文档抽取以及查询消歧上。


Per-model evolution logic. Panel (b) shows GAIA is the only benchmark where all four levers see substantial use; the Sonnet run alone shipped 11 prompt, 7 processor, 7 config, and 6 tools edits, because its failure set spans tool, prompt, and config problems simultaneously. The three models nonetheless diverge in a way that tracks their starting competence: Sonnet, with the most rounds, sweeps every lever; GPT-5.4 leans hardest on prompt $\left( {{45}\% \text{ of its ships }}\right)$ and barely touches config,since its reasoning is already strong enough that the remaining gains are mostly instruction-following; Qwen3.5's short run concentrates its few ships and, strikingly, lands its single tools ship at the highest yield of any cell. The shared logic is prompt-first for the behavioral clusters, with the scarce tools lever reserved for the one mechanical cluster prose cannot touch.
按模型的演化逻辑。（b）面板显示：GAIA 是唯一一个四个杠杆都被显著使用的基准；Sonnet 的运行单独就提交了 11 次提示、7 次处理器、7 次配置和 6 次工具编辑，因为它的失败集合同时覆盖了工具、提示和配置的问题。尽管如此，三个模型在某种程度上仍按其起始能力出现分歧：Sonnet（轮次最多）会遍历每个杠杆；GPT-5.4 最依赖提示 $\left( {{45}\% \text{ of its ships }}\right)$，几乎不触及 config，因为它的推理已足够强，剩余增益大多来自指令遵循；Qwen3.5 的短运行集中在它少量的几次提交，而且尤其突出的是，它那唯一一次 tools 提交的收益是该表中所有单元格里最高的。共享逻辑是：行为集群上的提示优先；稀缺的 tools 杠杆仅留给那些机械层面的集群，而这些集群的文字描述无法触及。


Did evolution close the clusters? Panel (c) shows which failure clusters were reduced by evolution. The largest improvement comes from the blocked-source cluster: the tool edit that introduced WikiTextFetch replaced unreliable browser-based Wikipedia fetching with a MediaWiki API call, reducing failures caused by empty or incomplete page retrieval. Prompt edits mainly targeted the reasoning cluster by encouraging more explicit verification, which contributed to steady gains across rounds. By contrast, figure / visual and document / table parsing failures remained harder to reduce, because they require information extraction from images, figures, PDFs, or structured tables. Overall, GAIA improves through a combination of tool edits that fix retrieval failures and prompt edits that reduce reasoning errors, while residual errors concentrate in visual and document-heavy tasks.
演化是否关闭了这些集群？（c）面板展示了哪些失败集群被演化所减少。最大的改进来自被阻断源的失败集：引入 WikiTextFetch 的那次工具编辑，用一次 MediaWiki API 调用取代了不可靠的基于浏览器的维基百科抓取，从而降低了由空内容或不完整页面检索引发的失败。提示编辑主要通过鼓励更明确的核验来瞄准推理集群，这带来了各轮持续的收益。相反，图/视觉以及文档/表格解析失败仍更难以降低，因为它们需要从图片、图表、PDF 或结构化表格中抽取信息。总体而言，GAIA 通过两类组合来改进：修复检索失败的工具编辑，以及减少推理错误的提示编辑；剩余错误则主要集中在视觉与文档负载更高的任务中。


### D.2 ALFWorld
### D.2 ALFWorld


ALFWorld is an embodied planning benchmark and the most prompt-dominated in our suite. Figure 9 shows its clusters, per-model logic, and effectiveness.
ALFWorld 是一种具身规划基准，也是我们套件中最“依赖提示词”的基准。图 9 展示了它的聚类、按模型的逻辑及其有效性。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_38.jpg?x=234&y=219&w=1363&h=532&r=0"/>



Figure 8 GAIA evolution analysis (103 tasks, exact-match). (a) Failure clusters among the tasks still unsolved; blocked-source and reasoning dominate, while figure/visual and parsing clusters are residual model gaps. (b) Share of shipped edits by bucket for each task model. (c) Lever effectiveness as hit-rate (tasks flipped / predicted) per model and bucket. The single Qwen3.5 tools ship is the highest-yield cell (0.67).
图 8 GAIA 演化分析（103 个任务，精确匹配）。(a) 仍未解决任务中的失败聚类；被阻塞的来源与推理占主导，而图像/视觉与解析聚类则是残余的模型缺口。(b) 各任务模型按桶统计已发布编辑的占比。(c) 以命中率（翻转任务/预测任务）衡量的提示词有效性，按模型和桶统计。唯一一项 Qwen3.5 tools 的发布单元产出最高（0.67）。


Failure clusters and their causes. Panel (a) summarizes the main failure clusters observed on ALFWorld. The dominant cluster is search / step-ceiling (89%), which covers episodes where the agent either searches rooms or receptacles in an inefficient order, or reaches the step limit before completing long interaction chains such as deep search or transform-then-place tasks. Prompt-rule side-effect failures (7%) occur when an added heuristic improves some tasks but unintentionally restricts behavior on others, causing the agent to skip a valid action or stop searching too early. Object-type confusion failures (4%) refer to cases where the agent confuses semantically similar objects. Together, these clusters show that ALFWorld failures mainly arise from search efficiency, over-constrained prompting, and object-specific grounding errors.
失败聚类及其原因。（a）总结了在 ALFWorld 上观察到的主要失败聚类。主导聚类是搜索 / 步数上限（89%）：涵盖了智能体要么以低效顺序搜索房间或容器，要么在完成诸如深度搜索或先变换再放置等长交互链之前就触及步数限制。提示规则带来的副作用失败（7%）发生在加入某个启发式能改善部分任务，却在其他任务上意外限制了行为，导致智能体跳过一个有效动作或过早停止搜索。对象类型混淆失败（4%）指智能体把在语义上相近的对象搞混的情况。综合来看，这些聚类表明 ALFWorld 的失败主要源于搜索效率、过度约束的提示，以及对象特定的定位错误。


Per-model evolution logic. Panel (b) shows that prompt dominance scales inversely with base-model strength: a prompt rule yields gains only for models that reliably follow it. Sonnet, being the strongest base, derives nearly all improvement from prompt edits alone; search-order heuristics in the system prompt suffice because it consistently obeys them. GPT-5.4 supplements prompts with a processor (introduced at round three) that manages its step budget for transformation tasks. Qwen3.5 requires the most varied mix (prompt, config, and processor), including a processor that intercepts its reasoning text and re-emits tool calls when needed, a mechanical fix for a failure that prompt-level steering cannot resolve. The shared pattern is prompt-first, with structural levers recruited only when prompts prove insufficient. The weaker the base model, the sooner evolution falls back from prompt-based steering to config or processor enforcement, visible in the growing non-prompt segments from Sonnet to Qwen.
按模型的演化逻辑。（b）显示：提示主导程度与基础模型强度呈反比——只有那些能可靠遵循提示规则的模型，提示规则才会带来收益。由于 Sonnet 是最强的基础模型，它几乎全部改进都来自提示编辑本身；系统提示里的搜索顺序启发式就足够了，因为它能持续遵循。GPT-5.4 在第三轮引入的处理器（processor）中用其补全提示：该处理器为变换类任务管理步预算。Qwen3.5 需要最多元的组合（提示、配置和处理器），其中包含一个拦截其推理文本并在需要时重新发出工具调用的处理器——这是提示级别引导无法解决的机械性修复。共同模式是“先提示”，只有在提示被证明不足时才调动结构性杠杆。基础模型越弱，演化越快从基于提示的引导回退到配置或处理器的强制约束，这可从 Sonnet 到 Qwen 的非提示部分不断增长中看出。


Did evolution close the clusters? Panel (c) shows that evolution reduced the main ALFWorld failure clusters, with different levers mattering for different task agents. For Qwen3.5, processor and config edits achieved the strongest effects, with hit-rates of 0.84 and 0.71 , respectively. These edits directly addressed mechanical failures by re-emitting missed tool calls and adjusting execution budgets, allowing Qwen3.5 to improve by +44.0pp and approach the closed-model runs. For Sonnet, the remaining failures were less structural, so prompt edits were sufficient for most gains, reaching a 0.49 hit-rate, while the processor edit had only a marginal effect (0.14). Two clusters were only partially reduced: prompt-rule side effects, which were introduced by some evolved heuristics and then patched in later rounds, and long-path failures, where some episodes still exceeded the available interaction budget. Overall, ALFWorld shows a clear model-dependent pattern: stronger models benefit mainly from prompt-level steering, whereas weaker models require more structural support through processor and configuration edits.
演化是否关闭了这些聚类？（c）表明，演化减少了主要的 ALFWorld 失败聚类，不同任务智能体依赖的杠杆也不同。对 Qwen3.5 而言，处理器与配置编辑带来了最强效果，命中率分别为 0.84 和 0.71。这些编辑通过重新发出遗漏的工具调用并调整执行预算，直接修复了机械性失败，使 Qwen3.5 提升了 +44.0pp，并接近“已关闭模型”的运行结果。对 Sonnet 来说，剩余失败的结构性较弱，因此提示编辑就足以带来大部分收益，命中率达到 0.49，而处理器编辑的影响只有很小的幅度（0.14）。只有两个聚类被部分减少：提示规则副作用——由部分进化出的启发式引入，随后在后续轮次中被修补；以及长路径失败——仍有一些样本超出了可用的交互预算。总体而言，ALFWorld 呈现出清晰的模型依赖模式：更强的模型主要受益于提示级别引导，而更弱的模型则需要通过处理器与配置编辑提供更多结构性支持。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_39.jpg?x=232&y=219&w=1365&h=499&r=0"/>



Figure 9 ALFWorld evolution analysis (134 tasks, goal-completion). (a) Failure clusters accumulated across all rounds; search inefficiency and the hard step-ceiling dominate, with two small clusters that evolution itself introduced (a prompt-rule side-effect) or transiently hit (object-type confusion). (b) Lever mix by model: the strong base (Sonnet) climbs on prompt almost alone, while weaker bases reach for more varied levers. (c) Lever effectiveness: structural levers (processor, config) are both used more and more effective on weaker models.
图 9 ALFWorld 演化分析（134 个任务，目标完成）。(a) 所有轮次累计的失败聚类；搜索低效与“困难的步数上限”占主导，并且有两个小聚类是由演化本身引入（提示规则副作用）或被短暂触发（对象类型混淆）。(b) 按模型的杠杆组合：强基础（Sonnet）几乎全靠提示就能攀升，而较弱的基础会尝试更多元的杠杆。(c) 杠杆有效性：结构性杠杆（处理器、配置）在弱模型上既被使用得更多，也同样更有效。


### D.3 WebShop
### D.3 WebShop


WebShop is a web-interaction benchmark and the noisiest run in our suite. Figure 10 shows its clusters, per-model logic, and effectiveness.
WebShop 是一个网页交互基准，也是我们套件中噪声最大的一次运行。图 10 展示了其聚类、各模型逻辑和有效性。


Failure clusters and their causes. Panel (a) summarizes the WebShop failure clusters accumulated across the run. Early failures are dominated by search and pagination loops, where the agent repeatedly reformulates queries or cycles through result pages without committing to a purchase. As evolution reduces these control-flow errors, the remaining failures shift toward product-selection judgment. The largest cluster, wrong product (46%), occurs when the agent selects an item from the wrong category or settles on a weak match before comparing alternatives. Pagination loop failures (21%) capture the remaining cases of repeated next/previous navigation without progress. Colour matching failures (17%) arise when the agent mishandles shade equivalence or site-specific color labels, such as treating "wine" and "red" as incompatible. Attribute check failures (17%) occur when the selected item is close to the request but fails on a required detail, such as size, sleeve length, or another unverified attribute. Overall, the cluster shift indicates that evolution first reduces navigation loops, after which the main errors concentrate in product matching and attribute verification.
失败聚类及其成因。面板 (a) 总结了整个运行过程中累积的 WebShop 失败聚类。早期失败主要是搜索和分页循环，智能体反复改写查询或在结果页之间来回切换，却不提交购买。随着演化减少这些控制流错误，剩余失败转向商品选择判断。最大聚类“选错商品”(46%) 出现在智能体从错误类别中选取物品，或在比较备选项之前就接受了一个较弱的匹配结果。分页循环失败(21%) 记录了反复下一页/上一页导航而无进展的其余情况。颜色匹配失败(17%) 源于智能体处理色调等价或站点特定颜色标签不当，例如将“wine”和“red”视为不兼容。属性检查失败(17%) 出现在所选商品与需求接近，但在某个必需细节上不符合，例如尺寸、袖长或其他未核验属性。总体来看，聚类变化表明演化首先减少了导航循环，随后主要错误集中到商品匹配和属性验证上。


Per-model evolution logic. Panel (b) shows that prompt edits drive most of the improvement across all three models, with processor edits serving as a consistent secondary lever. This pattern matches WebShop's main control-flow failures. Prompt rules help the agent search more efficiently and commit earlier, while advisory processors reinforce these rules during execution by adding warnings when the agent begins to repeat searches or cycle through pagination. For product-selection failures, evolution introduces more targeted support: a colour-matching tool helps resolve shade-equivalence cases, and config edits help weaker models maintain context over longer shopping sessions. Overall, WebShop requires a mixed response: prompts improve high-level shopping strategy, processors reduce navigation loops, tools support attribute matching, and config edits stabilize long-session behavior.
各模型的演化逻辑。面板 (b) 显示，提示词编辑推动了三种模型中大部分改进，而处理器编辑则作为稳定的次要手段。这一模式与 WebShop 的主要控制流失败相符。提示规则帮助智能体更高效地搜索并更早做出决策，而辅助处理器则在执行过程中通过在智能体开始重复搜索或在分页间循环时添加警告来强化这些规则。对于商品选择失败，演化引入了更有针对性的支持：颜色匹配工具帮助处理色调等价问题，配置编辑帮助较弱模型在更长的购物会话中保持上下文。总体而言，WebShop 需要混合响应：提示词改善高层购物策略，处理器减少导航循环，工具支持属性匹配，配置编辑稳定长会话行为。


Did evolution close the clusters? Panel (c) shows that evolution partially reduced the WebShop failure clusters. Prompt edits were the most consistently effective lever across models, with hit-rates of 0.37-0.50, while config edits helped the two weaker models maintain context over longer sessions. These changes reduced early search and pagination loops, raising performance from 60% to a peak of 76%. The remaining clusters proved harder to close. Advisory processors produced only modest gains (0.20-0.25), so some pagination failures persisted. The colour-matching tool did not improve performance in this run (0.0 hit-rate), leaving the colour-matching cluster largely unchanged. Overall, WebShop benefits most from prompt and config edits, while residual navigation loops and product-judgment errors remain the main sources of instability.
演化是否关闭了这些聚类？面板 (c) 显示，演化部分削弱了 WebShop 的失败聚类。提示词编辑是跨模型最稳定有效的手段，命中率为 0.37-0.50，而配置编辑帮助两个较弱模型在更长会话中保持上下文。这些变化减少了早期搜索和分页循环，将性能从 60% 提升至 76% 的峰值。剩余聚类更难消除。辅助处理器只带来了有限收益(0.20-0.25)，因此一些分页失败仍然存在。颜色匹配工具在本次运行中未提升性能(0.0 命中率)，使颜色匹配聚类基本未变。总体而言，WebShop 最受益于提示词和配置编辑，而残余的导航循环和商品判断错误仍是主要不稳定来源。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_40.jpg?x=235&y=325&w=1364&h=504&r=0"/>



Figure 10 WebShop evolution analysis (100 sessions). (a) Failure clusters across the run, after evolution has tamed the round-0 search/pagination loops; the residual is mostly product-choice judgment (wrong product, colour matching, attribute check). (b) Lever mix by model: prompt carries the climb, processor is the consistent second lever. (c) Lever effectiveness; prompt and config are the productive levers, the lone colour-matcher tool ship returned 0.0.
图 10 WebShop 演化分析（100 次会话）。(a) 全程失败聚类；在演化驯服了第 0 轮的搜索/分页循环后，残余主要是商品选择判断（选错商品、颜色匹配、属性检查）。(b) 各模型的杠杆组合：提示词带动上升，处理器是稳定的第二杠杆。(c) 杠杆有效性；提示词和配置是有效杠杆，唯一的颜色匹配工具 ship 返回了 0.0。


## D. ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench
## D. ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench


${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench stresses multi-turn dialogue under an explicit domain policy. Figure 11 pools the AEGIS runs across the airline, retail, and telecom domains.
${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench 在明确的领域政策下对多轮对话进行压力测试。图 11 将 AEGIS 在航空、零售和电信领域的运行结果汇总。


Failure clusters and their causes. Excluding harness-interrupt traces, the failures are judgment-heavy: the top two clusters, premature / unverified action (28%; committing a booking, refund, or device fix before a precondition holds) and wrong selection / count (24%), together exceed half and concern when to commit and what to pick rather than mechanical execution. The remainder is procedural (incomplete multi-step fix 16%, missed step / sub-task 14%) or policy-related (misinterpretation 13%). The smallest cluster, capability-boundary confusion (5%),is ${\tau }^{3}$ -specific: some telecom faults live on the user’s handset,where the agent has no device-side tool and the failure is its treating that boundary as a missing capability.
失败簇及其原因。剔除 harness-interrupt 轨迹后，失败主要是判断型：最大的两个簇是过早 / 未验证的操作（28%；在前置条件成立前就做出承诺，例如完成订票、退款或设备修复）和错误选择 / 计数（24%）；二者合计超过一半，关注的是何时提交、选择什么，而非机械执行。其余为流程型（不完整的多步骤修复 16%、遗漏步骤 / 子任务 14%）或与政策相关的（误解 13%）。最小的簇是能力边界混淆（5%），这是 ${\tau }^{3}$ 特有的：部分电信故障发生在用户手持设备上，而智能体没有设备侧工具，因而把这一边界当成了缺失能力。


Per-model evolution logic. Evolution is prompt-and-processor driven for every model, with zero tools edits: the tool set is fixed and no cluster is one that a new tool could close. Sonnet 4.6 splits prompt/processor (23/18),GPT-5.4 ships the most balanced mix $\left( {{19}/{20}}\right)$ ,and Qwen3.5-9B ships fewer overall $\left( {{14}/9}\right)$ . Since ${\tau }^{3}$ failures are control-flow and judgment errors, the productive levers are prompt rules that encode the policy's ordering constraints and processors that enforce them mid-dialogue.
按模型的演化逻辑。每个模型的演化都由提示词与处理器驱动，且为零工具编辑：工具集固定，并且没有任何簇是新工具能够关闭的。Sonnet 4.6 将提示词/处理器分配为（23/18），GPT-5.4 提供了最均衡的混合 $\left( {{19}/{20}}\right)$ ，而 Qwen3.5-9B 的整体 $\left( {{14}/9}\right)$ 更少。由于 ${\tau }^{3}$ 属于控制流与判断错误，起作用的关键在于：用提示词规则编码政策的排序约束，并由处理器在对话中途执行这些约束。


Did evolution close the clusters? Config is the sharpest lever where used (Qwen3.5 0.67, GPT-5.4 0.33 hit-rate) but is shipped rarely; the high-volume prompt and processor levers are moderately effective (0.27-0.35), matching the control-flow nature of the dominant clusters. Gains track base-model headroom: GPT-5.4 starts lowest (76.2%) and gains most (+14.5pp), Sonnet 4.6 gains +5.4pp, and near-ceiling Qwen3.5-9B only +1.1pp. The loop is not monotone; Sonnet's telecom run reaches 100% at R4, regresses to 80.7% at R7 after a sixth consecutive same-bucket edit, then recovers to 99.1% by R9 (Section 6.6). Overall, the ordering-enforcing levers close the premature-action and missed-step clusters most reliably, while wrong-selection and policy-judgment errors are the harder residual.
演化是否关闭了这些簇？当使用时，配置（config）是最锋利的杠杆（Qwen3.5 0.67，GPT-5.4 0.33 命中率），但很少被采用。高频的提示词与处理器杠杆效果适中（0.27-0.35），符合占主导地位的簇本质是控制流问题这一特征。收益与基础模型的余量一致：GPT-5.4 起点最低（76.2%）且提升最多（+14.5pp），Sonnet 4.6 提升 +5.4pp，而接近上限的 Qwen3.5-9B 仅 +1.1pp。该循环并非单调；Sonnet 的电信运行在 R4 达到 100% 后，由于连续第六次做同一桶内的编辑，在 R7 回落到 80.7%，随后在 R9 恢复到 99.1%（第 6.6 节）。总体而言，强制排序的杠杆最可靠地关闭了过早操作与遗漏步骤簇；而错误选择与政策判断错误是更难残留的问题。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_41.jpg?x=217&y=218&w=1383&h=564&r=0"/>



Figure 11 ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench evolution analysis,pooled over the airline,retail,and telecom domains. (a) Failure clusters from the logged digests (harness-interrupt traces excluded); judgment errors (premature action and wrong selection) dominate. (b) Lever mix by model: prompt and processor carry the climb, with zero tools edits since the tool set is fixed. (c) Lever effectiveness; config is sharpest where used (Qwen3.5 0.67) but rare, while prompt and processor are the consistent high-volume levers.
图 11 ${\tau }^{3}$ -Bench 的演化分析，跨航空、零售与电信领域进行汇聚。（a）来自记录摘要的失败簇（排除 harness-interrupt 轨迹）；判断错误（过早操作与错误选择）占主导。（b）按模型的杠杆组合：提示词与处理器承担了提升过程，且为零工具编辑，因为工具集固定。（c）杠杆有效性；配置在使用时最关键（Qwen3.5 0.67），但很少出现；而提示词与处理器是稳定且高频的杠杆。


### D.5 SWE-bench Verified
### D.5 SWE-bench Verified


SWE-bench Verified stresses repository-level code editing. Figure 12 shows its clusters, per-model logic, and effectiveness.
SWE-bench Verified 聚焦于仓库级代码编辑。图 12 展示了它的簇、各模型逻辑以及有效性。


Failure clusters and their causes. Panel (a) summarizes the failure clusters pooled across all rounds and all three models. The dominant cluster is incomplete fix $\left( {{62}\% }\right)$ ,where the agent reaches the right region and produces a valid patch but covers only one branch or call site while the gold patch needs several. Wrong diagnosis (19%) follows, covering edits to the wrong file or abstraction level after misreading the root cause. The remaining tail is mechanical rather than cognitive: no edit attempted (6%), Edit anchor mismatch (5%), and budget exhausted (4%). Notably the composition is the inverse of reward-hacking: failures are under-fixes, not gamed evaluations, because the harness applies the gold test patch before the model patch and blocks test-file writes.
失败簇及其原因。图(a)汇总了所有轮次与三个模型共同汇聚的失败簇。主要簇是未完成修复 $\left( {{62}\% }\right)$ ：智能体进入了正确区域并生成了有效补丁，但只覆盖了一个分支或调用点，而金标准补丁需要覆盖多个。错误诊断（19%）紧随其后：由于误读根因，对错误文件或抽象层级进行了修改。其余长尾偏机械而非认知：未尝试编辑（6%）、编辑锚点不匹配（5%）以及预算耗尽（4%）。值得注意的是，这种构成与“奖励欺骗”相反：失败是未完成修复，而非被用来“对评测动手脚”，因为 harness 会先应用金标准测试补丁，再应用模型补丁，并阻止对测试文件的写入。


Per-model evolution logic. Panel (b) shows that SWE-bench is prompt-first for every model, with the secondary lever tracking base-model strength. All three runs ship zero tools edits, since unlike GAIA the failure set has no mechanical-retrieval cluster a tool could close. Sonnet pairs prompt with an equal share of processor edits (7 each), using workflow nudges to shape an already-competent coder; GPT-5.4 leans hardest on prompt (8 ships) and uses config (4) to revert a harmful nudge and restructure its strategy phases; Qwen3.5 spreads its few ships across prompt, processor, and config (6/3/3). The shared logic is prompt-first, with structural levers recruited as the base model weakens.
逐模型演化逻辑。图(b)显示，对每个模型而言，SWE-bench 都是先提示词( prompt-first )；次要杠杆则用于跟踪基础模型的强弱。三次运行都完全不进行工具编辑：与 GAIA 不同，失败集合没有任何“机械检索”类簇，工具无法将其关闭。Sonnet 将提示词与等量的处理器编辑配对（各 7 次），通过流程层面的提示来塑造一个本就较为胜任的编码者；GPT-5.4 则最依赖提示词（8 次），并使用配置（4 次）来撤销有害提示并重构其策略阶段；Qwen3.5 将少量运行分散到提示词、处理器与配置（6/3/3）。共享逻辑始终是提示词优先：随着基础模型变弱，结构性杠杆才被逐步纳入。


Did evolution close the clusters? Panel (c) reveals a sharp capability floor. For the strong models the productive levers genuinely close failures: GPT-5.4's config edits reach 0.48 and prompt 0.39, while Sonnet's prompt and processor levers both land at 0.40. For Qwen3.5-9B every lever collapses to near-zero (prompt 0.05, config 0.05, processor 0.06 ), an order of magnitude lower, because the 9B base cannot execute the predicted fixes. The same loop that lifts GPT-5.4 from 45% to a 64% peak and stabilizes Sonnet near 87% yields only noise on Qwen3.5 (peak 42%, zero durable gains). Overall SWE-bench improves through prompt edits that broaden fix scope and config edits that restore workflow pacing, but only for models strong enough to act on them.
演化能否关闭这些簇？图(c)揭示了鲜明的能力下限。对于强模型，真正的有效杠杆确实能够关闭失败：GPT-5.4 的配置编辑达到 0.48、提示词达到 0.39；而 Sonnet 的提示词与处理器杠杆都落在 0.40。对 Qwen3.5-9B，所有杠杆都崩塌到接近零（提示词 0.05、配置 0.05、处理器 0.06），低了一个数量级，因为 9B 基础模型无法执行预期的修复。用于将 GPT-5.4 从 45% 拉升到峰值 64% 并使 Sonnet 稳定在约 87% 的同一循环，在 Qwen3.5 上只产生噪声（峰值 42%，没有持久增益）。总体而言，SWE-bench 的提升来自提示词编辑：扩大修复范围；以及配置编辑：恢复工作流节奏，但仅适用于足够强、能够真正执行这些杠杆的模型。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d8qhfo491nqc738vl770_42.jpg?x=232&y=217&w=1365&h=607&r=0"/>



Figure 12 SWE-bench Verified evolution analysis (55 tasks, resolved-rate). (a) Failure clusters pooled across all rounds and all three task models; incomplete fix and wrong diagnosis dominate, while the mechanical tail (no-edit, anchor mismatch, budget) is residual; failures are under-fixes, not gamed evaluations. (b) Lever mix by model: every run is prompt-first and ships zero tools edits, with the secondary lever shifting from processor (Sonnet) to config (GPT-5.4) to a varied mix (Qwen3.5). (c) Lever effectiveness as hit-rate (tasks flipped / predicted); strong models reach 0.39-0.48 on their productive levers,whereas every Qwen3.5-9B lever collapses to $\approx  {0.05}$ ,a capability floor below which evolution cannot compound.
图 12 SWE-bench Verified 演化分析（55 个任务，resolved-rate）。(a) 将所有轮次与三个任务模型汇聚后的失败簇：未完成修复与错误诊断占主导，而机械长尾（不编辑、锚点不匹配、预算）只是残余；失败是未完成修复，而非被“玩弄”的评测。(b) 各模型的杠杆组合：每次运行都以提示词优先，并且零工具编辑；次要杠杆从处理器（Sonnet）转向配置（GPT-5.4），再在 Qwen3.5 上变为混合。(c) 杠杆有效性以命中率衡量（被翻转的任务/预测的任务）；强模型在其有效杠杆上达到 0.39-0.48，而每个 Qwen3.5-9B 的杠杆都坍塌为 $\approx  {0.05}$ ，即演化无法进一步累积的能力下限之下。


## E Reproducibility and Artifacts
## E 可复现性与产物


### E.1 Per-Run Directory Layout
### E.1 每轮目录布局


Each evolution run writes a self-describing directory. The layout below lets a reader reconstruct any decision in this paper from the logged artifacts.
每次进化运行都会写入一个自描述目录。下列布局使读者能够根据记录的工件重建本文中的任何决策。


runs/<run_name>/ (per-run artifact layout)
runs/<run_name>/（每轮工件布局）
